### [1] [Report of the 5th PVUW Challenge: Towards More Diverse Modalities in Pixel-Level Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26031)
*Chang Liu,Henghui Ding,Nikhila Ravi,Yunchao Wei,Shuting He,Song Bai,Philip Torr,Leilei Cao,Jinrong Zhang,Deshui Miao,Xusheng He,Dengxian Gong,Zhiyu Wang,Mingqi Gao,Jihwan Hong,Canyang Wu,Weili Guan,Jianlong Wu,Liqiang Nie,Xingsen Huang,Yameng Gu,Xiaogang Yu,Xin Li,Ming-Hsuan Yang,Sijie Li,Jungong Han,Quanzhu Niu,Shihao Chen,Yuanzheng Wu,Yikang Zhou,Tao Zhang,Haobo Yuan,Lu Qi,Shunping Ji,Chao Yang,Chao Tian,Guoqing Zhu,Kai Yang,Zhifan Mo,Haijun Zhang,Xudong Kang,Shutao Li,Jaeyoung Do*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文总结了2026年CVPR PVUW挑战赛的目标、数据集和顶级方法，涵盖三个赛道：MOSE（密集遮挡场景中的目标跟踪）、MeViS-Text（运动引导语言定位）和新设立的MeViS-Audio（声音驱动的目标分割），通过新发布的挑战性数据和分析多模态解决方案，展示了视频场景理解的最新进展和未来方向。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在高度无约束的真实视频场景中，现有的视频理解方法在密集遮挡、复杂运动和多模态融合等挑战下仍存在不足，亟需一个统一的评估平台来推动技术进步。

Method: PVUW 2026挑战赛设置了三个专用赛道：MOSE赛道（密集杂乱和严重遮挡场景中的目标跟踪）、MeViS-Text赛道（通过运动聚焦的语言表达定位目标）以及新设立的MeViS-Audio赛道（声学驱动的目标分割），并发布了新的挑战性数据，由参赛者提交多模态前沿解决方案。

Result: 通过对参赛者提交的前沿多模态解决方案进行分析，报告展示了社区在鲁棒视频场景理解方面的最新技术进展。

Conclusion: 本报告通过引入新数据和评估多模态方案，突显了领域的最新技术突破，并为未来鲁棒视频场景理解指明了有前景的研究方向。

Original Abstract: This report summarizes the objectives, datasets, and top-performing methodologies of the 2026 Pixel-level Video Understanding in the Wild (PVUW) Challenge, hosted at CVPR 2026, which evaluates state-of-the-art models under highly unconstrained conditions. To provide a comprehensive assessment, the 2026 edition features three specialized tracks: the MOSE track for tracking objects within densely cluttered and severely occluded scenarios; the MeViS-Text track for localizing targets via motion-focused linguistic expressions; and the newly inaugurated MeViS-Audio track, which pioneers acoustic-driven object segmentation. By introducing previously unreleased challenging data and analyzing the cutting-edge, multimodal solutions submitted by participants, this report highlights the community's latest technical advancements and charts promising future directions for robust video scene comprehension.

中文摘要翻译: 本报告总结了2026年CVPR举办的"野外像素级视频理解"（PVUW）挑战赛的目标、数据集和最佳方法。该挑战赛在高度无约束的条件下评估当前最先进的模型。为提供全面评估，2026届赛事设立了三个专项赛道：MOSE赛道，专注于密集杂乱和严重遮挡场景中的目标跟踪；MeViS-Text赛道，通过运动聚焦的语言表达来定位目标；以及新设立的MeViS-Audio赛道，开创了声学驱动的目标分割任务。通过引入此前未发布的高难度数据，并分析参赛者提交的前沿多模态解决方案，本报告展示了社区最新的技术进步，并为鲁棒视频场景理解描绘了有前景的未来研究方向。

</details>


### [2] [Evaluating the Alignment Between GeoAI Explanations and Domain Knowledge in Satellite-Based Flood Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26051)
*Hyunho Lee,Wenwen Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ADAGE框架，通过通道分组SHAP方法系统性评估深度学习模型在卫星洪水制图任务中的解释是否与遥感领域知识一致，实验证明该框架能定量评估对齐程度并帮助专家识别不一致的解释。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 深度学习模型在卫星洪水制图中表现优异，但其决策过程不透明，阻碍了在关键科学和业务流程中的应用。缺乏系统性评估模型解释是否与遥感领域知识一致的框架。

Method: 提出ADAGE框架，采用通道分组SHAP（Channel-Group SHAP）方法估计分组输入通道对像素级预测的贡献，通过对齐分数定量评估模型解释与领域知识参考解释之间的一致性。

Result: 在两个卫星洪水制图任务上的实验表明：ADAGE框架能够(1)定量评估模型解释与领域知识解释之间的对齐程度；(2)通过对齐分数帮助领域专家识别不一致的解释。

Conclusion: 本研究弥合了GeoAI地球观测中可解释性与领域知识之间的鸿沟，增强了GeoAI模型在科学和业务流程中的适用性。

Original Abstract: The increasing number of satellites has improved the temporal resolution of Earth observation, making satellite-based flood mapping a promising approach for operational flood monitoring. Deep learning-based approaches for flood mapping using satellite imagery, an important application within Geospatial Artificial Intelligence (GeoAI), have shown improved predictive performance by learning complex spatial and spectral patterns from large volumes of remote sensing data. However, the opaque decision-making processes of deep learning models remain a major barrier to their integration into critical scientific and operational workflows. This highlights the need for a systematic assessment of whether model explanations align with established domain knowledge in remote sensing. To address this research gap, this study introduces the ADAGE (Alignment between Domain Knowledge And GeoAI Explanation Evaluation) framework. The proposed framework is designed to systematically evaluate how well explanations of deep learning models align with established remote sensing knowledge, particularly regarding the distinctive spectral properties of the Earth's surface. The ADAGE framework employs Channel-Group SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) method to estimate the contributions of grouped input channels to pixel-level predictions. Experiments on two satellite-based flood mapping tasks demonstrate that the ADAGE framework can (1) quantitatively assess the alignment between model explanations and reference explanations derived from domain knowledge and (2) help domain experts identify misaligned explanations through alignment scores. This study contributes to bridging the gap between explainability and domain knowledge in GeoAI for Earth observation, enhancing the applicability of GeoAI models in scientific and operational workflows.

中文摘要翻译: 卫星数量的增加提高了地球观测的时间分辨率，使得基于卫星的洪水制图成为业务化洪水监测的一种有前景的方法。基于深度学习的卫星影像洪水制图方法是地球空间人工智能（GeoAI）的重要应用，通过学习遥感大数据中复杂的空间和光谱模式，展现了更优的预测性能。然而，深度学习模型不透明的决策过程仍是其融入关键科学和业务流程的主要障碍。这凸显了系统性评估模型解释是否与遥感领域已有知识一致的必要性。为填补这一研究空白，本文提出了ADAGE（领域知识与GeoAI解释评估对齐）框架。该框架旨在系统评估深度学习模型的解释与已有遥感知识（特别是关于地球表面独特光谱特性的知识）之间的对齐程度。ADAGE框架采用通道分组SHAP（Shapley加性解释）方法来估计分组输入通道对像素级预测的贡献。在两个卫星洪水制图任务上的实验表明，ADAGE框架能够(1)定量评估模型解释与领域知识导出的参考解释之间的对齐程度，(2)通过对齐分数帮助领域专家识别不一致的解释。本研究有助于弥合GeoAI地球观测中可解释性与领域知识之间的鸿沟，增强了GeoAI模型在科学和业务流程中的适用性。

</details>


### [3] [FruitProM-V2: Robust Probabilistic Maturity Estimation and Detection of Fruits and Vegetables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26084)
*Rahul Harsha Cheppally,Sidharth Rai,Sudan Baral,Benjamin Vail,Ajay Sharda*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出将水果成熟度识别从多分类问题改为概率性连续变量建模，通过分布检测头和累积分布函数来预测成熟度，从而更好地处理相邻成熟阶段间的模糊性和标注噪声，提高估计的鲁棒性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统将成熟度识别视为多分类任务的方法强制在视觉相似的相邻阶段之间划出清晰边界，这与成熟度作为连续生物过程的本质不符。通过标注可靠性研究发现标注者分歧集中在相邻成熟阶段，因此需要更合理地建模成熟度的不确定性。

Method: 将成熟度建模为潜在连续变量，使用分布检测头进行概率预测，并通过累积分布函数（CDF）将连续分布转换为类别概率，从而实现概率化的成熟度估计。

Result: 在干净标注下，该方法的性能与标准检测器相当，同时能更好地表示不确定性；在引入受控标注噪声时，该概率模型相比基线表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 显式地对成熟度不确定性进行建模可以得到更可靠的视觉成熟度估计，尤其在实际应用中标注存在噪声的情况下更具优势。

Original Abstract: Accurate fruit maturity identification is essential for determining harvest timing, as incorrect assessment directly affects yield and post-harvest quality. Although ripening is a continuous biological process, vision-based maturity estimation is typically formulated as a multi-class classification task, which imposes sharp boundaries between visually similar stages. To examine this limitation, we perform an annotation reliability study with two independent annotators on a held-out tomato dataset and observe disagreement concentrated near adjacent maturity stages. Motivated by this observation, we model maturity as a latent continuous variable and predict it probabilistically using a distributional detection head, converting the distribution into class probabilities through the cumulative distribution function (CDF). The proposed formulation maintains comparable performance to a standard detector under clean labels while better representing uncertainty. Furthermore, when controlled label noise is introduced during training, the probabilistic model demonstrates improved robustness relative to the baseline, indicating that explicitly modeling maturity uncertainty leads to more reliable visual maturity estimation.

中文摘要翻译: 准确的水果成熟度识别对于确定收获时机至关重要，因为错误的评估会直接影响产量和采后品质。尽管成熟是一个连续的生物过程，基于视觉的成熟度估计通常被表述为多分类任务，这会在视觉相似的阶段之间施加尖锐的边界。为探究这一局限性，我们使用两位独立标注员对一个留出的番茄数据集进行了标注可靠性研究，观察到标注分歧主要集中在相邻成熟阶段。受此观察启发，我们将成熟度建模为潜在的连续变量，并使用分布检测头对其进行概率预测，通过累积分布函数（CDF）将分布转换为类别概率。所提出的公式在干净标注下保持了与标准检测器相当的性能，同时能更好地表示不确定性。此外，当在训练过程中引入受控的标注噪声时，该概率模型相比基线展现出更强的鲁棒性，表明显式地对成熟度不确定性进行建模能够带来更可靠的视觉成熟度估计。

</details>


### [4] [Sample Selection Using Multi-Task Autoencoders in Federated Learning with Non-IID Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26116)
*Emre Ardıç,Yakup Genç*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于多任务自编码器和异常检测方法的联邦学习样本选择框架，通过损失分析和特征分析滤除噪声样本，显著提升图像分类任务中的模型精度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 联邦学习中，冗余、恶意或异常样本会导致模型性能下降和效率降低，现有方法难以有效识别和过滤这些低质量样本。

Method: 采用多任务自编码器估计样本贡献，结合损失分析和特征分析；使用OCSVM、孤立森林和自适应损失阈值三种无监督异常检测方法滤除噪声样本；提出基于多类深度SVDD损失的服务器端特征样本选择方法。

Result: 在CIFAR10和MNIST数据集上，损失选择方法在CIFAR10上使用OCSVM提升7.02%，在MNIST上使用AT提升1.83%；特征选择方法在CIFAR10上使用OCSVM额外提升0.99%。

Conclusion: 所提方法在不同客户端数量、非IID分布和高达40%噪声条件下均能有效提升模型精度，验证了损失和特征双重样本选择机制的有效性。

Original Abstract: Federated learning is a machine learning paradigm in which multiple devices collaboratively train a model under the supervision of a central server while ensuring data privacy. However, its performance is often hindered by redundant, malicious, or abnormal samples, leading to model degradation and inefficiency. To overcome these issues, we propose novel sample selection methods for image classification, employing a multitask autoencoder to estimate sample contributions through loss and feature analysis. Our approach incorporates unsupervised outlier detection, using one-class support vector machine (OCSVM), isolation forest (IF), and adaptive loss threshold (AT) methods managed by a central server to filter noisy samples on clients. We also propose a multi-class deep support vector data description (SVDD) loss controlled by a central server to enhance feature-based sample selection. We validate our methods on CIFAR10 and MNIST datasets across varying numbers of clients, non-IID distributions, and noise levels up to 40%. The results show significant accuracy improvements with loss-based sample selection, achieving gains of up to 7.02% on CIFAR10 with OCSVM and 1.83% on MNIST with AT. Additionally, our federated SVDD loss further improves feature-based sample selection, yielding accuracy gains of up to 0.99% on CIFAR10 with OCSVM. These results show the effectiveness of our methods in improving model accuracy across various client counts and noise conditions.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习是一种机器学习范式，其中多个设备在中央服务器的监督下协同训练模型，同时确保数据隐私。然而，其性能常常受到冗余、恶意或异常样本的阻碍，导致模型退化和效率低下。为克服这些问题，我们针对图像分类任务提出了一种新颖的样本选择方法，采用多任务自编码器通过损失和特征分析来估计样本贡献。我们的方法结合了无监督异常检测技术，使用一类支持向量机（OCSVM）、孤立森林（IF）和自适应损失阈值（AT）方法（由中央服务器管理）来过滤客户端上的噪声样本。我们还提出了一种由中央服务器控制的多类深度支持向量数据描述（SVDD）损失，以增强基于特征的样本选择。我们在CIFAR10和MNIST数据集上，针对不同客户端数量、非独立同分布（non-IID）分布以及高达40%的噪声水平进行了验证。结果表明，基于损失的样本选择带来了显著的精度提升，在CIFAR10上使用OCSVM提升了7.02%，在MNIST上使用AT提升了1.83%。此外，我们的联邦SVDD损失进一步改进了基于特征的样本选择，在CIFAR10上使用OCSVM获得了高达0.99%的精度提升。这些结果表明，我们的方法在不同客户端数量和噪声条件下均能有效提高模型精度。

</details>


### [5] [A Data-Centric Framework for Intraoperative Fluorescence Lifetime Imaging for Glioma Surgical Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26147)
*Silvia Noble Anbunesan,Mohamed Abul Hassan,Jinyi Qi,Lisanne Kraft,Han Sung Lee,Orin Bloch,Laura Marcu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种数据驱动AI（DC-AI）框架，结合置信学习、类别精炼和靶向标签评估，用于胶质母细胞瘤（GBM）切除边缘的实时荧光寿命成像（FLIm）多分类，在192个组织边缘数据上实现三分类96%准确率，并通过SHAP分析和盲法重评估验证了数据可靠性和模型鲁棒性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 胶质瘤术中浸润程度评估对最大化切除肿瘤同时保留功能脑组织至关重要，但FLIm的临床应用面临生物异质性、类别不平衡和组织病理学标注变异性等挑战，亟需系统性提高数据质量和模型鲁棒性的方法。

Method: 提出数据驱动AI（DC-AI）框架，包含三个核心步骤：（1）置信学习（CL）量化FLIm点级置信度并识别标签不一致性；（2）迭代类别合并将原始七类方案精炼为三类（低、中、高）；（3）靶向标签评估对置信学习标记的边缘进行盲法重评，并利用SHAP分析解释类别特异性FLIm特征重要性。

Result: 在31例IDH野生型GBM患者的192个组织边缘数据上，三分类任务达到96%准确率；SHAP分析揭示了浸润谱中不同类别的光学特征差异；低置信预测的贡献因素包括灰质成分（生物学因素）和血液污染（采集因素）；盲法重评证实了病理学家内部标注变异性，证明了选择性重标注优于穷举式审查。

Conclusion: DC-AI框架能够系统性地提高数据可靠性、增强模型鲁棒性并优化FLIm信号的生物学解释，为开发临床可行的实时胶质瘤边缘评估光学工具提供了支持。

Original Abstract: Accurate intraoperative assessment of glioma infiltration is essential for maximizing tumor resection while preserving functional brain tissue. Fluorescence lifetime imaging (FLIm) offers real-time, label-free biochemical contrast, but its clinical utility is challenged by biological heterogeneity, class imbalance, and variability in histopathological labeling. We present a data-centric AI (DC-AI) framework that integrates confident learning (CL), class refinement, and targeted label evaluation to develop a robust multi-class FLIm classifier for glioblastoma (GBM) resection margins. FLIm data were collected from 192 tissue margins across 31 newly diagnosed IDH-wildtype GBM patients and initially labeled into seven tumor cellularity classes by an expert neuropathologist. CL was applied to quantify FLIm point-level confidence, identify label inconsistencies, and guide iterative class merging into a three-class scheme ("low", "moderate", "high"). The resulting high-fidelity dataset enabled training a model that achieved 96% accuracy in the three-class task. SHAP analysis revealed class-specific FLIm feature importance, highlighting distinct optical signatures across the infiltration spectrum. Targeted FLIm analysis further identified biological (e.g., gray matter composition) and acquisition-related (e.g., blood contamination) contributors to low-confidence predictions. Blinded re-evaluation of margins flagged by CL demonstrated intra-pathologist variability, underscoring the value of selective relabeling rather than exhaustive review. Together, these findings demonstrate that a DC-AI framework can systematically improve data reliability, enhance model robustness, and refine biological interpretation of FLIm signals, supporting the development of clinically actionable optical tools for real-time glioma margin assessment.

中文摘要翻译: 准确评估术中胶质瘤浸润程度对于最大化肿瘤切除同时保留功能性脑组织至关重要。荧光寿命成像（FLIm）能够提供实时、无标记的生化对比，但其临床应用受到生物异质性、类别不平衡以及组织病理学标注变异性的挑战。本文提出一种数据驱动AI（DC-AI）框架，整合了置信学习（CL）、类别精炼和靶向标签评估，用于开发针对胶质母细胞瘤（GBM）切除边缘的鲁棒多分类FLIm分类器。FLIm数据采集自31例新诊断的IDH野生型GBM患者的192个组织边缘，初始由一名神经病理学专家标注为七类肿瘤细胞丰度类别。应用置信学习量化FLIm点级置信度，识别标注不一致性，并引导迭代类别合并为三类方案（"低"、"中"、"高"）。由此产生的高保真数据集使模型在三分类任务中达到96%准确率。SHAP分析揭示了类别特异性的FLIm特征重要性，突显了整个浸润谱中不同的光学特征。靶向FLIm分析进一步识别了导致低置信预测的生物学因素（如灰质成分）和采集相关因素（如血液污染）。对置信学习标记的边缘进行盲法重评估，展示了病理学家内部的变异性，强调了选择性重标注而非穷举式审查的价值。综上，这些发现证明DC-AI框架能够系统性地提高数据可靠性、增强模型鲁棒性，并优化FLIm信号的生物学解释，为开发用于实时胶质瘤边缘评估的临床可行光学工具提供了支持。

</details>


### [6] [Why Domain Matters: A Preliminary Study of Domain Effects in Underwater Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26174)
*Melanie Wille,Dimity Miller,Tobias Fischer,Scarlett Raine*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于可测量图像、场景和采集特征的水下域定义框架，替代传统合成风格迁移方法，实现语义一致的图像分组与领域特定检测性能评估，揭示隐藏的失败模式。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有水下领域迁移基准通过合成风格迁移模拟数据分布偏差，无法捕捉能见度、光照、场景构成等真实场景因素，限制了对实际环境效果的分析。

Method: 提出一种标注框架，利用可测量的图像、场景和采集特征定义水下领域，实现语义一致的图像分组，支持领域特定的检测性能评估和失败分析。

Result: 在公开数据集上验证，展示了不同领域因素下的系统性变化，并揭示了隐藏的失败模式。

Conclusion: 该框架相比合成风格迁移更能捕捉物理上有意义的因素，支持更深入的真实世界性能分析。

Original Abstract: Domain shift, where deviations between training and deployment data distributions degrade model performance, is a key challenge in underwater environments. Existing benchmarks testing performance for underwater domain shift simulate variability through synthetic style transfer. This fails to capture intrinsic scene factors such as visibility, illumination, scene composition, or acquisition factors, limiting analysis of real-world effects. We propose a labeling framework that defines underwater domains using measurable image, scene, and acquisition characteristics. Unlike prior benchmarks, it captures physically meaningful factors, enabling semantically consistent image grouping and supporting domain-specific evaluation of detection performance including failure analysis. We validate this on public datasets, showing systematic variations across domain factors and revealing hidden failure modes.

中文摘要翻译: 领域偏移（即训练数据和部署数据分布之间的偏差导致模型性能下降）是水下环境中的一个关键挑战。现有用于测试水下领域偏移性能的基准通过合成风格迁移模拟数据分布变化，但这无法捕捉能见度、光照、场景构成或采集因素等内在场景特征，限制了对真实世界效果的分析。我们提出一种标注框架，利用可测量的图像、场景和采集特征定义水下领域。与现有基准不同，该框架能够捕捉物理上有意义的因素，实现语义一致的图像分组，并支持包括失败分析在内的领域特定检测性能评估。我们在公开数据集上验证了该方法，展示了不同领域因素下的系统性变化，并揭示了隐藏的失败模式。

</details>

### [8] [FASH-iCNN: Making Editorial Fashion Identity Inspectable Through Multimodal CNN Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26186)
*Morayo Danielle Adeyemi,Ryan A. Rossi,Franck Dernoncourt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FASH-iCNN多模态系统，从Vogue runway图像中解码时尚品牌的审美逻辑。系统能识别服装的品牌、年代和色彩传统，并发现纹理和亮度是品牌身份的主要载体，而非颜色。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前时尚AI系统隐式编码了特定品牌、编辑和历史的审美逻辑而不加披露，缺乏可解释性。作者旨在让这种文化逻辑变得可检视，揭示哪些视觉特征承载了品牌和时代的编辑身份。

Method: 训练多模态系统FASH-iCNN，基于15个时尚品牌1991-2024年间87,547张Vogue runway图像。通过服装-only模型识别品牌（78.2% top-1/14类）、年代（88.6% top-1）和具体年份（58.3% top-1，平均误差2.2年）。通过移除颜色和纹理通道进行消融实验，探测视觉信号来源。

Result: 移除颜色仅使品牌识别准确率下降10.6个百分点，而移除纹理导致下降37.6个百分点，表明纹理和亮度是编辑身份的主要载体。系统能高精度识别品牌、年代和年份。

Conclusion: FASH-iCNN将编辑文化视为信号而非背景噪声，能够揭示预测结果中编码了哪些品牌、编辑和历史时刻，使时尚AI系统的文化逻辑变得透明可检视。

Original Abstract: Fashion AI systems routinely encode the aesthetic logic of specific houses, editors, and historical moments without disclosing it. We present FASH-iCNN, a multimodal system trained on 87,547 Vogue runway images across 15 fashion houses spanning 1991-2024 that makes this cultural logic inspectable. Given a photograph of a garment, the system recovers which house produced it, which era it belongs to, and which color tradition it reflects. A clothing-only model identifies the fashion house at 78.2% top-1 across 14 houses, the decade at 88.6% top-1, and the specific year at 58.3% top-1 across 34 years with a mean error of just 2.2 years. Probing which visual channels carry this signal reveals a sharp dissociation: removing color costs only 10.6pp of house identity accuracy, while removing texture costs 37.6pp, establishing texture and luminance as the primary carriers of editorial identity. FASH-iCNN treats editorial culture as the signal rather than background noise, identifying which houses, eras, and color traditions shaped each output so that users can see not just what the system predicts but which houses, editors, and historical moments are encoded in that prediction.

中文摘要翻译: 时尚AI系统通常隐式编码特定品牌、编辑和历史的审美逻辑而不加披露。本文提出FASH-iCNN，一个基于15个时尚品牌1991-2024年间87,547张Vogue runway图像训练的多模态系统，使这种文化逻辑变得可检视。给定一张服装照片，系统能够恢复其所属品牌、年代以及所反映的色彩传统。服装-only模型在14个品牌上达到78.2%的top-1品牌识别准确率，在年代识别上达到88.6%的top-1准确率，在34年间具体年份识别上达到58.3%的top-1准确率，平均误差仅为2.2年。探究承载这些信号的视觉通道发现显著的分化：去除颜色仅使品牌身份准确率下降10.6个百分点，而去除纹理则导致37.6个百分点的下降，表明纹理和亮度是编辑身份的主要载体。FASH-iCNN将编辑文化视为信号而非背景噪声，识别出哪些品牌、时代和色彩传统塑造了每个输出，使用户不仅能看见系统的预测结果，还能看见该预测中编码了哪些品牌、编辑和历史时刻。

### [9] [Seeking Consensus: Geometric-Semantic On-the-Fly Recalibration for Open-Vocabulary Remote Sensing Semantic Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26221)
*Guanchun Wang,Chenxiao Wu,Xiangrong Zhang,Zelin Peng,Jianxun Lai,Tianyang Zhang,Xu Tang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SeeCo，一种即插即用的训练无关框架，通过对遥感图像中开放词汇语义分割模型进行几何共识与语义共识的在线校准，有效提升分割性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有遥感开放词汇语义分割方法采用静态推理范式，忽略了每幅场景的独特分布，导致不同地物语义模糊且前景激活不完整。

Method: 提出SeeCo框架，包含几何共识学习（GCL）通过多视角一致观测和语义共识学习（SCL）通过文本描述自适应校准，二者通过在线共识注入器（OCI）协作重新校准视觉和文本语义，无需训练即可在推理过程中动态调整语义-几何对齐。

Result: 在八个遥感开放词汇语义分割基准数据集上取得一致提升，验证了方法的有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: SeeCo作为一种即插即用、无需训练框架，通过在线寻求双重共识能够有效缓解欠激活和语义偏差问题，显著增强遥感图像开放词汇语义分割的性能。

Original Abstract: Open-vocabulary semantic segmentation (OVSS) in remote sensing images is a promising task that employs textual descriptions for identifying undefined land cover categories. Despite notable advances, existing methods typically employ a static inference paradigm, overlooking the distinct distribution of each scene, resulting in semantic ambiguity in diverse land covers and incomplete foreground activation. Motivated by this, we propose Seeking Consensus, termed SeeCo, a plug-and-play framework to boost the performance of training-free OVSS models in remote sensing images, which recalibrates arbitrary OVSS models on-the-fly by seeking dual consensus: geometric consensus learning (GCL) through multi-view consistent observations and semantic consensus learning (SCL) via textual description adaptive calibration, which assists collaborative recalibration of visual and textual semantics. The two consensus are injected via an online consensus injector (OCI), effectively alleviating the under-activation and semantic bias. SeeCo requires no specific training process, yet recalibrates semantic-geometric alignment for each unique scene during inference. Extensive experiments on eight remote sensing OVSS benchmarks show consistent gains, proving its effectiveness and universality.

中文摘要翻译: 遥感图像中的开放词汇语义分割（OVSS）是一项有前景的任务，它利用文本描述来识别未定义的土地覆盖类别。尽管已有显著进展，现有方法通常采用静态推理范式，忽略了每个场景的独特分布，导致不同地物之间存在语义模糊性以及前景激活不完整。受此启发，我们提出Seeking Consensus（简称SeeCo），一种即插即用的框架，用于提升遥感图像中无需训练的OVSS模型的性能。该框架通过寻求双重共识——即通过多视角一致观测的几何共识学习（GCL）和通过文本描述自适应校准的语义共识学习（SCL）——在线重新校准任意OVSS模型，从而辅助视觉与文本语义的协同校准。这两种共识通过在线共识注入器（OCI）注入，有效缓解了欠激活和语义偏差问题。SeeCo无需特定的训练过程，即可在推理过程中为每个独特场景重新校准语义-几何对齐。在八个遥感OVSS基准数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法取得了持续的性能提升，证明了其有效性和通用性。

### [10] [EnerGS: Energy-Based Gaussian Splatting with Partial Geometric Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26238)
*Rui Song,Tianhui Cai,Markus Gross,Yun Zhang,Walter Zimmer,Zhiyu Huang,Olaf Wysocki,Jiaqi Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对3D高斯溅射训练中几何先验（如LiDAR）在户外大场景下空间不完整、不均匀的问题，提出EnerGS，将部分可观测几何建模为连续能量场，提供软几何引导而非硬约束，显著提升稀疏多视图和单目设置下的光度质量与几何稳定性，缓解过拟合。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有3DGS方法在户外大场景中依赖LiDAR等几何先验进行初始化或训练约束，但这些几何监督往往空间上不完整且不均匀，作为可靠先验效果有限，甚至损害重建质量。因此需要一种能有效利用部分几何信息且不引入硬约束的方法。

Method: 将部分可观测的几何信息建模为连续能量场，提出EnerGS方法。该方法不将几何作为硬约束，而是提供软几何引导，使几何信息引导高斯原语的优化过程，而不直接限制解空间。

Result: 在大型户外场景的实验中，EnerGS在稀疏多视图和单目设置下均一致提升了光度重建质量和几何稳定性，并有效缓解了3DGS训练中的过拟合问题。

Conclusion: EnerGS通过软几何引导策略，有效解决了户外大场景中几何先验不完整的问题，在提升重建质量的同时增强了几何稳定性，是一种优于传统硬约束的替代方案。

Original Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has been widely adopted for scene reconstruction, where training inherently constitutes a highly coupled and non-convex optimization problem. Recent works commonly incorporate geometric priors, such as LiDAR measurements, either for initialization or as training constraints, with the goal of improving photometric reconstruction quality. However, in large-scale outdoor scenarios, such geometric supervision is often spatially incomplete and uneven, which limits its effectiveness as a reliable prior and can even be detrimental to the final reconstruction. To address this challenge, we model partially observable geometry as a continuous energy field induced by geometric evidence and propose EnerGS. Rather than enforcing geometry as a hard constraint, EnerGS provides a soft geometric guidance for the optimization of Gaussian primitives, allowing geometric information to steer the optimization process without directly restricting the solution space. Extensive experiments on large-scale outdoor scenes demonstrate that, under both sparse multi-view and monocular settings, EnerGS consistently improves photometric quality and geometric stability, while effectively mitigating overfitting during 3DGS training.

中文摘要翻译: 3D高斯溅射（3DGS）已被广泛应用于场景重建，其训练本质上构成一个高度耦合且非凸的优化问题。近年来的工作通常引入几何先验（如LiDAR测量）用于初始化或作为训练约束，旨在提升光度重建质量。然而，在大型户外场景中，这类几何监督往往在空间上不完整且不均匀，从而限制了其作为可靠先验的有效性，甚至可能对最终重建产生负面影响。为应对这一挑战，本文将部分可观测的几何建模为由几何证据诱导的连续能量场，并提出EnerGS。EnerGS不将几何作为硬约束，而是为高斯原语的优化提供软几何引导，使得几何信息能够引导优化过程，同时不直接限制解空间。在大型户外场景上的大量实验表明，在稀疏多视图和单目设置下，EnerGS均能一致地提升光度质量和几何稳定性，同时有效缓解3DGS训练中的过拟合问题。

</details>


### [11] [Camera-RFID Fusion for Robust Asset Tracking in Forested Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26241)
*John Hateley,Sriram Narasimhan,Omid Abari*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种相机与RFID融合框架，通过深度信息、物体信息和先进轨迹匹配算法，解决了森林环境中标签定位精度从米级提升到厘米级的问题，并首次在自然森林环境中实现了相机-RFID融合的资产跟踪。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 森林环境中RFID信号衰减和多径效应导致空间精度仅达米级，而立体视觉相机虽可达厘米级精度，但单独使用视觉无法解决空间关联模糊和密集遮挡问题。融合两种模态可兼顾视觉的高精度与RFID的非视距识别优势，但核心挑战在于精确关联两种传感器产生的异构轨迹。

Method: 提出了一种相机-RFID融合框架，集成深度信息与物体信息，并结合先进的轨迹匹配算法，实现两种传感器轨迹的精确关联，从而将定位精度从米级提升至厘米级。

Result: 该方法成功弥合了米级到厘米级的精度差距，即使资产暂时离开相机视野也能实现可靠的标签定位。这是首次将相机-RFID融合应用于自然森林环境中的资产跟踪。

Conclusion: 通过融合相机与RFID两种模态，结合深度信息、物体信息和轨迹匹配算法，可以有效克服单一传感器的局限性，在森林等复杂环境中实现高精度、鲁棒的资产定位与跟踪。

Original Abstract: Passive RFID tags offer a cost-effective and scalable solution for tracking numerous deployed assets. However, in forested environments, signal attenuation and multipath effects generally limit RFID spatial accuracy to the meter level. Conversely, while cameras employing stereo vision can achieve centimeter-level precision, relying solely on computer vision fails to resolve issues arising from spatial association ambiguity and partial occlusions in dense settings. Fusing these modalities allows systems to harness the high-accuracy benefits of vision while retaining the robust, non-line-of-sight identification advantages of RFID. Yet, a primary challenge in achieving this, which is the central focus of this paper, lies in accurately associating the disparate trajectories generated by these two sensors. To overcome this limitation, we introduce a novel camera--RFID fusion framework that integrates depth and object information with advanced trajectory-matching algorithms. By successfully bridging the meter-to-centimeter accuracy gap, the proposed approach helps achieve reliable tag localization even when assets temporarily leave the camera's field of view. To the best of our knowledge, this represents the first application of camera--RFID fusion for asset tracking in natural forested environments.

中文摘要翻译: 无源RFID标签为跟踪大量部署的资产提供了一种经济高效且可扩展的解决方案。然而，在森林环境中，信号衰减和多径效应通常将RFID的空间精度限制在米级水平。相反，采用立体视觉的相机虽然可以达到厘米级精度，但仅依靠计算机视觉无法解决密集场景下空间关联模糊和部分遮挡带来的问题。融合这两种模态可以使系统充分利用视觉的高精度优势，同时保留RFID鲁棒的非视距识别能力。然而，实现这一目标的主要挑战——也是本文的核心焦点——在于精确关联由这两种传感器产生的不同轨迹。为了克服这一限制，我们提出了一种新颖的相机-RFID融合框架，该框架将深度信息和物体信息与先进的轨迹匹配算法相结合。通过成功弥合米级到厘米级的精度差距，所提出的方法即使当资产暂时离开相机视野时也能实现可靠的标签定位。据我们所知，这是首次将相机-RFID融合应用于自然森林环境中的资产跟踪。

### [12] [Beyond Shortcuts: Mitigating Visual Illusions in Frozen VLMs via Qualitative Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26250)
*Hao Guo,Fei Wang,Junjie Chen,Yiqi Nie,Jiaqi Zhao,Qiankun Li,Subin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SQI框架，一种无需训练、基于数据驱动的推理方法，通过公理约束注入、层次化场景分解和反事实自验证三个模块，提升冻结视觉-语言模型在光学错觉下的感知鲁棒性，在DataCV 2026挑战赛中获得第二名。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的视觉-语言模型（VLM）在面对光学错觉时感知鲁棒性极差，模型往往依赖语言先验和记忆化原型（快捷启发式）而非直接视觉证据，导致推理错误。需要一种无需微调、能增强VLM视觉基础能力的方法来弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 提出结构化定性推理（SQI）框架，包含三个模块：(1) 公理约束注入——抑制错误的度量估计和定量幻觉；(2) 层次化场景分解——从复杂背景干扰中解耦出目标视觉流形；(3) 反事实自验证——通过对抗性推理步骤缓解确认偏差。这些定性约束在推理时被编排协同，将高层语言推理与低层视觉感知对齐。

Result: 在DataCV 2026挑战赛（任务I：经典错觉理解）中排名第二。实验表明SQI在不同错觉类别上显著提升了准确性，且无需任何模型微调即可提供优越的诊断可解释性。

Conclusion: 结构化定性基础（structured qualitative grounding）是开发下一代抗错觉视觉-语言系统的有效范式，展示了在不修改模型参数的前提下增强感知鲁棒性的潜力。

Original Abstract: While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved state-of-the-art performance in general visual tasks, their perceptual robustness remains remarkably brittle when confronted with optical illusions. These failures are often attributed to shortcut heuristics, where models prioritize linguistic priors and memorized prototypes over direct visual evidence. In this work, we propose Structured Qualitative Inference (SQI), a training-free, data-centric framework designed to fortify visual grounding in frozen VLMs. SQI addresses perceptual anomalies through three systematic modules: (1) Axiomatic Constraint Injection, which suppresses erroneous metric estimations and quantitative hallucinations; (2) Hierarchical Scene Decomposition, which decouples target visual manifolds from complex background distractors; and (3) Counterfactual Self-Verification, an adversarial reasoning step that mitigates confirmation bias. By orchestrating these qualitative constraints at inference time, SQI effectively aligns high-level linguistic reasoning with low-level visual perception. Our framework was evaluated on the DataCV 2026 Challenge (Task I: Classic Illusion Understanding), where it ranked 2nd place overall. Experimental results demonstrate that SQI not only significantly enhances accuracy across diverse illusion categories but also provides superior diagnostic interpretability without any model fine-tuning. Our success underscores the potential of structured qualitative grounding as a robust paradigm for developing next-generation, illusion-resistant vision-language systems.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管视觉-语言模型（VLM）在通用视觉任务中取得了最先进的性能，但其在面对光学错觉时的感知鲁棒性仍然极其脆弱。这些失败通常归因于快捷启发式——模型优先依赖语言先验和记忆化原型而非直接视觉证据。在这项工作中，我们提出了结构化定性推理（SQI），一个无需训练、基于数据驱动的框架，旨在增强冻结VLM中的视觉基础能力。SQI通过三个系统化的模块来处理感知异常：(1) 公理约束注入——抑制错误的度量估计和定量幻觉；(2) 层次化场景分解——从复杂背景干扰中解耦出目标视觉流形；(3) 反事实自验证——一种缓解确认偏差的对抗性推理步骤。通过在推理时编排这些定性约束，SQI有效将高层语言推理与低层视觉感知对齐。我们的框架在DataCV 2026挑战赛（任务I：经典错觉理解）中进行了评估，总体排名第二。实验结果表明，SQI不仅在不同错觉类别上显著提升了准确性，而且在无需任何模型微调的情况下提供了优越的诊断可解释性。我们的成功强调了结构化定性基础作为开发下一代抗错觉视觉-语言系统的鲁棒范式的潜力。

### [14] [OmniTrend: Content-Context Modeling for Scalable Social Popularity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26252)
*Liliang Ye,Guiyi Zeng,Yunyao Zhang,Yi-Ping Phoebe Chen,Junqing Yu,Zikai Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OmniTrend提出了一种统一框架，将社交媒体流行度分解为内容吸引力与环境曝光度两个可解释因素，分别建模后联合预测，提升了可解释性和跨平台迁移能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有流行度预测方法仅关注内容信号，未能将其与曝光相关的模式分离开来，导致学习到的表征吸收了平台特定的可见性效应，削弱了可解释性和跨平台迁移能力。

Method: 提出OmniTrend统一框架，包含两个模块：内容模块从视觉、音频和文本线索中学习跨模态表示以量化内在吸引力；上下文模块从发布时间、作者活跃度、主题趋势和基于检索的邻域统计等外生信号中估计曝光度。分别学习内容吸引力和上下文曝光度的独立预测器，最终整合为流行度估计值。

Result: 该方法使每个因素的作用变得明确，支持在图像和视频平台之间的鲁棒迁移，提升了可解释性和跨平台泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过将流行度分解为内容吸引力与上下文曝光度两个可解释因素并分别建模，OmniTrend有效提升了预测的可解释性和跨平台迁移能力，为社交媒体流行度预测提供了新范式。

Original Abstract: Predicting social media popularity requires understanding both the intrinsic appeal of content and the external context that determines how it is exposed to users. Existing methods focus on content signals but do not separate them from exposure-related patterns, which causes the learned representations to absorb platform-specific visibility effects and weakens both interpretability and cross-platform transfer. This paper introduces OmniTrend, a unified framework that models popularity as the joint outcome of content attractiveness and contextual exposure. The content module learns cross-modal representations from visual, audio, and textual cues to quantify intrinsic appeal, while the context module estimates exposure from exogenous signals such as posting time, author activity, topical trends, and retrieval-based neighborhood statistics. OmniTrend learns separate predictors for content attractiveness and contextual exposure and integrates them in the final popularity estimate, which makes the role of each factor explicit and supports robust transfer across image and video platforms.

### [15] [GaitKD: A Universal Decoupled Distillation Framework for Efficient Gait Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26255)
*Yuqi Li,Qian Zhou,Huiran Duan,Jingjie Wang,Shunli Zhang,Chuanguang Yang,Guoying Zhao,Yingli Tian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出GaitKD，一种针对步态识别的知识蒸馏框架，通过解耦为决策级和边界级蒸馏两个互补组件，有效将知识从复杂教师模型迁移至轻量学生模型，在多个基准上取得一致提升。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 高性能步态模型通常依赖深且计算昂贵的架构，难以实际部署；标准知识蒸馏对具有部分结构化特性的步态模型效果不佳，因为其监督同时来自部分级分类logits和部分级检索嵌入。

Method: 提出GaitKD框架，包含两个互补组件：(1) 决策级蒸馏：通过部分校准的logit蒸馏对齐师生模型，传递类间决策关系；(2) 边界级蒸馏：通过激活边界目标保留教师诱导的嵌入空间划分，替代直接特征回归。采用简单的对齐部分级设计，支持异构师生步态模型且不引入额外推理成本。

Result: 在多个步态识别基准和师生模型配置下，GaitKD相较于强基线方法取得一致改进；两种蒸馏组件互补；边界保留蒸馏比直接特征回归提供更稳定的性能。

Conclusion: 决策级和边界级蒸馏两个迁移组件具有互补性，边界保留蒸馏比直接特征回归更稳定有效，GaitKD在不增加推理成本的前提下实现了高效的步态知识迁移。

Original Abstract: Gait recognition is an attractive biometric modality for long-range and contact-free identification, but high-performing gait models often rely on deep and computationally expensive architectures that are difficult to deploy in practice. Knowledge distillation (KD) offers a natural way to transfer knowledge from a powerful teacher to an efficient student; however, standard KD is often less effective for part-structured gait models, where supervision is formed from both part-wise classification logits and part-wise retrieval embeddings. In this paper, we propose GaitKD, a distillation framework that decouples gait knowledge transfer into two complementary components: decision-level distillation and boundary-level distillation. Specifically, GaitKD aligns the teacher and student through part-calibrated logit distillation to transfer inter-class decision relations, while preserving the teacher-induced partitioning of the embedding space through an activation-boundary objective instead of direct feature regression. With a simple aligned part-wise design, GaitKD supports heterogeneous teacher-student gait models without introducing additional inference cost. Experimental results across multiple gait recognition benchmarks and teacher-student configurations show consistent improvements over strong gait baselines. Our study demonstrates that the two transfer components are complementary, and boundary-preserving distillation provides more stable performance than direct feature regression. Source code is available at https://github.com/liyiersan/GaitKD/

中文摘要翻译: 步态识别是一种适用于远距离和无接触身份识别的有吸引力的生物特征识别模态，但高性能步态模型通常依赖于深度且计算代价昂贵的架构，难以在实际中部署。知识蒸馏为将知识从强大的教师模型迁移至高效的学生模型提供了一种自然方式；然而，对于具有部分结构特性的步态模型，标准KD往往效果不佳，因为其监督信号同时来自部分级的分类logits和部分级的检索嵌入。本文提出GaitKD，一种将步态知识迁移解耦为两个互补组件的蒸馏框架：决策级蒸馏和边界级蒸馏。具体而言，GaitKD通过部分校准的logit蒸馏对齐教师和学生模型，以传递类间决策关系；同时通过激活边界目标而非直接特征回归来保留教师模型诱导的嵌入空间划分。借助简单的对齐部分级设计，GaitKD支持异构的师生步态模型，且不引入额外推理成本。在多个步态识别基准和师生模型配置下的实验结果表明，GaitKD相较于强步态基线方法取得了一致的改进。我们的研究表明，两个迁移组件具有互补性，且边界保留蒸馏比直接特征回归提供更稳定的性能。源代码已公开于https://github.com/liyiersan/GaitKD/。

### [16] [Multiple Consistent 2D-3D Mappings for Robust Zero-Shot 3D Visual Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26261)
*Yufei Yin,Jie Zheng,Qianke Meng,Zhou Yu,Minghao Chen,Jiajun Ding,Min Tan,Yuling Xi,Zhiwen Chen,Chengfei Lv*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MCM-VG通过建立多模态一致的2D-3D映射，结合语义对齐、实例修正和视点蒸馏三个模块，实现了鲁棒的零样本3D视觉定位，在ScanRefer和Nr3D基准上达到了新SOTA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有零样本3D视觉定位方法受限于开放词汇3D提案质量差（类别不准确、几何不精确）以及多视角推理的空间冗余问题，亟需更鲁棒的解决方案。

Method: 提出MCM-VG框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) 语义对齐模块，利用LLM驱动查询解析和粗到细的2D-3D匹配纠正类别错配；(2) 实例修正模块，借助VLM引导的2D分割重建缺失目标，通过反投影建立精确3D几何；(3) 视点蒸馏模块，聚类3D相机方向提取最优帧，将RGB帧与鸟瞰图组合成简洁视觉提示集，将目标消歧建模为VLM的多选推理任务。

Result: 在ScanRefer基准上，Acc@0.25达到62.0%，Acc@0.5达到53.6%，分别以6.4%和4.0%的绝对优势超越此前最优方法。

Conclusion: 通过明确建立多个一致的2D-3D映射，MCM-VG有效克服了低质量3D提案和空间冗余问题，为零样本3D视觉定位设立了新标杆。

Original Abstract: Zero-shot 3D Visual Grounding (3DVG) is a critical capability for open-world embodied AI. However, existing methods are fundamentally bottlenecked by the poor quality of open-vocabulary 3D proposals, suffering from inaccurate categories and imprecise geometries, as well as the spatial redundancy of exhaustive multi-view reasoning. To address these challenges, we propose MCM-VG, a novel framework that achieves robust zero-shot 3DVG by explicitly establishing Multiple Consistent 2D-3D Mappings. Instead of passively relying on noisy 3D segments, MCM-VG enforces 2D-3D consistency across three fundamental dimensions to achieve precise target localization and reliable reasoning. First, a Semantic Alignment module corrects category mismatches via LLM-driven query parsing and coarse-to-fine 2D-3D matching. Second, an Instance Rectification module leverages VLM-guided 2D segmentations to reconstruct missing targets, back-projecting these reliable visual priors to establish accurate 3D geometries. Finally, to eliminate spatial redundancy, a Viewpoint Distillation module clusters 3D camera directions to extract optimal frames. By pairing these optimal RGB frames with Bird's Eye View maps into concise visual prompt sets, we formulate the final target disambiguation as a multiple-choice reasoning task for Vision-Language Models.
  Extensive evaluations on ScanRefer and Nr3D benchmarks demonstrate that MCM-VG sets a new state-of-the-art for zero-shot 3D visual grounding. Remarkably, it achieves 62.0\% and 53.6\% in Acc@0.25 and Acc@0.5 on ScanRefer, outperforming previous baselines by substantial margins of 6.4\% and 4.0\%.

中文摘要翻译: 零样本3D视觉定位（3DVG）是开放世界具身智能的关键能力。然而，现有方法从根本上受限于开放词汇3D提案质量差——类别不准确且几何不精确——以及穷举式多视角推理的空间冗余问题。为解决这些挑战，我们提出MCM-VG，一种通过明确建立多个一致的2D-3D映射来实现鲁棒零样本3DVG的新颖框架。MCM-VG不被动依赖有噪声的3D分割结果，而是在三个基本维度上强制2D-3D一致性，以实现精确的目标定位和可靠的推理。首先，语义对齐模块通过LLM驱动的查询解析和由粗到细的2D-3D匹配来纠正类别错配。其次，实例修正模块利用VLM引导的2D分割来重建缺失目标，将这些可靠的视觉先验反投影以建立精确的3D几何结构。最后，为消除空间冗余，视点蒸馏模块对3D相机方向进行聚类以提取最优帧。通过将这些最优RGB帧与鸟瞰图配对成简洁的视觉提示集，我们将最终的目标消歧建模为视觉语言模型的多选推理任务。在ScanRefer和Nr3D基准上的大量评估表明，MCM-VG为零样本3D视觉定位设立了新的最先进水平。值得注意的是，它在ScanRefer上的Acc@0.25和Acc@0.5分别达到62.0%和53.6%，以6.4%和4.0%的显著优势超越了此前基线方法。

### [17] [Semantic Foam: Unifying Spatial and Semantic Scene Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26262)
*Amr Sharafeldin,Shrisudhan Govindarajan,Thomas Walker,Aryan Mikaeili,Daniel Rebain,Kwang Moo Yi,Andrea Tagliasacchi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Semantic Foam，基于Radiant Foam的体素Voronoi网格结构，通过在每个单元上定义显式语义特征场，实现空间正则化，提升语义分割的跨视图一致性和遮挡鲁棒性，在物体级分割任务上优于Gaussian Grouping和SAGA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有3D场景重建方法（如3D Gaussian Splatting）虽能实现实时照片级新视图合成，但难以与传统人工3D资产交互；已有的语义分解方法在分割质量和跨视图一致性方面仍存在显著挑战。

Method: 扩展Radiant Foam表示，利用其体素Voronoi网格的固有空间结构，在每个单元级别上增加显式语义特征场，通过直接空间正则化提升跨视图一致性，缓解遮挡和不一致监督引起的伪影。

Result: 在物体级分割任务上，该方法优于当前最先进的Gaussian Grouping和SAGA方法。

Conclusion: 基于Radiant Foam的体素结构引入显式语义特征场，能够有效提升语义分割的跨视图一致性和遮挡鲁棒性，为交互式图形应用中的语义分解提供了新的有效方案。

Original Abstract: Modern scene reconstruction methods, such as 3D Gaussian Splatting, enable photo-realistic novel view synthesis at real-time speeds. However, their adoption in interactive graphics applications remains limited due to the difficulty of interacting with these representations compared to traditional, human-authored 3D assets. While prior work has attempted to impose semantic decomposition on these models, significant challenges remain in segmentation quality and cross-view consistency.To address these limitations, we introduce Semantic Foam, which extends the recently proposed Radiant Foam representation to semantic decomposition tasks. Our approach leverages the inherent spatial structure of Radiant Foam's volumetric Voronoi mesh and augments it with an explicit semantic feature field defined at the cell level. This design enables direct spatial regularization, improving consistency across views and mitigating artifacts caused by occlusion and inconsistent supervision, which are common issues in point-based representations.Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves superior object-level segmentation performance compared to state-of-the-art approaches such as Gaussian Grouping and SAGA.Project page: http://semanticfoam.github.io/

中文摘要翻译: 现代场景重建方法（如3D高斯泼溅）能够以实时速度实现照片级的新视图合成。然而，由于与这些表示形式交互的难度相较于传统人工制作的3D资产更大，它们在交互式图形应用中的采用仍然有限。虽然先前的工作尝试对这些模型施加语义分解，但在分割质量和跨视图一致性方面仍然存在显著挑战。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了Semantic Foam，它将最近提出的Radiant Foam表示扩展到了语义分解任务。我们的方法利用了Radiant Foam的体素Voronoi网格固有的空间结构，并在单元级别上为其增加了显式语义特征场。这种设计能够实现直接的空间正则化，从而提升跨视图的一致性，并减轻由遮挡和不一致监督引起的伪影——而这些是基于点的表示中常见的问题。实验结果表明，与Gaussian Grouping和SAGA等最先进方法相比，我们的方法在物体级分割性能上取得了更优的结果。

</details>


### [18] [High-Dimensional Noise to Low-Dimensional Manifolds: A Manifold-Space Diffusion Framework for Degraded Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26279)
*Boxiang Yang,Ning Chen,Xia Yue,Yichang Luo,Yingbo Fan,Haoyuan Zhang,Haoyu Ma,Jun Yue,Shanjun Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个流形空间扩散框架（MSDiff），通过将高光谱图像映射到低维流形并利用扩散模型正则化分布，实现对复杂退化条件下的鲁棒分类。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 高光谱数据本质高维低秩，判别信息集中在低维潜在流形上，但真实场景中的多种退化因素会破坏这种流形结构，引入冗余和非判别性变化，现有方法难以有效应对。

Method: 首先通过判别性光谱-空间重建任务将退化影响的高维HSI数据映射到紧凑的低维流形，保留类别语义并减少冗余变化；然后在该流形上应用扩散生成模型正则化光谱-空间分布，逐步细化和稳定潜在特征以抵抗残留退化。

Result: 在多个高光谱基准数据集上，MSDiff在多种复合退化设置下均取得优于现有最先进方法的一致性性能提升。

Conclusion: 在低维流形上直接进行扩散分布建模，能够有效解耦退化引起的扰动与内在判别结构，增强复杂退化下的表示稳定性，为鲁棒高光谱分类提供了有效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Recently, Hyperspectral Image (HSI) classification has attracted increasing attention in remote sensing. However, HSI data are inherently high-dimensional but low-rank, with discriminative information concentrated on a low-dimensional latent manifold. In real-world remote sensing scenarios, the superposition of multiple degradation factors disrupts this intrinsic manifold structure, driving samples away from their original low-dimensional distribution and introducing substantial redundant and non-discriminative variations. To better handle this challenge, this paper proposes a manifold-space diffusion framework (MSDiff) for robust hyperspectral classification under complex degradation conditions. Specifically, the proposed method first maps high-dimensional, degradation-affected HSI data into a compact low-dimensional manifold through a discriminative spectral-spatial reconstruction task, preserving class semantics and reducing redundant variations. A diffusion-based generative model is then applied to regularize the spectral-spatial distribution within the manifold, enabling progressive refinement and stabilization of latent features against residual degradations. The key advantage of the proposed framework lies in performing diffusion-based distribution modeling directly on the low-dimensional manifold, effectively decoupling degradation-induced disturbances from intrinsic discriminative structures and enhancing representation stability under complex degradations. Experimental results on multiple hyperspectral benchmarks demonstrate consistent performance improvements over state-of-the-art methods under diverse composite degradation settings. The code will be available at https://github.com/yangboxiang1207/MSDiff

中文摘要翻译: 近年来，高光谱图像分类在遥感领域引起了越来越多的关注。然而，HSI数据本质上是高维且低秩的，其判别信息集中在低维潜在流形上。在真实遥感场景中，多种退化因素的叠加破坏了这一内在流形结构，使样本偏离其原始低维分布，并引入大量冗余和非判别性变化。为了更好地应对这一挑战，本文提出了一种流形空间扩散框架（MSDiff），用于复杂退化条件下的鲁棒高光谱分类。具体而言，该方法首先通过判别性光谱-空间重建任务，将受到退化影响的高维HSI数据映射到一个紧凑的低维流形上，以保留类别语义并减少冗余变化。然后，在该流形上应用基于扩散的生成模型来正则化光谱-空间分布，从而对潜在特征进行逐步细化和稳定，以抵抗残留退化。该框架的关键优势在于直接在低维流形上执行基于扩散的分布建模，有效解耦退化引起的扰动与内在判别结构，增强复杂退化下的表示稳定性。在多个高光谱基准数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在多种复合退化设置下均取得了优于现有最先进方法的一致性性能提升。代码将在 https://github.com/yangboxiang1207/MSDiff 上发布。

</details>


### [19] [MedSynapse-V: Bridging Visual Perception and Clinical Intuition via Latent Memory Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26283)
*Chunzheng Zhu,Jiaqi Zeng,Junyu Jiang,Jianxin Lin,Yijun Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种隐式诊断记忆演化框架，通过在模型隐空间动态合成临床医生的内隐诊断记忆，解决医学视觉语言模型中由离散分词导致的认知偏差问题，在多个数据集上显著超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有医学视觉语言模型（VLM）因离散分词导致量化损失、长程信息消散及缺乏病例自适应专家知识，与临床医生在影像判读时即时调用的隐式诊断记忆存在根本性的认知错位。

Method: 提出三个核心模块：1) 元查询先验记忆化（Meta Query for Prior Memorization），通过可学习探针从解剖先验编码器检索结构化先验生成压缩隐式记忆；2) 因果反事实精炼（CCR），利用强化学习和基于区域特征掩蔽的反事实奖励量化记忆的因果贡献，剪枝冗余；3) 内在记忆转移（IMT），采用特权-自主双分支范式，通过全词汇散度对齐将教师分支的诊断模式内化到学生分支。

Result: 在多个数据集上的综合实验表明，该框架通过将外部专家知识转化为内生参数，在诊断准确率上显著优于现有最先进方法，特别是思维链（chain-of-thought）范式的方法。

Conclusion: 通过在模型隐空间演化隐式诊断记忆，能够有效弥合医学VLM与临床专家之间的认知鸿沟，将外部专家知识内化为模型自身参数，从而提升诊断性能。

Original Abstract: High-precision medical diagnosis relies not only on static imaging features but also on the implicit diagnostic memory experts instantly invoke during image interpretation. We pinpoint a fundamental cognitive misalignment in medical VLMs caused by discrete tokenization, leading to quantization loss, long-range information dissipation, and missing case-adaptive expertise. To bridge this gap, we propose ours, a framework for latent diagnostic memory evolution that simulates the experiential invocation of clinicians by dynamically synthesizing implicit diagnostic memories within the model's hidden stream. Specifically, it begins with a Meta Query for Prior Memorization mechanism, where learnable probes retrieve structured priors from an anatomical prior encoder to generate condensed implicit memories. To ensure clinical fidelity, we introduce Causal Counterfactual Refinement (CCR), which leverages reinforcement learning and counterfactual rewards derived from region-level feature masking to quantify the causal contribution of each memory, thereby pruning redundancies and aligning latent representations with diagnostic logic. This evolutionary process culminates in Intrinsic Memory Transition (IMT), a privileged-autonomous dual-branch paradigm that internalizes teacher-branch diagnostic patterns into the student-branch via full-vocabulary divergence alignment. Comprehensive empirical evaluations across multiple datasets demonstrate that ours, by transferring external expertise into endogenous parameters, significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods, particularly chain-of-thought paradigms, in diagnostic accuracy.

中文摘要翻译: 高精度医学诊断不仅依赖于静态影像特征，还依赖于专家在图像解读过程中即时调用的隐式诊断记忆。我们发现医学视觉语言模型（VLM）存在一种由离散分词导致的根本性认知错位，表现为量化损失、长程信息消散以及缺乏病例自适应的专家知识。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了ours——一个隐式诊断记忆演化框架，通过在模型隐式流中动态合成隐式诊断记忆来模拟临床医生的经验性调用。具体而言，该框架首先引入元查询先验记忆化机制，通过可学习探针从解剖先验编码器中检索结构化先验，生成压缩的隐式记忆。为确保临床保真度，我们提出了因果反事实精炼（CCR），利用强化学习和源自区域级特征掩蔽的反事实奖励来量化每个记忆的因果贡献，从而剪枝冗余并使隐式表示与诊断逻辑对齐。该演化过程最终进入内在记忆转移（IMT），一种特权-自主双分支范式，通过全词汇散度对齐将教师分支的诊断模式内化到学生分支。跨多个数据集的综合实证评估表明，ours通过将外部专家知识转化为内生参数，在诊断准确率上显著优于现有最先进方法，特别是思维链范式的方法。

</details>


### [20] [CheXthought: A global multimodal dataset of clinical chain-of-thought reasoning and visual attention for chest X-ray interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26288)
*Sonali Sharma,Jin Long,George Shih,Sarah Eid,Christian Bluethgen,Francine L. Jacobson,Emily B. Tsai,Global Radiology Consortium,Ahmed M. Alaa,Curtis P. Langlotz*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了CheXthought，一个包含103,592条思维链推理轨迹和6,609,082个视觉注意力标注的多模态资源，覆盖71个国家501位放射科医师对50,312张胸部X光片的解读，用于提升视觉-语言模型在临床推理中的事实准确性、空间定位能力和可解释性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前视觉-语言模型主要基于配对图像和报告训练，缺乏支撑临床推理的认知过程和视觉注意力信息，导致模型在事实准确性、空间定位和可解释性方面存在不足。

Method: 构建了包含思维链推理轨迹（103,592条）和同步视觉注意力标注（6,609,082个）的多模态数据集CheXthought，覆盖50,312张多读者胸部X光片；并基于该数据训练视觉-语言模型，利用注意力数据作为推理时提示以恢复遗漏发现和减少幻觉。

Result: CheXthought推理在事实准确性和空间定位上显著优于现有最先进视觉-语言模型思维链；视觉注意力作为推理时提示可恢复遗漏发现并显著减少幻觉；基于CheXthought训练的模型在病理分类、视觉忠实性、时间推理和不确定性沟通方面表现更强；利用多读者标注可直接从图像预测人-人和人-AI分歧。

Conclusion: CheXthought作为推进多模态临床推理及开发更透明、可解释视觉-语言模型的资源，能够有效提升模型的事实准确性、减少幻觉，并实现案例难度和不确定性的透明沟通。

Original Abstract: Chest X-ray interpretation is one of the most frequently performed diagnostic tasks in medicine and a primary target for AI development, yet current vision--language models are primarily trained on datasets of paired images and reports, not the cognitive processes and visual attention that underlie clinical reasoning. Here, we present CheXthought, a global, multimodal resource containing 103,592 chain-of-thought reasoning traces and 6,609,082 synchronized visual attention annotations across 50,312 multi-read chest X-rays from 501 radiologists in 71 countries. Our analysis reveals clinical reasoning patterns in how experts deploy distinct visual search strategies, integrate clinical context, and communicate uncertainty. We demonstrate the clinical utility of CheXthought across four dimensions. First, CheXthought reasoning significantly outperforms state--of--the--art vision--language model chain-of-thought in factual accuracy and spatial grounding. Second, visual attention data used as an inference--time hint recovers missed findings and significantly reduces hallucinations. Third, models trained on CheXthought data achieve significantly stronger pathology classification, visual faithfulness, temporal reasoning and uncertainty communication. Fourth, leveraging CheXthought's multi-reader annotations, we predict both human--human and human--AI disagreement directly from an image, enabling transparent communication of case difficulty, uncertainty and model reliability. These findings establish CheXthought as a resource for advancing multimodal clinical reasoning and the development of more transparent, interpretable vision--language models.

中文摘要翻译: 胸部X光片解读是医学中最常执行的诊断任务之一，也是人工智能开发的主要目标，然而当前的视觉-语言模型主要基于配对的图像和报告数据集进行训练，而非支撑临床推理的认知过程和视觉注意力。本文提出CheXthought，这是一个全球性的多模态资源，包含来自71个国家501名放射科医师对50,312张多读者胸部X光片的103,592条思维链推理轨迹和6,609,082个同步视觉注意力标注。我们的分析揭示了专家在部署不同视觉搜索策略、整合临床背景以及沟通不确定性方面的临床推理模式。我们从四个维度展示了CheXthought的临床实用性。第一，CheXthought推理在事实准确性和空间定位上显著优于最先进的视觉-语言模型思维链。第二，作为推理时提示使用的视觉注意力数据能够恢复遗漏的发现并显著减少幻觉。第三，基于CheXthought数据训练的模型在病理分类、视觉忠实性、时间推理和不确定性沟通方面表现显著更强。第四，利用CheXthought的多读者标注，我们能够直接从图像预测人-人和人-AI之间的分歧，从而实现案例难度、不确定性和模型可靠性的透明沟通。这些发现确立了CheXthought作为推进多模态临床推理以及开发更透明、可解释的视觉-语言模型的重要资源。

### [21] [Point Cloud Registration via Probabilistic Self-Update Local Correspondence and Line Vector Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26318)
*Kuo-Liang Chung,Yu-Cheng Lin,Wu-Chi Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于概率自更新局部对应与线向量集的双RANSAC点云配准算法，在保证精度的同时显著提升时间效率，RMSE改善至少10%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有点云配准方法在精度与效率之间存在权衡，尤其是在处理大规模点云时，计算开销大、收敛速度慢，亟需一种快速且有效的配准算法。

Method: 提出双RANSAC交互模型：全局RANSAC评估全局对应集，局部RANSAC操作于动态更新的局部集。局部集通过角度直方图统计和线向量长度保持技术构建；采用概率自更新策略每轮交互后优化局部集；引入全局早停条件平衡精度与效率；最后用加权奇异值分解估计配准解。

Result: 在公开数据集上的评估表明，所提算法在时间效率上优于现有方法，且均方根误差（RMSE）相比最先进方法改善至少10%。

Conclusion: 基于概率自更新局部对应与线向量集的双RANSAC框架能够有效兼顾点云配准的精度与效率，具有实际应用价值。

Original Abstract: Point cloud registration (PCR) is a fundamental task for integrating 3D observations in remote sensing applications. This paper proposes a fast and effective PCR algorithm utilizing probabilistic self-updating local correspondence and line vector sets. Our dual RANSAC interaction model comprises a global RANSAC evaluating the global correspondence set and a local RANSAC operating on dynamically updated local sets. Initially, these local sets are constructed using angle histogram statistics and line vector length preservation techniques. To improve accuracy, a probabilistic self-updating strategy refines the local sets after each interaction round. To reduce runtime, we introduce a global early termination condition that optimally balances accuracy and efficiency. Finally, a weighted singular value decomposition estimates the registration solution. Evaluations on public datasets demonstrate our algorithm achieves superior time efficiency and at least a 10% root mean square error improvement over state-of-the-art methods. The C++ source code is publicly available at https://github.com/ivpml84079/Probabilistic-Self-Update-Line-Vector-Set-Based-Point-Cloud-Registration.

中文摘要翻译: 点云配准（PCR）是遥感应用中整合三维观测数据的基础任务。本文提出一种利用概率自更新局部对应与线向量集的快速有效点云配准算法。我们的双RANSAC交互模型包括一个评估全局对应集的全局RANSAC和一个在动态更新局部集上操作的局部RANSAC。初始时，这些局部集通过角度直方图统计和线向量长度保持技术构建。为提高精度，每轮交互后采用概率自更新策略优化局部集。为减少运行时间，我们引入全局早停条件，以最优平衡精度与效率。最后，采用加权奇异值分解估计配准解。在公开数据集上的评估表明，我们的算法实现了优越的时间效率，且均方根误差相比最先进方法改善至少10%。C++源代码已公开在 https://github.com/ivpml84079/Probabilistic-Self-Update-Line-Vector-Set-Based-Point-Cloud-Registration。

### [22] [Motion-Driven Multi-Object Tracking of Model Organisms in Space Science Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26321)
*Jianing You,Han Wang,Kang Liu,Jiale Ding,Fengjie Chu,Zihan Guo,Shengyang Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ART-Track运动驱动跟踪框架，专为微重力条件下弱外观线索的多动物视频跟踪设计，显著减少了斑马鱼和果蝇序列中的身份切换，为下游行为分析提供可靠基础。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 空间科学实验视频中多动物跟踪面临外观线索弱、成像质量低、运动复杂、交互频繁等挑战，现有方法难以在微重力条件下实现长期、可解释的个体轨迹跟踪。

Method: 首先构建SpaceAnimal-MOT数据集以刻画微重力下运动复杂性；提出ART-Track框架，包含：（1）多模型运动估计处理突变机动和非线性运动；（2）运动状态驱动关联减少密集交互下的身份切换；（3）不确定性自适应融合动态平衡空间线索与运动线索。

Result: 在斑马鱼和果蝇序列上，ART-Track显著减少了身份切换次数，并在遮挡、形变和高密度交互下保持更稳定的关联，为定量行为分析提供更可靠的跟踪基础。

Conclusion: ART-Track有效解决了微重力环境下多动物视频跟踪的难点，在复杂场景下表现优于现有方法，代码已开源。

Original Abstract: Automated animal behavior analysis relies on long-term, interpretable individual trajectories; however, multi-animal tracking in space science experimental videos remains highly challenging due to weak appearance cues, low-quality imaging, complex maneuvering behaviors, and frequent interactions. To address this problem, we first construct the SpaceAnimal-MOT dataset to characterize the motion complexity and long-term identity preservation challenges in biological videos acquired under microgravity conditions. We then propose ART-Track (Adaptive Robust Tracking), a motion-driven tracking framework tailored to this setting. Specifically, multi-model motion estimation is introduced to handle abrupt maneuvers and nonlinear motion, motion-state-driven association is designed to reduce identity switches under dense interactions and temporary mismatch, and uncertainty-adaptive fusion is used to dynamically balance spatial and motion cues when prediction reliability varies. Experimental results show that ART-Track significantly reduces identity switches on zebrafish and fruitfly sequences, while maintaining more stable association under occlusion, deformation, and high-density interactions, thereby providing a more reliable tracking foundation for downstream quantitative behavior analysis. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/yyy7777777/ART_TRACK/tree/main.

中文摘要翻译: 自动化动物行为分析依赖于长期、可解释的个体轨迹；然而，空间科学实验视频中的多动物跟踪由于弱外观线索、低质量成像、复杂机动行为和频繁交互而极具挑战性。为解决这一问题，我们首先构建了SpaceAnimal-MOT数据集，以刻画微重力条件下获取的生物视频中的运动复杂性和长期身份保持挑战。随后，我们提出ART-Track（自适应鲁棒跟踪），一种针对该场景定制的运动驱动跟踪框架。具体而言，引入多模型运动估计以处理突变机动和非线性运动，设计运动状态驱动关联以减少密集交互和临时失配下的身份切换，并采用不确定性自适应融合在预测可靠性变化时动态平衡空间线索与运动线索。实验结果表明，ART-Track在斑马鱼和果蝇序列上显著减少了身份切换，同时在遮挡、形变和高密度交互下保持更稳定的关联，从而为下游定量行为分析提供更可靠的跟踪基础。代码已开源：https://github.com/yyy7777777/ART_TRACK/tree/main。

### [23] [Federated Medical Image Classification under Class and Domain Imbalance exploiting Synthetic Sample Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26324)

### [24] [SpatialFusion: Endowing Unified Image Generation with Intrinsic 3D Geometric Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26341)
*Haiyi Qiu,Kaihang Pan,Jiacheng Li,Juncheng Li,Siliang Tang,Yueting Zhuang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SpatialFusion框架，通过混合Transformer架构增强MLLM的3D几何建模能力，并将显式深度图注入扩散骨干，实现空间感知的统一图像生成，在空间感知任务上超越GPT-4o。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有统一图像生成模型虽然结合了MLLM的语义理解与扩散模型的生成能力，但由于缺乏内在的空间理解和显式几何引导，在空间感知任务中表现受限。

Method: 1) 采用混合Transformer架构，在MLLM基础上增加并行空间Transformer，通过共享自注意力机制增强3D几何建模；2) 空间Transformer从语义上下文中学习推导目标的度量深度图；3) 通过专门的深度适配器将深度图注入扩散骨干，提供精确空间约束；4) 采用渐进式两阶段训练策略。

Result: 在空间感知基准上显著提升性能，优于GPT-4o等领先模型；在文本到图像生成和图像编辑场景中均取得泛化性能提升，且推理开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 将显式3D几何感知内化到统一图像生成模型中是可行且有效的，能够在几乎不增加推理成本的情况下大幅提升空间感知能力。

Original Abstract: Recent unified image generation models have achieved remarkable success by employing MLLMs for semantic understanding and diffusion backbones for image generation. However, these models remain fundamentally limited in spatially-aware tasks due to a lack of intrinsic spatial understanding and the absence of explicit geometric guidance during generation. In this paper, we propose SpatialFusion, a novel framework that internalizes 3D geometric awareness into unified image generation models. Specifically, we first employ a Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) architecture to augment the MLLM with a parallel spatial transformer to enhance 3D geometric modeling capability. By sharing self-attention with the MLLM, the spatial transformer learns to derive metric-depth maps of target images from rich semantic contexts. These explicit geometric scaffolds are then injected into the diffusion backbone through a specialized depth adapter, providing precise spatial constraints for spatially-coherent image generation. Through a progressive two-stage training strategy, SpatialFusion significantly enhances performance on spatially-aware benchmarks, notably outperforming leading models such as GPT-4o. Additionally, it achieves generalized performance gains across both text-to-image generation and image editing scenarios, all while maintaining negligible inference overhead.

中文摘要翻译: 近期，统一图像生成模型通过结合多模态大语言模型进行语义理解和扩散骨干进行图像生成取得了显著成功。然而，这些模型由于缺乏内在的空间理解以及在生成过程中缺少显式的几何引导，在空间感知任务中仍然存在根本性的局限。本文提出SpatialFusion，一种将3D几何感知内化到统一图像生成模型中的新型框架。具体而言，我们首先采用混合Transformer架构，通过并行的空间Transformer增强多模态大语言模型的3D几何建模能力。通过共享自注意力机制，空间Transformer学会从丰富的语义上下文中推导出目标图像的度量深度图。这些显式的几何支架通过专门的深度适配器注入扩散骨干，为空间一致的图像生成提供精确的空间约束。通过渐进式两阶段训练策略，SpatialFusion在空间感知基准上显著提升了性能，尤其超越了GPT-4o等领先模型。此外，该方法在文本到图像生成和图像编辑场景中均取得了泛化性能提升，同时保持了可忽略不计的推理开销。

### [25] [ACPO: Anchor-Constrained Perceptual Optimization for Diffusion Models with No-Reference Quality Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26348)
*Yang Yang,Feifan Meng,Han Fang,Weiming Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种锚点约束优化框架，将无参考感知质量（NR-IQA）融入扩散模型训练，解决了直接优化感知信号导致的训练不稳定和分布漂移问题，在保持生成多样性和保真度的同时提升感知质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有扩散模型训练主要依赖全参考目标（如像素级相似度），虽然保证了保真度，但在主观视觉感知质量和文本-图像语义一致性方面存在不足。直接引入无参考感知质量信号会产生与原始扩散目标不匹配的问题，导致训练不稳定和分布漂移。

Method: 提出锚点约束优化框架：利用学习的NR-IQA模型提供感知引导信号，同时引入基于锚点的正则化项，强制微调模型在噪声预测上与基础扩散模型保持一致，从而在提升感知质量与保持生成保真度之间取得平衡。

Result: 实验表明该方法能一致性地提升感知质量，同时保持生成多样性和训练稳定性，验证了锚点约束感知优化的有效性。

Conclusion: 锚点约束优化框架能够有效将无参考感知质量融入扩散模型训练，解决了训练不稳定和分布漂移问题，实现了感知质量提升与生成保真度的平衡。

Original Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in image generation, yet their training is predominantly driven by full-reference objectives that enforce pixel-wise similarity to ground-truth images.Such supervision, while effective for fidelity, may insufficient in terms of subjective visual perception quality and text-image semantic consistency. In this work, we investigate the problem of incorporating no-reference perceptual quality into diffusion training. A key challenge is that directly optimizing perceptual signals, such as those provided by no-reference image quality assessment (NR-IQA) models, introduces a mismatch with the original diffusion objective, leading to training instability and distributional drift during fine-tuning. To address this issue, we propose an anchor-constrained optimization framework that enables stable perceptual adaptation. Specifically, we leverage a learned NR-IQA model as a perceptual guidance signal, while introducing an anchor-based regularization that enforces consistency with the base diffusion model in terms of noise prediction. This design effectively balances perceptual quality improvement and generative fidelity, allowing controlled adaptation toward perceptually favorable outputs without compromising the original generative behavior. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method consistently enhances perceptual quality while preserving generation diversity and training stability, highlighting the effectiveness of anchor-constrained perceptual optimization for diffusion models.

中文摘要翻译: 扩散模型在图像生成领域取得了显著成功，但其训练主要依赖全参考目标函数，强制生成图像与真实图像在像素级别保持相似。这种监督方式虽然能保证保真度，但在主观视觉感知质量和文本-图像语义一致性方面可能不足。本文研究了将无参考感知质量融入扩散训练的问题。一个关键挑战在于：直接优化感知信号（例如无参考图像质量评估模型提供的信号）会与原始扩散目标产生不匹配，导致微调过程中的训练不稳定和分布漂移。为解决这一问题，我们提出了一种锚点约束优化框架，实现了稳定的感知适应。具体而言，我们利用学习到的无参考图像质量评估模型作为感知引导信号，同时引入基于锚点的正则化项，强制微调模型在噪声预测上与基础扩散模型保持一致。这种设计有效平衡了感知质量提升与生成保真度，允许在不对原始生成行为造成损害的前提下，向感知上更优的输出进行受控适应。大量实验证明，我们的方法能够一致性地提升感知质量，同时保持生成多样性和训练稳定性，验证了锚点约束感知优化对扩散模型的有效性。

### [26] [GateMOT: Q-Gated Attention for Dense Object Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26353)
*Mingjin Lv,Zelin Liu,Feifei Shao,Yi-Ping Phoebe Chen,Junqing Yu,Wei Yang,Zikai Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GateMOT提出基于Q-Gated Attention（Q-Attention）的高效注意力变体，将Query改造为可学习的门控单元，实现线性复杂度的密集目标跟踪，在BEE24等数据集上达到SOTA性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准注意力机制的二次复杂度不适用于高分辨率特征上的密集运动估计，导致Dense Object Tracking在拥挤和严重遮挡场景中无法充分利用基于注意力的建模能力。

Method: 提出Q-Gated Attention（Q-Attention），将Query从相似性条件项改造为可学习的门控单元（Gating-Query），生成概率门对Key特征进行逐元素调制，实现显式相关性选择而非全局聚合；并行Q-Attention多头将共享特征图转化为检测、运动和重识别任务的特异性表示，构成线性复杂度的紧耦合多任务解码器。

Result: 在BEE24上达到HOTA 48.4、MOTA 67.8、IDF1 64.5的SOTA结果，并在多个密集目标跟踪基准上表现强劲。

Conclusion: Q-Attention是一种简单、有效且可迁移的注意力构建模块，适用于密集跟踪场景中的注意力跟踪。

Original Abstract: While large models demonstrate the strong representational power of vanilla attention, this core mechanism cannot be directly applied to Dense Object Tracking: its quadratic all-to-all interactions are computationally prohibitive for dense motion estimation on high-resolution features. This mismatch prevents Dense Object Tracking from fully leveraging attention-based modeling in crowded and occlusion-heavy scenes. To address this challenge, we introduce GateMOT, an online tracking framework centered on Q-Gated Attention (Q-Attention), an efficient and spatially aware attention variant. Our key idea is to repurpose the Query from a similarity-conditioning term into a learnable gating unit. This Gating-Query (Gating-Q) produces a probabilistic gate that modulates Key features in an element-wise manner, enabling explicit relevance selection instead of costly global aggregation. Built on this mechanism, parallel Q-Attention heads transform one shared feature map into task-specific yet consistent representations for detection, motion, and re-identification, yielding a tightly coupled multi-task decoder with linear-complexity gating operations. GateMOT achieves state-of-the-art HOTA of 48.4, MOTA of 67.8, and IDF1 of 64.5 on BEE24, and demonstrates strong performance on additional Dense Object Tracking benchmarks. These results show that Q-Attention is a simple, effective, and transferable building block for attention-based tracking in dense tracking scenarios.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管大模型展示了普通注意力机制强大的表示能力，但这一核心机制无法直接应用于密集目标跟踪：其二次方的全对全交互在高分辨率特征上进行密集运动估计时计算代价过高。这种不匹配阻碍了密集目标跟踪在拥挤和严重遮挡场景中充分利用基于注意力的建模。为此，我们提出GateMOT，一种以Q-Gated Attention（Q-Attention）为核心的在线跟踪框架，这是一种高效且具有空间感知能力的注意力变体。我们的关键思想是将Query从相似性条件项重新设计为可学习的门控单元。该门控查询（Gating-Q）生成一个概率门，以逐元素方式调制Key特征，从而实现显式的相关性选择而非昂贵的全局聚合。基于这一机制，并行的Q-Attention多头将共享特征图转化为检测、运动和重识别的任务特异性且一致的表示，构成一个具有线性复杂度门控操作的紧耦合多任务解码器。GateMOT在BEE24上达到了HOTA 48.4、MOTA 67.8和IDF1 64.5的SOTA结果，并在多个密集目标跟踪基准上展现出强劲性能。这些结果表明，Q-Attention是密集跟踪场景中基于注意力跟踪的一种简单、有效且可迁移的构建模块。

</details>


### [27] [CO-EVO: Co-evolving Semantic Anchoring and Style Diversification for Federated DG-ReID](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26363)
*Fengchun Zhang,Qiang Ma,Liuyu Xiang,Jinshan Lai,Tingxuan Huang,Jianwei Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CO-EVO联邦学习框架，通过语义净化（CSA）和风格多样化（GSD）协同演化机制，解决联邦域泛化行人重识别中的风格偏差问题，实现跨域鲁棒泛化并达到SOTA性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 联邦域泛化行人重识别面临跨客户端风格差异导致的捷径学习问题，模型容易过拟合到特定域的相机偏差而非通用身份特征，且缺乏全局监督使得这一挑战更为严峻。

Method: 提出CO-EVO框架，包含三部分：(1) Camera-Invariant Semantic Anchoring (CSA)：学习跨相机一致的语义锚点，过滤局部成像噪声；(2) Global Style Diversification (GSD) + Global Camera-Style Bank (GCSB)：合成逼真的风格扰动，扩展训练数据视觉边界；(3) 协同演化循环：净化后的语义锚点作为引力中心，引导图像编码器在不同风格变化中学习鲁棒的解剖学属性。

Result: 大量实验表明CO-EVO达到SOTA性能，验证了语义净化与风格扩展的协同作用对鲁棒跨域泛化的必要性。

Conclusion: 语义净化与风格多样化之间的协同演化机制是解决联邦域泛化行人重识别中语义-风格冲突的关键，证明了该范式对跨域泛化的有效性。

Original Abstract: Federated domain generalization for person re-identification (FedDG-ReID) aims to collaboratively train a pedestrian retrieval model across multiple decentralized source domains such that it can generalize to unseen target environments without compromising raw data privacy. However, this task is significantly challenged by the inherent stylistic gaps across decentralized clients. Without global supervision, models easily succumb to shortcut learning where representations overfit to domain specific camera biases rather than universal identity features. We propose CO-EVO, a novel federated framework that resolves this semantic-style conflict through a co-evolutionary mechanism. On the semantic side, Camera-Invariant Semantic Anchoring (CSA) learns identity prompts with cross-camera consistency to establish purified and domain-agnostic anchors that filter out local imaging noise. On the visual side, Global Style Diversification (GSD), powered by a Global Camera-Style Bank (GCSB), synthesizes realistic perturbations to expand the visual boundaries of training data. The core of CO-EVO is its co-evolutionary loop where purified anchors act as gravitational centers to guide the image encoder toward robust anatomical attributes amidst diverse style variations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CO-EVO achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance, proving that the synergy between semantic purification and style expansion is essential for robust cross-domain generalization. Our code is available at: https://github.com/NanYiyuzurn/ACL-LGPS-2026.

中文摘要翻译: 面向行人重识别的联邦域泛化（FedDG-ReID）旨在跨多个分散的源域协同训练行人检索模型，使其能够在无需暴露原始数据隐私的情况下泛化到未见过的目标环境。然而，该任务因分散客户端之间固有的风格差异而面临显著挑战。在缺乏全局监督的情况下，模型容易陷入捷径学习，即表示过度拟合特定的域相机偏差而非通用的身份特征。本文提出CO-EVO，一种通过协同演化机制解决这种语义-风格冲突的新型联邦框架。在语义侧，跨相机不变的语义锚定（CSA）学习具有跨相机一致性的身份提示，建立净化且域无关的锚点，以过滤局部成像噪声。在视觉侧，由全局相机风格库（GCSB）驱动的全局风格多样化（GSD）合成逼真的扰动，扩展训练数据的视觉边界。CO-EVO的核心在于其协同演化循环，其中净化后的锚点作为引力中心，引导图像编码器在不同风格变化中学习鲁棒的解剖学属性。大量实验表明，CO-EVO达到了最先进的性能，证明语义净化与风格扩展之间的协同作用对于鲁棒的跨域泛化至关重要。我们的代码可在 https://github.com/NanYiyuzurn/ACL-LGPS-2026 获取。

### [28] [Beyond Fixed Formulas: Data-Driven Linear Predictor for Efficient Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26365)
*Zhirong Shen,Rui Huang,Jiacheng Liu,Chang Zou,Peiliang Cai,Shikang Zheng,Zhengyi Shi,Liang Feng,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: L2P提出了一种可学习的线性预测器（Learnable Linear Predictor），用数据驱动的每时间步可学习权重替代手工设计的固定系数，实现DiT特征缓存的高效加速，在约20秒训练后显著优于现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有Diffusion Transformers (DiTs)的特征缓存方法依赖手工设计的预测公式，在激进跳步（aggressive skipping）下效果显著下降，需要更鲁棒的数据驱动方案。

Method: 提出L2P（Learnable Linear Predictor），一种数据驱动的特征缓存框架：用可学习的每时间步权重替换固定系数，通过训练快速（约20秒）学习从历史轨迹重构当前特征的最优线性预测。

Result: 在FLUX.1-dev上实现4.55倍FLOPs降低和4.15倍延迟加速；在Qwen-Image模型上最高支持7.18倍加速且保持高视觉保真度，远超现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 学习线性预测器对于高效DiT推理非常有效，简单数据驱动方法可大幅超越复杂手工设计的缓存策略。

Original Abstract: To address the high sampling cost of Diffusion Transformers (DiTs), feature caching offers a training-free acceleration method. However, existing methods rely on hand-crafted forecasting formulas that fail under aggressive skipping. We propose L2P (Learnable Linear Predictor), a simple data-driven caching framework that replaces fixed coefficients with learnable per-timestep weights. Rapidly trained in ~20 seconds on a single GPU, L2P accurately reconstructs current features from past trajectories. L2P significantly outperforms existing baselines: it achieves a 4.55x FLOPs reduction and 4.15x latency speedup on FLUX.1-dev, and maintains high visual fidelity under up to 7.18x acceleration on Qwen-Image models, where prior methods show noticeable quality degradation. Our results show learning linear predictors is highly effective for efficient DiT inference. Code is available at https://github.com/Aredstone/L2P-Cache.

中文摘要翻译: 为了解决扩散变换器（Diffusion Transformers, DiTs）的高采样成本问题，特征缓存提供了一种免训练的加速方法。然而，现有方法依赖手工设计的预测公式，在激进跳步下表现不佳。我们提出L2P（可学习线性预测器），一种简单的数据驱动缓存框架，用可学习的每时间步权重替换固定系数。L2P在单GPU上约20秒内快速训练完成，能准确地从历史轨迹重构当前特征。L2P显著优于现有基线：在FLUX.1-dev上实现4.55倍FLOPs降低和4.15倍延迟加速；在Qwen-Image模型上最高支持7.18倍加速且保持高视觉保真度，而先前方法在此条件下出现明显的质量退化。我们的结果表明，学习线性预测器对于高效DiT推理非常有效。代码已开源在https://github.com/Aredstone/L2P-Cache。

### [29] [Seamless Indoor-Outdoor Mapping for INGENIOUS First Responders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26368)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在大型自然灾害和人为灾难中，第一响应者不仅需要室外三维模型，还需要建筑物内部的三维空间信息。现有方法难以在无GPS环境下实现高自动化的室内外无缝建模，因此需要一种能够自主融合室内外点云的技术。

Original Abstract: In several applications it is desired to have 3D models not only from the outdoor spaces but also from inside the building. By looking at the AprilTags before entering the building, the ground-based system is registered to world coordinates. Without the further need of any global positioning, it creates a point cloud from the indoor spaces that fits with the point could from the aerial view. This allows a co-visualization of both point-clouds as a seamless indoor-outdoor 3D model in real time.

### [30] [Topology-Aware Representation Alignment for Semi-Supervised Vision-Language Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26370)
*Junwon You,Mihyun Jang,Sangwoo Mo,Jae-Hun Jung*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ToMA框架，利用持续同调提取拓扑显著边，在多模态表示之间进行对齐，提升视觉-语言模型在专业领域（如遥感、时尚检索）上的泛化能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有半监督视觉-语言学习方法仅进行成对对齐，无法建模多模态表示流形的全局结构；现有基于拓扑的对齐方法依赖持续图匹配，既不能保证几何对齐，也无法利用图像-文本配对信息。

Method: 提出拓扑感知的多模态表示对齐框架（ToMA），利用持续同调识别拓扑显著边（包括H_0死亡边和轻量H_1诞生边），通过已有的跨模态对应关系实现跨模态边对齐，无需构造2-单纯形。

Result: 在遥感数据上取得明显提升，在时尚检索上获得适度但一致的收益；ToMA比基于拓扑的替代目标更稳定，轻量H_1诞生边能提供有效的高阶结构信号。

Conclusion: ToMA通过拓扑感知的边对齐有效建模多模态表示流形的全局结构，在专业领域上稳定提升视觉-语言模型的泛化性能。

Original Abstract: Vision-language models have shown strong performance, but they often generalize poorly to specialized domains. While semi-supervised vision-language learning mitigates this limitation by leveraging a small set of labeled image-text pairs together with abundant unlabeled images, existing methods remain fundamentally pairwise and fail to model the global structure of multimodal representation manifolds. Existing topology-based alignment methods rely on persistence diagram matching, which neither guarantees geometric alignment nor utilizes the image-text pairing information central to vision-language learning. We propose Topology-Aware Multimodal Representation Alignment (ToMA), a framework that uses persistent homology to identify topologically salient edges and aligns them across modalities through available cross-modal correspondences. ToMA leverages both H_0-death edges and lightweight H_1-birth edges, allowing it to capture both connectivity and cycle structure without constructing 2-simplices. Experiments show that ToMA yields stable gains, with clear improvements on remote sensing and modest but consistent benefits on fashion retrieval. Additional analysis shows that ToMA is more stable than alternative topology-based objectives and that lightweight H_1-birth edges provide useful higher-order structural signals.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言模型表现出较强的性能，但在专业领域上通常泛化较差。尽管半监督视觉-语言学习通过利用少量标注的图像-文本对和大量无标注图像来缓解这一局限，现有方法本质上仍是成对的，无法建模多模态表示流形的全局结构。现有的基于拓扑的对齐方法依赖持续图匹配，既不能保证几何对齐，也无法利用视觉-语言学习中核心的图像-文本配对信息。我们提出拓扑感知的多模态表示对齐框架（ToMA），该框架利用持续同调识别拓扑显著边，并通过已有的跨模态对应关系在模态间对齐这些边。ToMA同时利用H_0死亡边和轻量级H_1诞生边，能够在无需构造2-单纯形的情况下捕获连通性和环结构。实验表明，ToMA取得了稳定的增益，在遥感任务上提升明显，在时尚检索上取得适度但一致的改进。进一步分析显示，ToMA比基于拓扑的替代目标更稳定，且轻量级H_1诞生边能提供有效的高阶结构信号。

### [31] [A Multimodal Pre-trained Network for Integrated EEG-Video Seizure Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26379)
*Tong Lu,Ke Xu,Zimo Zhang,Zitong Zhao,Danwei Weng,Ruiyu Wang,Miao Liu,Zizuo Zhang,Jingyi Yao,Yixuan Zhao,Wenchao Zhang,Min Wang,Guoming Luan,Minmin Luo,Zhifeng Yue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出EEGVFusion，一种结合自监督EEG表示学习、时空视频编码、最优传输对齐和双向交叉注意力的多模态框架，用于小鼠癫痫发作检测，在两个评估设定下均实现了高平衡准确率和低误报率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 手动审阅同步视频-EEG记录耗时耗力，而单模态系统存在互补性缺陷：视频方法易被良性行为混淆，EEG方法易受发作期运动伪影干扰。因此需要一种多模态融合框架来整合神经和行为证据。

Method: 提出EEGVFusion多模态框架，包含四个关键组件：自监督EEG表示学习、时空视频编码、最优传输对齐（OT alignment）以及双向交叉注意力机制，用于融合EEG和视频模态信息。

Result: 在随机会话划分中，平衡准确率达0.9957，事件敏感性完美，事件误报率仅0.6250 FP/h。在留出受试者（Subject 110）评估中，平衡准确率达0.9718，事件误报率从EEG-only的2.7250 FP/h降至0.4833 FP/h，同时保持完美的事件敏感性。消融实验表明EEG预训练和OT对齐有助于减少误报。

Conclusion: EEGVFusion多模态融合框架能够有效整合神经和行为证据，在小鼠癫痫发作检测中显著优于单模态方法，在保持高敏感性的同时大幅降低误报率。

Original Abstract: Reliable seizure detection in mouse models is essential for preclinical epilepsy research, yet manual review of synchronized video-EEG recordings is labor-intensive and single-modality systems fail for complementary reasons: video-based methods are easily confounded by benign behaviors, whereas EEG-based methods are vulnerable to ictal motion artifacts. We present EEGVFusion, a multimodal framework that combines self-supervised EEG representation learning, spatio-temporal video encoding, optimal-transport alignment, and bidirectional cross-attention to integrate neural and behavioral evidence. We also curate an expert-annotated dataset of synchronized EEG and video recordings comprising 93 sessions from 15 mice for training and evaluation. In the random-session split, EEGVFusion achieved a Balanced Accuracy of 0.9957 with perfect event sensitivity and an Event FAR of 0.6250 FP/h, indicating strong seizure detection performance with a low false-alarm burden. In a single held-out-subject evaluation with Subject 110 reserved for testing, EEGVFusion achieved a Balanced Accuracy of 0.9718 and reduced Event FAR from 2.7250 FP/h for the EEG-only counterpart to 0.4833 FP/h while preserving perfect event sensitivity. Targeted ablations further showed that EEG pre-training and OT alignment help reduce false alarms while preserving event sensitivity.

中文摘要翻译: 小鼠模型中可靠的癫痫发作检测对于临床前癫痫研究至关重要，然而对同步视频-EEG记录的手动审阅耗时费力，且单模态系统因互补性原因而失效：基于视频的方法容易被良性行为混淆，而基于EEG的方法易受发作期运动伪影干扰。本文提出EEGVFusion，一个多模态框架，结合了自监督EEG表示学习、时空视频编码、最优传输对齐和双向交叉注意力机制，以整合神经和行为证据。我们还整理了一个专家标注的同步EEG和视频记录数据集，包含15只小鼠的93个会话用于训练和评估。在随机会话划分中，EEGVFusion实现了0.9957的平衡准确率，具有完美的事件敏感性和0.6250 FP/h的事件误报率，表明其具有强癫痫检测性能和低误报负担。在留出单个受试者评估（Subject 110保留用于测试）中，EEGVFusion实现了0.9718的平衡准确率，并将事件误报率从仅EEG对应模型的2.7250 FP/h降至0.4833 FP/h，同时保持完美的事件敏感性。定向消融实验进一步表明，EEG预训练和最优传输对齐有助于在保持事件敏感性的同时减少误报。

### [32] [Decoupled Prototype Matching with Vision Foundation Models for Few-Shot Industrial Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26404)
*Hari Prasanth S. M.,Nilusha Jayawickrama,Risto Ojala*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于视觉基础模型的少样本工业目标检测框架，通过构建类别原型和相似度匹配实现无需训练的目标检测，在三个工业数据集上AP提升6.9%，并支持仅用少量参考图像快速新增检测目标。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 工业场景中目标种类频繁变更，标注大规模数据集成本高昂且难以维护，现有方法难以在少量标注样本下实现有效检测。

Method: 利用视觉基础模型从少量参考样本中提取特征构建类别原型；推理时使用分割模型生成候选目标区域，提取嵌入特征并与类别原型进行相似度匹配完成检测。

Result: 在Benchmark for 6D Object Pose Estimation的三个工业数据集上，按照官方2D目标检测评估协议，相比现有最优的无训练检测方法，AP提升6.9%。

Conclusion: 该方法无需CAD模型或大规模标注数据集，仅需少量参考图像即可新增检测目标，具有竞争性检测性能，非常适合实际工业应用场景。

Original Abstract: Industrial object detection systems typically rely on large annotated datasets, which are expensive to collect and challenging to maintain in industrial scenarios where the inventory of objects changes frequently. This work addresses the challenge of few-shot object detection in such industrial scenarios, where only a limited number of labeled samples are available for newly introduced objects. We present a detection framework that leverages vision foundation models to recognize objects with minimal supervision. The method constructs class prototypes from a small set of reference samples by extracting feature representations. For a given query scene during inference, object regions are generated using a segmentation model, and feature embeddings are extracted and matched with class prototypes using similarity matching. We evaluate the detection method on three established industrial datasets from the Benchmark for 6D Object Pose Estimation benchmark following the official 2D object detection evaluation protocol. We demonstrate competitive detection performance, improving AP by 6.9% compared to the state-of-the-art training-free detection methods. Furthermore, the presented method is able to onboard new objects using only a few reference images, without requiring any CAD models or large annotated datasets. These properties make the approach well-suited for real-world industrial applications.

### [33] [Sparsity as a Key: Unlocking New Insights from Latent Structures for Out-of-Distribution Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26409)
*Ahyoung Oh,Wonseok Shin,Songkuk Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次将稀疏自编码器（SAE）应用于Vision Transformer（ViT）的[CLS]令牌，用于分布外（OOD）检测。通过Top-k SAE将密集[CLS]特征解耦为结构化潜在空间，发现分布内（ID）数据呈现一致的类特异性激活模式（Class Activation Profiles, CAPs），而OOD样本会破坏该结构。基于此提出核心能量轮廓散度评分函数，在FPR95指标上表现优异。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有OOD检测方法依赖于纠缠的特征表示，性能受限。SAE在LLM解释中取得了成功，但在Vision Transformer分析中尚未被充分探索，尤其是利用SAE对ViT的[CLS]令牌进行解耦分析以提升OOD检测能力。

Method: 提出基于Top-k稀疏自编码器的框架，对ViT的[CLS]令牌密集特征进行解耦，提取为结构化潜在空间；定义类激活配置文件（CAPs）描述ID数据的类特异性激活模式；设计核心能量轮廓散度评分函数，通过量化实际激活模式与理想CAP的偏差来检测OOD样本。

Result: 在多个基准测试上，该方法在FPR95指标上取得强结果（对安全关键应用至关重要），同时AUROC指标也达到竞争性水平。

Conclusion: SAE揭示的稀疏解耦特征可以作为视觉模型中鲁棒OOD检测的强大且可解释的工具。

Original Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have demonstrated significant success in interpreting Large Language Models (LLMs) by decomposing dense representations into sparse, semantic components. However, their potential for analyzing Vision Transformers (ViTs) remains largely under-explored. In this work, we present the first application of SAEs to the ViT [CLS] token for out-of-distribution (OOD) detection, addressing the limitation of existing methods that rely on entangled feature representations. We propose a novel framework utilizing a Top-k SAE to disentangle the dense [CLS] features into a structured latent space. Through this analysis, we reveal that in-distribution (ID) data exhibits consistent, class-specific activation patterns, which we formalize as Class Activation Profiles (CAPs). Our study uncovers a key structural invariant: while ID samples preserve a stable pattern within CAPs, OOD samples systematically disrupt this structure. Leveraging this insight, we introduce a scoring function based on the divergence of core energy profiles to quantify the deviation from ideal activation profiles. Our method achieves strong results on the FPR95 metric, critical for safety-sensitive applications across multiple benchmarks, while also achieving competitive AUROC. Overall, our findings demonstrate that the sparse, disentangled features revealed by SAEs can serve as a powerful, interpretable tool for robust OOD detection in vision models.

中文摘要翻译: 稀疏自编码器（SAE）在通过将密集表示分解为稀疏语义组件来解读大型语言模型（LLM）方面取得了显著成功。然而，其在分析Vision Transformer（ViT）方面的潜力仍未被充分探索。本文首次将SAE应用于ViT的[CLS]令牌进行分布外（OOD）检测，解决了现有方法依赖于纠缠特征表示的局限性。我们提出了一种利用Top-k SAE将密集[CLS]特征解耦为结构化潜在空间的新框架。通过这一分析，我们发现分布内（ID）数据呈现出一致的、类别特异性的激活模式，我们将其形式化为类激活配置文件（CAPs）。我们的研究揭示了一个关键的结构不变性：ID样本在CAPs内保持稳定的模式，而OOD样本则会系统地破坏这一结构。基于这一发现，我们引入了一种基于核心能量轮廓散度的评分函数，用于量化与理想激活配置文件的偏差。我们的方法在多个基准测试上的FPR95指标上取得了强结果（该指标对安全敏感应用至关重要），同时AUROC也达到了竞争性水平。总体而言，我们的发现表明，SAE揭示的稀疏解耦特征可以作为视觉模型中鲁棒OOD检测的一种强大且可解释的工具。
