### [34] [Delineating Knowledge Boundaries for Honest Large Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26419)
*Junru Song,Yimeng Hu,Yijing Chen,Huining Li,Qian Li,Lizhen Cui,Yuntao Du*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种系统框架，通过构建模型特定的“Visual-Idk”数据集并采用监督微调与偏好感知优化，增强大型视觉语言模型在面对超出其参数知识的未知问题时的拒绝能力，从而减少事实幻觉并提升可信度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 大型视觉语言模型在多模态任务中表现优异，但容易产生事实性幻觉，尤其在长尾或专业领域；此外，现有模型在面对超出其参数知识的问题时缺乏有效的拒绝能力。

Method: 首先通过多样本一致性探测构建模型特定的“Visual-Idk”数据集，以区分已知与未知事实；然后采用监督微调（SFT）结合偏好感知优化（如DPO、ORPO）对模型进行对齐，从而界定其知识边界。

Result: 在Visual-Idk数据集上，Truthful Rate从57.9%提升至67.3%；内部探针实验表明模型真正识别了知识边界而非仅记忆拒绝模式；该方法还能泛化至分布外的医学和感知领域。

Conclusion: 该框架能够有效增强VLM的拒绝能力，减少幻觉，提升模型在未知问题上的可信度与审慎性，为构建更值得信赖的视觉助手提供了可行路径。

Original Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved remarkable multimodal performance yet remain prone to factual hallucinations, particularly in long-tail or specialized domains. Moreover, current models exhibit a weak capacity to refuse queries that exceed their parametric knowledge. In this paper, we propose a systematic framework to enhance the refusal capability of VLMs when facing such unknown questions. We first curate a model-specific "Visual-Idk" (Visual-I don't know) dataset, leveraging multi-sample consistency probing to distinguish between known and unknown facts. We then align the model using supervised fine-tuning followed by preference-aware optimization (e.g., DPO, ORPO) to effectively delineate its knowledge boundaries. Results on the Visual-Idk dataset show our method improves the Truthful Rate from 57.9\% to 67.3\%. Additionally, internal probing also demonstrates that the model genuinely recognizes its boundaries instead of just memorizing refusal patterns. Our framework further generalizes to out-of-distribution medical and perceptual domains, providing a robust path toward more trustworthy and prudent visual assistants.

中文摘要翻译: 大型视觉语言模型（VLM）在多模态任务中取得了显著性能，但仍容易产生事实性幻觉，尤其在长尾或专业领域。此外，当前模型在面对超出其参数知识的问题时，表现出较弱的拒绝能力。本文提出一个系统框架，用于增强VLM在面对此类未知问题时的拒绝能力。我们首先通过多样本一致性探测，构建了一个模型特定的“Visual-Idk”（视觉—我不知道）数据集，以区分已知与未知事实。随后，通过监督微调结合偏好感知优化（如DPO、ORPO）对模型进行对齐，有效界定其知识边界。在Visual-Idk数据集上的实验结果显示，我们的方法将Truthful Rate从57.9%提升至67.3%。此外，内部探针实验也表明，模型真正识别了自身知识边界，而不仅仅是记忆了拒绝模式。该框架还能泛化至分布外的医学和感知领域，为构建更可信、更审慎的视觉助手提供了一条稳健路径。

</details>


### [35] [Attribution-Guided Multimodal Deepfake Detection via Cross-Modal Forensic Fingerprints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26453)
*Wasim Ahmad,Wei Zhang,Xuerui Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AMDD框架，通过生成器归因引导的多模态深度伪造检测，在FakeAVCeleb上达到99.7%平衡准确率，并揭示了跨数据集泛化中的挑战。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有二分类检测方法容易学习数据集特定伪影而非真实生成痕迹，缺乏归因能力的检测器可能学到错误信号。相比二分类，归因引导学习能对共享嵌入空间施加更强的几何约束，迫使模型编码生成器特定的取证内容。

Method: 提出AMDD框架，联合学习检测和归因操作。将生成器归因作为结构化正则化约束表示几何；引入跨模态取证指纹一致性（CMFFC）损失，强制视觉和音频流中生成器诱导伪影的对齐。视觉编码器使用ResNet50+时间注意力，音频编码器使用预训练ResNet18处理梅尔频谱图。

Result: 在FakeAVCeleb上达到99.7%平衡准确率、99.8% AUC和95.9%归因准确率。跨数据集评估（DeepfakeTIMIT, DFDM, LAV-DF）证实真实视频检测鲁棒泛化，但未见生成器上的伪造检测仍是开放挑战。

Conclusion: 归因引导的多模态学习能有效提升深度伪造检测性能，跨数据集泛化中真实视频检测表现稳健，但应对未知生成器的伪造检测仍需进一步研究。

Original Abstract: Audio-visual deepfakes have reached a level of realism that makes perceptual detection unreliable, threatening media integrity and biometric security. While multimodal detection has shown promise, most approaches are binary classification tasks that often latch onto dataset-specific artifacts rather than genuine generative traces. We argue that a detector incapable of identifying how a video was forged is likely learning the wrong signal. Unlike binary detection, attribution-guided learning imposes a stronger geometric constraint on the shared embedding space, forcing the model to encode generator-specific forensic content rather than shortcuts.
  We propose the Attribution-Guided Multimodal Deepfake Detection (AMDD) framework, which jointly learns to detect and attribute manipulation. AMDD treats generator attribution as a structured regularization that constrains representation geometry toward forensically meaningful features. We introduce a Cross-Modal Forensic Fingerprint Consistency (CMFFC) loss to enforce alignment between generator-induced artifacts in visual and audio streams. This exploits the fact that coherent manipulation leaves correlated traces across modalities, grounded in the physical coupling between speech and facial articulation that synthetic pipelines routinely disrupt.
  Architecturally, we pair a ResNet50 with temporal attention for visual encoding against a pretrained ResNet18 for mel spectrograms, closing the encoder capacity gap found in prior models. On FakeAVCeleb, AMDD achieves 99.7% balanced accuracy and 99.8% AUC with 95.9% attribution accuracy. Cross-dataset evaluation on DeepfakeTIMIT, DFDM, and LAV-DF confirms that real video detection generalizes robustly, while fake detection on unseen generators remains an open challenge that we analyze in depth.

中文摘要翻译: 音视频深度伪造已达到使感知检测不可靠的真实感水平，威胁着媒体完整性和生物特征安全。虽然多模态检测已展现出前景，但大多数方法属于二分类任务，往往捕捉数据集特定的伪影而非真正的生成痕迹。我们认为，无法识别视频是如何伪造的检测器很可能在学习错误的信号。与二分类检测不同，归因引导学习对共享嵌入空间施加了更强的几何约束，迫使模型编码生成器特定的取证内容而非捷径。我们提出了归因引导的多模态深度伪造检测（AMDD）框架，该框架联合学习检测和归因操作。AMDD将生成器归因视为一种结构化正则化，约束表示几何朝向取证有意义的特征。我们引入跨模态取证指纹一致性（CMFFC）损失，强制视觉和音频流中生成器诱导伪影的对齐。这利用了以下事实：一致的操控会在跨模态间留下相关痕迹，其基础在于语音与面部关节运动之间的物理耦合——而合成管线通常会破坏这种耦合。在架构上，我们将带有时间注意力的ResNet50用于视觉编码，与用于梅尔频谱图的预训练ResNet18配对，弥补了先前模型中编码器容量的差距。在FakeAVCeleb上，AMDD实现了99.7%的平衡准确率、99.8%的AUC以及95.9%的归因准确率。在DeepfakeTIMIT、DFDM和LAV-DF上的跨数据集评估证实，真实视频检测能够鲁棒地泛化，而未见生成器上的伪造检测仍是一个开放性挑战——我们对此进行了深入分析。

</details>


### [36] [Last-Layer-Centric Feature Recombination: Unleashing 3D Geometric Knowledge in DINOv3 for Monocular Depth Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26454)
*Gongshu Wang,Zhirui Wang,Kan Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统地分析了DINOv3中3D信息的分布规律，发现其呈非均匀分布——深层编码更强的几何信息。据此提出最后一层特征重组（LFR）模块，以最后一层为几何锚点，按最小相似度准则自适应选择互补的中间层特征进行融合，在单目深度估计任务上取得最优性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有工作通常以均匀间隔采样固定数量的中间Transformer层来构建多尺度特征，这一做法隐含假设几何信息在各层均匀分布，可能未能充分利用视觉基础模型中编码的3D结构信息。本文旨在揭示真实分布规律并据此设计更高效的特征利用策略。

Method: 首先对DINOv3进行逐层系统分析，揭示3D信息呈非均匀分布。然后提出最后一层特征重组（LFR）模块：将最后一层视为几何锚点，按最小相似度准则自适应选择互补的中间层，通过紧凑线性适配器将所选特征与最后一层特征融合。

Result: 实验表明LFR模块持续提升了单目深度估计的精度，取得了当前最优性能。分析揭示了视觉基础模型中几何知识的组织结构，为密集3D任务中释放模型潜力提供了高效策略。

Conclusion: 视觉基础模型中的3D几何信息呈非均匀分布，深层具有更强的深度可预测性和样本间几何变化捕捉能力。LFR模块能有效利用这一规律提升密集3D预测任务的性能。

Original Abstract: Monocular depth estimation (MDE) is a fundamental yet inherently ill-posed task. Recent vision foundation models (VFMs), particularly DINO-based transformers, have significantly improved accuracy and generalization for dense prediction. Prior works generally follow a unified paradigm: sampling a fixed set of intermediate transformer layers at uniform intervals to build multi-scale features. This common practice implicitly assumes that geometric information is uniformly distributed across layers, which may underutilize the structural 3D cues encoded in VFMs. In this study, we present a systematic layer-wise analysis of DINOv3, revealing that 3D information is distributed non-uniformly: deeper layers exhibit stronger depth predictability and better capture inter-sample geometric variation. Motivated by this, we introduce a Last-Layer-Centric Feature Recombination (LFR) module to enhance geometric expressiveness. LFR treats the final layer as a geometric anchor and adaptively selects complementary intermediate layers according to a minimal-similarity criterion. Selected features are fused with the last-layer representation via compact linear adapters.Extensive experiments show that LFR module consistently improves MDE accuracy and achieves state-of-the-art performance. Our analysis sheds light on how geometric knowledge is organized within VFMs and offers an efficient strategy for unlocking their potential in dense 3D tasks.

中文摘要翻译: 单目深度估计（MDE）是一项基础但本质不适定的任务。最近的视觉基础模型（VFMs），特别是基于DINO的Transformer，显著提升了密集预测的准确性和泛化能力。以往工作通常遵循统一范式：以均匀间隔采样固定数量的中间Transformer层来构建多尺度特征。这一常见做法隐含假设几何信息在各层中均匀分布，可能未能充分利用VFM中编码的结构性3D线索。在本研究中，我们对DINOv3进行了系统的逐层分析，揭示出3D信息呈非均匀分布：更深层具有更强的深度可预测性，并能更好地捕捉样本间的几何变化。受此启发，我们引入了一个最后一层特征重组（LFR）模块来增强几何表达能力。LFR将最后一层视为几何锚点，并根据最小相似度准则自适应地选择互补的中间层。所选特征通过紧凑的线性适配器与最后一层表示进行融合。大量实验表明，LFR模块持续提升了MDE精度并取得了最先进的性能。我们的分析揭示了几何知识在VFM中的组织方式，并为在密集3D任务中释放其潜力提供了一种高效策略。

### [37] [A Multistage Extraction Pipeline for Long Scanned Financial Documents: An Empirical Study in Industrial KYC Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26462)
*Yuxuan Han,Yuanxing Zhang,Yushuo Wang,Yichao Jin,Kenneth Zhu Ke,Jingyuan Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种多阶段提取框架，通过分离页面定位与多模态推理，在长篇幅、多语种、扫描版金融文档的结构化信息提取中，比直接端到端的PDF到VLM方法提升了高达31.9个百分点的字段级准确率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 工业KYC和合规流程中需要从长篇幅、多语种、非机器可读的扫描金融文档中提取结构化信息，现有视觉语言模型直接端到端应用于完整财务报告时，在真实场景下提取结果不可靠。

Method: 提出一个多阶段提取框架，包含图像预处理、多语种OCR、混合页面级检索和紧凑型VLM结构化提取四个阶段，将页面定位与多模态推理分离。

Result: 在120份生产级KYC文档（约3000页多语种扫描页）上评估，所提流水线在所有OCR-VLM组合上均优于直接PDF-to-VLM基线，字段级准确率最高提升31.9个百分点；最佳配置PaddleOCR+MiniCPM2.6达到87.27%准确率；消融实验表明页面级检索是性能提升的主导因素。

Conclusion: 多阶段分离架构（页面定位与多模态推理分离）能够显著提升长篇幅多语种扫描金融文档的结构化信息提取准确性，其中页面级检索是最关键的组件。

Original Abstract: Structured information extraction from long, multilingual scanned financial documents is a core requirement in industrial KYC and compliance workflows. Although recent vision-language models achieve strong benchmark performance, directly applying them end to end to full financial reports often leads to unreliable extraction under real world conditions. We present a multistage extraction framework that integrates image preprocessing, multilingual OCR, hybrid page-level retrieval, and compact VLM-based structured extraction. The design separates page localization from multimodal reasoning, enabling more accurate extraction from complex multipage documents. We evaluated the framework on 120 production KYC documents comprising about 3000 multilingual scanned pages. Across multiple OCR-VLM combinations, the proposed pipeline consistently outperforms direct PDF-to-VLM baselines, improving field-level accuracy by up to 31.9 percentage points. The best configuration, PaddleOCR with MiniCPM2.6, achieves 87.27 percent accuracy. Ablation studies show that page-level retrieval is the dominant factor in performance improvements, particularly for complex financial statements and non-English documents.

### [38] [Cross-Domain Transfer of Hyperspectral Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26478)
*Nick Theisen,Peer Neubert*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出跨域迁移策略，将遥感领域训练的高光谱基础模型直接用于近感高光谱语义分割，无需跨模态桥接，在保留光谱信息的同时简化架构，实验表明该方法优于传统域内训练，缩小了与跨模态方法的差距。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 高光谱图像语义分割通常依赖域内训练，但数据有限限制了模型性能。现有方法通过跨模态技术桥接RGB与高光谱以利用视觉基础模型，但要么丢弃了光谱信息，要么增加了架构复杂性。因此，作者提出跨域迁移作为替代方案。

Method: 提出跨域迁移策略，直接复用遥感领域预训练的高光谱基础模型用于近感应用，无需跨模态桥接，保留完整光谱信息且保持架构简洁。在HS3-Bench基准上系统评估了域内同模态训练、跨模态迁移和跨域迁移三种策略。

Conclusion: 跨域迁移是一种有效的高光谱语义分割方案，能够在不同应用中推进更有效的分割性能，尤其适用于数据有限的场景。

Original Abstract: Hyperspectral imaging (HSI) semantic segmentation typically relies on in-domain training, but limited data availability often restricts model performance in real-world applications. Current approaches to leverage foundation models in proximal sensing use cross-modality techniques, bridging RGB and HSI to exploit vision foundation models. However, these methods either discard spectral information or introduce architectural complexity. We propose cross-domain transfer as an alternative, reusing HSI foundation models - originally trained in remote sensing - for proximal sensing applications. By eliminating the need to bridge modality gaps, our approach preserves spectral information while maintaining a simple architecture. Using the HS3-Bench benchmark, we systematically evaluate and compare conventional in-domain, in-modality training, cross-modality transfer and cross-domain transfer strategies. Our results demonstrate that cross-domain transfer achieves large performance improvements over in-domain, in-modality training, reduces the performance gap to cross-modality approaches and maintains strong performance in limited data settings. 中文摘要翻译: 高光谱成像（HSI）语义分割通常依赖于域内训练，但在实际应用中，有限的数据可获取性常常限制了模型性能。当前在近感中利用基础模型的方法采用跨模态技术，桥接RGB与HSI以利用视觉基础模型。然而，这些方法要么丢弃了光谱信息，要么引入了架构复杂性。我们提出跨域迁移作为替代方案，直接复用最初在遥感领域训练的高光谱基础模型，用于近感应用。通过消除模态桥接的需求，我们的方法在保持简单架构的同时保留了光谱信息。利用HS3-Bench基准，我们系统评估并比较了传统的域内同模态训练、跨模态迁移和跨域迁移策略。实验结果表明，跨域迁移相比域内同模态训练取得了大幅性能提升，缩小了与跨模态方法的性能差距，并在数据有限的场景中保持较强性能。因此，本工作推动了高光谱语义分割在多样化应用中的更有效发展。

### [39] [Delta Score Matters! Spatial Adaptive Multi Guidance in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26503)
*Haosen Li,Wenshuo Chen,Lei Wang,Shaofeng Liang,Bowen Tian,Soning Lai,Yutao Yue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需训练、零额外计算成本的采样算法SAMG，通过几何视角分析Tweedie公式，揭示CFG本质是切向线性外推，并据此设计自适应空间引导策略，在图像和视频生成中解决了细节-伪影困境，实现了更好的语义对齐、结构完整性和时间平滑性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准无分类器引导（CFG）使用全局统一标量，导致"细节-伪影困境"：低引导尺度无法注入复杂语义，高引导尺度则引发结构退化、颜色过饱和及视频时间不一致性。论文旨在从微分几何根源揭示这一缺陷并加以解决。

Method: 通过微分几何分析Tweedie公式，发现CFG本质是切向线性外推，但由于数据流形高度弯曲，均匀线性步长会引入严重的正交偏差。据此推导空间自适应引导的理论上界，提出SAMG算法：动态计算逐点条件引导能量，在高能量边界区域使用保守的最小尺度以保留精细微纹理，在低能量区域使用激进的最大尺度以最大化语义注入。

Result: 在多种图像架构（SD 1.5、SDXL、SD3.5 Medium）和视频架构（CogVideoX、ModelScope）上的大量实验表明，SAMG有效解决了细节-伪影困境，在无任何计算开销的情况下实现了更优的语义对齐、结构完整性和时间平滑性。

Conclusion: SAMG作为一种无需训练、零成本的采样算法，通过几何驱动的自适应空间引导，从根本上解决了CFG的细节-伪影困境，在图像和视频生成任务中均取得了显著提升。

Original Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in synthesizing complex static and temporal visuals, a breakthrough largely driven by Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG). However, despite its pivotal role in aligning generated content with textual prompts, standard CFG relies on a globally uniform scalar. This homogeneous amplification traps models in a well-documented "detail-artifact dilemma": low guidance scales fail to inject intricate semantics, while high scales inevitably cause structural degradation, color over-saturation, and temporal inconsistencies in videos. In this paper, we expose the physical root of this flaw through the lens of differential geometry. By analyzing Tweedie's Formula, we reveal that CFG intrinsically performs a tangential linear extrapolation. Because the natural data manifold is highly curved, this uniform linear step introduces a severe orthogonal deviation. To keep the generation trajectory safely bounded, we formulate a theoretical upper bound for spatial and adaptive guidance. Based on these geometric insights, we propose Spatial Adaptive Multi Guidance (SAMG), a training-free and virtually zero-cost sampling algorithm. SAMG dynamically computes point-wise conditional guidance energy, applying a conservative minimum scale to high-energy boundary regions to preserve delicate micro-textures, while deploying an aggressive maximum scale in low-energy regions to maximize semantic injection. Extensive experiments across diverse image (SD 1.5, SDXL, SD3.5 Medium) and video (CogVideoX, ModelScope) architectures demonstrate that SAMG effectively resolves the detail-artifact dilemma, achieving superior semantic alignment, structural integrity, and temporal smoothness without any computational overhead.

中文摘要翻译: 扩散模型在合成复杂的静态和动态视觉内容方面取得了显著成功，这一突破很大程度上得益于无分类器引导（CFG）。然而，尽管CFG在将生成内容与文本提示对齐方面发挥了关键作用，标准CFG依赖于全局统一的标量。这种同质化的放大方式将模型困在了众所周知的"细节-伪影困境"中：低引导尺度无法注入精细语义，而高引导尺度则不可避免地导致结构退化、颜色过饱和以及视频中的时间不一致性。本文通过微分几何的视角揭示了这一缺陷的物理根源。通过分析Tweedie公式，我们发现CFG本质上执行的是切向线性外推。由于自然数据流形高度弯曲，这种均匀的线性步长会引入严重的正交偏差。为将生成轨迹安全地约束在边界内，我们推导了空间自适应引导的理论上界。基于这些几何洞见，我们提出了空间自适应多引导（SAMG），一种无需训练且几乎零成本的采样算法。SAMG动态计算逐点条件引导能量，在高能量边界区域应用保守的最小尺度以保留精细微纹理，同时在低能量区域部署激进的最大尺度以最大化语义注入。跨多种图像架构（SD 1.5、SDXL、SD3.5 Medium）和视频架构（CogVideoX、ModelScope）的大量实验表明，SAMG有效解决了细节-伪影困境，在无任何计算开销的情况下实现了更优的语义对齐、结构完整性和时间平滑性。

</details>


### [40] [MTCurv: Deep learning for direct microtubule curvature mapping in noisy fluorescence microscopy images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26517)
*Achraf Ait Laydi,Sidi Mohamed Sid'El Moctar,Yousef El Mourabit,Hélène Bouvrais*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出MTCurv，一种基于深度学习的无分割微管曲率回归框架，直接从噪声显微图像中估计曲率图，通过合成数据训练、注意力残差U-Net和梯度一致性损失函数，实现了鲁棒的曲率预测，并发现Spearman相关是更可靠的评估指标。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有微管曲率提取方法依赖图像分割及前后处理，对分割错误高度敏感，在噪声、低对比度、部分可见等不利成像条件下容易失败，因此需要一种不依赖分割的、直接从噪声图像回归曲率的方法。

Method: 提出MTCurv框架：1) 构建带有逐像素曲率标注的合成数据集；2) 将曲率估计重新定义为回归问题；3) 采用基于注意力机制的残差U-Net架构；4) 设计梯度感知损失函数，结合均方误差与梯度一致性项，减少幻觉并增强空间一致性。

Result: 在两个难度递增的数据集上，MTCurv能准确恢复局部微管曲率，即使存在背景荧光干扰；消融实验验证了残差编码和注意力解码的贡献；指标评估发现感知指标和盲指标不适用于曲率估计，基于相关的指标（特别是Spearman相关）更可靠。

Conclusion: 本文为丝状结构曲率分析提供了实用工具，并为生物医学成像中的几何感知回归提供了方法论见解。

Original Abstract: Accurate quantification of the geometry of curvilinear biological structures is essential for understanding cellular mechanics and disease-related morphological alterations. Microtubule curvature is a key descriptor of filament rigidity and mechanical perturbations. However, reliable curvature extraction from fluorescence microscopy images remains challenging due to noise, low contrast, and partial filament visibility. Existing approaches rely on segmentation pipelines with pre or post-processing, which are highly sensitive to segmentation errors and often fail under adverse imaging conditions. In this work, we propose MTCurv, a deep learning framework for direct, segmenta-tion-free regression of microtubule curvature maps from noisy microscopy images. Leveraging a synthetic dataset with pixel-wise curvature annotations, we reformulated curvature estimation as a regression problem and adapted an attention-based residual U-Net. To reduce hallucinations and enforce spatial coherence, we introduced a gradient-aware loss combining Mean Squared Error with a gradient consistency term. Beyond model and loss design, we evaluated commonly used regression and image quality metrics, revealing that many perceptual and blind metrics are poorly suited for curvature estimation. Correlation-based metrics, particularly Spearman correlation, emerged as more reliable indicators of curvature prediction quality. Experiments on two datasets of increasing difficulty demonstrated that MTCurv accurately recovers local microtubule curvatures, even in the presence of background fluorescence. Ablation studies highlighted the contribution of both residual encoding and attention-based decoding. Overall, this work provides a practical tool for filament curvature analysis and methodological insights for geometry-aware regression in biomedical imaging. Datasets and code are made available.

中文摘要翻译: 准确量化曲线生物结构的几何特征对于理解细胞力学和疾病相关的形态变化至关重要。微管曲率是衡量丝状刚性和机械扰动的关键描述符。然而，由于噪声、低对比度和丝状部分可见性差，从荧光显微图像中可靠地提取曲率仍然具有挑战性。现有方法依赖带有预处理或后处理的分割流程，这些方法对分割错误高度敏感，且在不利成像条件下常常失败。本文提出MTCurv，一种深度学习框架，用于从噪声显微图像中直接进行无分割的微管曲率图回归。利用带有逐像素曲率标注的合成数据集，我们将曲率估计重新定义为回归问题，并适配了基于注意力机制的残差U-Net。为减少幻觉并增强空间一致性，我们引入了一种梯度感知损失函数，结合了均方误差与梯度一致性项。除模型和损失设计外，我们评估了常用的回归和图像质量指标，发现许多感知指标和盲指标不适合曲率估计。基于相关的指标，特别是Spearman相关，成为更可靠的曲率预测质量指标。在两个难度递增的数据集上的实验表明，MTCurv能准确恢复局部微管曲率，即使在存在背景荧光的情况下。消融研究突显了残差编码和注意力解码的贡献。总体而言，本文为丝状结构曲率分析提供了实用工具，并为生物医学成像中的几何感知回归提供了方法论见解。数据集和代码已公开提供。

</details>


### [41] [3D-LENS: A 3D Lifting-based Elevated Novel-view Synthesis method for Single-View Aerial-Ground Re-Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26520)
*William Grolleau,Astrid Sabourin,Guillaume Lapouge,Catherine Achard*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次提出单视角空地再识别（SV AG-ReID）任务，并设计了一个基于3D网格重建与新颖视角合成的统一框架3D-LENS，解决跨视角域差异与无目标域数据下的行人检索问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有AG-ReID方法依赖配对跨视角标注，但在真实场景（如野外搜救）中目标域数据不可得，只能依靠单一视角的地面参考图进行检索。现有方法无法在无目标域数据下泛化到未见视角。

Method: 提出3D-LENS框架，包含两部分：1）基于大规模3D网格重建的几何一致新颖视角合成模块，生成跨视角图像；2）鲁棒表示学习方案，缓解合成图像与真实图像之间的域偏差。

Result: 在SV AG-ReID场景下达到最先进性能。相比2D生成基线（几何不一致）和传统3D方法（限于类特定模板），本文方法在多样类别上实现了视角一致的合成，并能捕捉如携带物品等细粒度细节。

Conclusion: 3D-LENS有效解决了无目标域数据下的单视角空地再识别问题，通过几何一致的新颖视角合成与鲁棒表示学习，实现了跨视角泛化，在多个类别上均优于现有方法。

Original Abstract: Aerial-Ground Re-Identification (AG-ReID) is constrained by the viewpoint-domain gap, as drastic viewpoint disparities occlude or distort discriminative features, making cross-viewpoint image retrieval challenging. While existing methods rely on paired cross-view annotations, real-world deployments, such as wilderness search-and-rescue (SAR), often lack target-domain data, requiring retrieval from ground-level references alone. To our knowledge, we are the first to address this challenge by formalizing the Single-View AG-ReID (SV AG-ReID) setting, where models trained on a single real viewpoint must generalize to an unseen viewpoint. We propose 3D Lifting-based Elevated Novel-view Synthesis (3D-LENS), a unified framework combining geometrically-consistent novel view synthesis that leverages large-scale 3D mesh reconstruction, with a robust representation learning scheme to mitigate synthetic-to-real bias. Unlike 2D generative baselines that suffer from geometric inconsistencies or prior 3D methods that are restricted to class-specific templates, our approach ensures view-consistent synthesis across diverse categories without predefined templates that fail to capture fine-grained details, such as carried objects. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on SV AG-ReID scenarios. Code and data will be released at https://github.com/TurtleSmoke/3D-LENS.

中文摘要翻译: 空地再识别（AG-ReID）受限于视角域差异，由于剧烈的视角差异会遮挡或扭曲判别性特征，使得跨视角图像检索具有挑战性。现有方法依赖配对的跨视角标注，然而真实部署场景（如野外搜救）往往缺乏目标域数据，只能依靠地面参考图进行检索。据我们所知，我们是首个通过形式化单视角空地再识别（SV AG-ReID）设置来应对这一挑战的工作，该设置要求仅在单一真实视角上训练的模型泛化到未见过的视角。我们提出基于3D提升的高空新颖视角合成（3D-LENS），这是一个统一框架，结合了几何一致的新颖视角合成（利用大规模3D网格重建）与鲁棒的表示学习方案以缓解合成到真实的偏差。与受限于几何不一致的2D生成基线方法或局限于类特定模板的先前3D方法不同，我们的方法在无需预定义模板的情况下，确保了跨多样类别的一致视角合成，并能捕捉如携带物品等细粒度细节。大量实验表明，我们的方法在SV AG-ReID场景中达到了最先进性能。代码和数据将在https://github.com/TurtleSmoke/3D-LENS发布。

</details>


### [42] [DenseStep2M: A Scalable, Training-Free Pipeline for Dense Instructional Video Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26565)
*Mingji Ge,Qirui Chen,Zeqian Li,Weidi Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个无需训练的全自动管线，从非结构化教学视频中提取高质量程序性标注，构建了包含约10万视频和200万步骤的大规模数据集DenseStep2M，在密集视频描述、程序步骤定位和跨模态检索等下游任务上取得显著提升，并展现出良好的零样本泛化能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有长视频理解面临两大挑战：教学视频语料库（如HowTo100M）中存在嘈杂的ASR转录文本，以及旁白与视觉内容之间的时间对齐不一致，导致难以获得高质量的程序性标注用于模型训练。

Method: 提出一个自动化的、无需训练的管线：1) 将视频分割为连贯的镜头片段；2) 过滤对齐质量差的内容；3) 利用先进的多模态大语言模型（Qwen2.5-VL和DeepSeek-R1）生成结构化的、具有时间锚定的程序性步骤。

Result: 构建了DenseStep2M数据集（约10万视频、200万步骤）和DenseCaption100人工标注基准。实验表明：自动生成的步骤与人工标注高度一致；在该数据集上微调的模型在密集视频描述、程序步骤定位和跨模态检索任务上取得显著提升，并在自我中心、外部视角和混合视角领域均表现出鲁棒的零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: DenseStep2M数据集在促进多模态对齐和长期活动推理方面效果显著，为长视频理解提供了高质量的训练资源。

Original Abstract: Long-term video understanding requires interpreting complex temporal events and reasoning over procedural activities. While instructional video corpora, like HowTo100M, offer rich resources for model training, they present significant challenges, including noisy ASR transcripts and inconsistent temporal alignments between narration and visual content. In this work, we introduce an automated, training-free pipeline to extract high-quality procedural annotations from in-the-wild instructional videos. Our approach segments videos into coherent shots, filters poorly aligned content, and leverages state-of-the-art multimodal and large language models (Qwen2.5-VL and DeepSeek-R1) to generate structured, temporally grounded procedural steps.
  This pipeline yields DenseStep2M, a large-scale dataset comprising approximately 100K videos and 2M detailed instructional steps, designed to support comprehensive long-form video understanding. To rigorously evaluate our pipeline, we curate DenseCaption100, a benchmark of high-quality, human-written captions. Evaluations demonstrate strong alignment between our auto-generated steps and human annotations. Furthermore, we validate the utility of DenseStep2M across three core downstream tasks: dense video captioning, procedural step grounding, and cross-modal retrieval. Models fine-tuned on DenseStep2M achieve substantial gains in captioning quality and temporal localization, while exhibiting robust zero-shot generalization across egocentric, exocentric, and mixed-perspective domains. These results underscore the effectiveness of DenseStep2M in facilitating advanced multimodal alignment and long-term activity reasoning. Our dataset is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/mingjige/DenseStep2M.

中文摘要翻译: 长视频理解需要解读复杂的时序事件并对程序性活动进行推理。尽管教学视频语料库（如HowTo100M）为模型训练提供了丰富资源，但它们也带来了显著挑战，包括嘈杂的ASR转录文本以及旁白与视觉内容之间的时间对齐不一致。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种自动化的、无需训练的管线，用于从野外教学视频中提取高质量的程序性标注。我们的方法将视频分割为连贯的镜头片段，过滤对齐质量差的内容，并利用最先进的多模态大语言模型（Qwen2.5-VL和DeepSeek-R1）生成结构化的、具有时间锚定的程序性步骤。该管线生成了DenseStep2M——一个大规模数据集，包含约10万个视频和200万个详细教学步骤，旨在支持全面的长视频理解。为严格评估我们的管线，我们整理了DenseCaption100——一个高质量人工标注描述的基准。评估结果表明，我们的自动生成步骤与人工标注高度一致。此外，我们在三个核心下游任务上验证了DenseStep2M的实用性：密集视频描述、程序步骤定位和跨模态检索。在DenseStep2M上微调的模型在描述质量和时序定位方面取得了显著提升，同时在自我中心、外部视角和混合视角领域均表现出鲁棒的零样本泛化能力。这些结果凸显了DenseStep2M在促进高级多模态对齐和长期活动推理方面的有效性。我们的数据集可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/mingjige/DenseStep2M获取。

### [43] [AirZoo: A Unified Large-Scale Dataset for Grounding Aerial Geometric 3D Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26567)
*Xiaoya Cheng,Rouwan Wu,Xinyi Liu,Zeyu Cui,Yan Liu,Na Zhao,Yu Liu,Maojun Zhang,Shen Yan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AirZoo是一个面向航空几何3D视觉的大规模统一数据集与基准，通过可扩展的生成流程、全面的场景多样性和丰富的几何标注，为无人机感知相关模型提供强大的预训练引擎，显著提升了多项前沿模型的性能上限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有数据驱动3D视觉方法在地面或物体级视角上表现良好，但面对无人机(UAV)航拍场景中复杂的视角变换和多样环境条件时，缺乏大规模、高保真的训练数据。现有基准难以支撑航空几何3D视觉的发展，因此亟需一个统一的大规模数据集和基准来填补这一空白。

Method: AirZoo利用全球可获取的摄影测量3D网格，设计了可扩展的生成流程，支持自定义无人机飞行轨迹和可配置的天气/光照条件；覆盖22个国家378个区域，包含结构化城市和非结构化自然环境；为每帧提供同步的像素级度量深度和6自由度地理参考位姿标注；并设立了航空图像检索、跨视角匹配和多视角3D重建三个评估赛道。

Result: 在公开基准和新采集的真实世界基准上的大量实验表明，基于AirZoo微调可显著提升MegaLoc、RoMa、VGGT、Depth Anything 3等多项前沿模型的性能，建立了航空空间智能的新性能上限。

Conclusion: AirZoo作为一个大规模、多样化且标注丰富的航空几何3D视觉数据集与基准，能够作为强大的预训练引擎，有效推动航空空间智能的发展。

Original Abstract: Despite the rapid progress in data-driven 3D vision, aerial geometric 3D vision remains a formidable challenge due to the severe scarcity of large-scale, high-fidelity training data. Existing benchmarks, predominantly biased toward ground-level or object-centric views, do not account for complex viewpoint transformations and diverse environmental conditions in UAV-based sensing. To bridge this critical gap, we propose AirZoo, a unified large-scale dataset and benchmark for grounding aerial geometric 3D vision. AirZoo possesses three appealing properties: 1) Scalable Generation Pipeline: Leveraging freely available, world-scale photogrammetric 3D meshes, it renders vast outdoor environments with customizable UAV flight trajectories and configurable weather/illumination. 2) Comprehensive Scene Diversity: It provides the most extensive coverage of region types to date (spanning 378 regions across 22 countries), systematically encompassing both highly structured urban landscapes and complex unstructured natural environments. 3) Rich Geometric Annotations: Each frame provides synchronized, pixel-level metric depth and precise 6-DoF geo-referenced poses, essential for geometry-aware learning. Through three rigorous evaluation tracks -- aerial image retrieval, cross-view matching, and multi-view 3D reconstruction -- we demonstrate that AirZoo serves as a powerful pre-training engine. Extensive experiments on both public and newly collected real-world benchmarks reveal that fine-tuning on AirZoo yields substantial performance gains for SoTA models (e.g., MegaLoc, RoMa, VGGT, and Depth Anything 3), establishing a new performance upper bound for aerial spatial intelligence.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管数据驱动的3D视觉领域取得了快速进展，但由于大规模、高保真训练数据的严重匮乏，航空几何3D视觉仍然是一项艰巨的挑战。现有的基准主要偏向地面或物体级视角，未能考虑无人机感知中复杂的视角变换和多样的环境条件。为填补这一关键空白，我们提出了AirZoo——一个面向航空几何3D视觉的统一大规模数据集与基准。AirZoo具有三个吸引人的特性：1) 可扩展的生成流程：利用可自由获取的世界级摄影测量3D网格，渲染广阔的户外环境，支持可定制的无人机飞行轨迹和可配置的天气/光照条件。2) 全面的场景多样性：它提供了迄今为止最广泛的区域类型覆盖（涵盖22个国家的378个区域），系统性地包含了高度结构化的城市景观和复杂的非结构化自然环境。3) 丰富的几何标注：每帧提供同步的像素级度量深度和精确的6自由度地理参考位姿，这对几何感知学习至关重要。通过三个严格的评估赛道——航空图像检索、跨视角匹配和多视角3D重建——我们证明了AirZoo作为一个强大的预训练引擎。在公开基准和新采集的真实世界基准上的大量实验表明，基于AirZoo微调可为SoTA模型（例如MegaLoc、RoMa、VGGT和Depth Anything 3）带来显著的性能提升，为航空空间智能建立了新的性能上限。

### [44] [FunFace: Feature Utility and Norm Estimation for Face Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26598)
*Žiga Babnik,Fadi Boutros,Naser Damer,Deepak Kumar Jain,Peter Peer,Vitomir Štruc*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出FunFace损失函数，通过将生物识别效用（基于确定性比率估计）融入自适应间隔，在高质量基准上达到SOTA水平，并在低质量基准上实现超越。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有自适应间隔损失函数通过特征范数表达图像质量，虽与生物识别效用有一定相关性，但未能完全涵盖效用的所有方面。因此需要一种能更全面纳入生物识别效用的自适应间隔损失函数。

Method: 提出FunFace（Face Recognition Through Utility and Norm Estimation），受AdaFace启发，将基于Certainty Ratio估计的生物识别效用纳入自适应间隔损失函数中，用于训练人脸识别模型。

Result: FunFace在高质量样本基准测试上取得与最先进FR模型相当的结果，在低质量基准测试上超越现有SOTA方法。

Conclusion: FunFace通过整合生物识别效用到自适应间隔中，有效提升了人脸识别模型在低质量样本上的性能，同时保持了高质量样本上的竞争力。

Original Abstract: Face Recognition (FR) is used in a variety of application domains, from entertainment and banking to security and surveillance. Such applications rely on the FR model to be robust and perform well in a variety of settings. To achieve this, state-of-the-art FR models typically use expressive adaptive margin loss functions, which tie the feature norm to concepts related to sample quality, such as recognizability and perceptual image quality. Recently, through the development of Face Image Quality Assessment (FIQA) techniques, biometric utility has become the preferred measure of face-image quality and has been shown to be a better predictor of the usefulness of samples for face recognition compared to more human-centric aspects, such as resolution, blur, and lighting, tied to general image quality. While image quality expressed through feature norms exhibits a certain level of correlation with biometric utility, it does not fully encapsulate all aspects of utility. To address this point, we propose a new adaptive margin loss, FunFace (Face Recognition Through Utility and Norm Estimation), which incorporates biometric utility, estimated by the Certainty Ratio, into the adaptive margin, taking inspiration from AdaFace. We show that FunFace (when used to train a face recognition model) achieves competitive results to other state-of-the-art FR models on benchmarks containing high-quality samples, while surpassing them on low quality benchmarks.

中文摘要翻译: 人脸识别（FR）被广泛应用于从娱乐、银行到安防监控等多个领域。这些应用要求FR模型在各种场景下都具备鲁棒性和良好性能。为此，最先进的FR模型通常使用具有表现力的自适应间隔损失函数，将特征范数与样本质量相关概念（如可识别性和感知图像质量）相关联。近年来，随着人脸图像质量评估（FIQA）技术的发展，生物识别效用已成为人脸图像质量的首选衡量标准，并且已被证明相比更以人为中心的质量方面（如分辨率、模糊度和光照等通用图像质量指标），能更好地预测样本对人脸识别的有用性。虽然通过特征范数表达的图像质量与生物识别效用存在一定相关性，但并未完全涵盖效用的所有方面。针对这一问题，我们提出了一种新的自适应间隔损失函数FunFace（基于效用和范数估计的人脸识别），该函数受AdaFace启发，将基于确定性比率（Certainty Ratio）估计的生物识别效用纳入自适应间隔。我们证明，FunFace（用于训练人脸识别模型时）在包含高质量样本的基准测试中能取得与最先进FR模型相当的结果，同时在低质量基准测试中超越它们。

</details>


### [45] [State Beyond Appearance: Diagnosing and Improving State Consistency in Dial-Based Measurement Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26614)
*Yuanze Hu,Gen Li,Yuqin Lan,Qingchen Yu,Zhichao Yang,Junwei Jing,Zhaoxin Fan,Xiaotie Deng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 当前多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在表盘测量读数任务上表现脆弱，易受视角和光照变化干扰，忽视了状态的内在几何结构。本文提出TriSCA三阶段状态一致性对齐框架，通过距离感知表示对齐、元数据监督和状态目标对齐，显著提升了表盘读数的准确性和鲁棒性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有MLLMs在通用多模态任务上表现优异，但在表盘测量读数任务上精度不足，且对视角和光照变化极其敏感，即便表盘内部状态未变，性能也会大幅下降。探针分析表明，模型忽略了表盘测量任务固有的状态几何结构，转而依赖浅层外观线索，亟需针对性的方法来解决这一问题。

Method: 提出TriSCA（三阶段状态一致性对齐框架），包括：（1）状态距离感知的表示对齐；（2）基于元数据的观测到状态监督；（3）状态感知的目标对齐。通过三个层面的对齐策略，使模型学习表盘状态的固有几何结构而非浅层外观特征。

Result: 在受控时钟和仪表基准测试以及外部真实世界基准上的大量消融实验和评估实验表明，该方法有效提升了表盘读数的准确性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 现有MLLMs在表盘测量任务中因忽略状态几何结构而表现脆弱，本文提出的TriSCA框架通过三阶段状态一致性对齐，有效解决了这一问题。

Original Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved impressive progress on general multimodal tasks, yet they remain brittle on dial-based measurement reading. In this paper, we study this problem through controlled benchmarks and feature-space probing, and show that current MLLMs not only achieve unsatisfactory accuracy on dial-based readout, but also suffer sharp performance drops under viewpoint and illumination changes even when the underlying dial state remains fixed. Our probing analysis further reveals that same-state samples under appearance variation are not consistently clustered, while neighboring states fail to preserve the local structure implied by continuous dial values. These findings suggest that existing MLLMs largely ignore the intrinsic state geometry of dial measurement tasks and instead rely on superficial appearance cues. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose TriSCA, a tri-level state-consistent alignment framework for dial-based measurement reading. Specifically, TriSCA consists of state-distance-aware representation alignment, metadata-grounded observation-to-state supervision, and state-aware objective alignment. Extensive ablation studies and evaluation experiments on controlled clock and gauge benchmarks, together with evaluation on an external real-world benchmark, demonstrate the effectiveness of our method.

中文摘要翻译: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在通用多模态任务上取得了令人瞩目的进展，但在表盘测量读数任务上仍然表现脆弱。本文通过受控基准测试和特征空间探针分析研究了这一问题，结果表明，当前的MLLMs不仅在表盘读数上准确率不尽人意，而且在视角和光照变化下性能急剧下降，即使底层表盘状态保持不变。我们的探针分析进一步揭示，在外观变化条件下，相同状态的样本未能形成一致的聚类，而相邻状态也无法保持连续刻度值所隐含的局部结构。这些发现表明，现有MLLMs在很大程度上忽略了表盘测量任务的内在状态几何结构，转而依赖浅层外观线索。基于这一诊断，我们提出了TriSCA，一种面向表盘测量读数的三阶段状态一致性对齐框架。具体而言，TriSCA包括状态距离感知的表示对齐、基于元数据的观测到状态监督以及状态感知的目标对齐。在受控时钟和仪表基准测试上的大量消融研究和评估实验，以及在外部真实世界基准上的评估，均证明了我们方法的有效性。

### [46] [SnapPose3D: Diffusion-Based Single-Frame 2D-to-3D Lifting of Human Poses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26620)
*Alessandro Simoni,Riccardo Catalini,Davide Di Nucci,Guido Borghi,Davide Davoli,Lorenzo Garattoni,Gianpiero Francesca,Yuki Kawana,Roberto Vezzani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SnapPose3D，一种基于扩散模型的单帧2D-to-3D人体姿态提升框架，通过确定性去噪训练和推理时概率采样生成多个假设并聚合得到准确姿态，在多个基准上达到SOTA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有2D-to-3D姿态提升方法存在深度模糊性和关节不确定性问题，即同一2D位置可映射到多个3D位置导致多种可能姿态；多数方法依赖时序序列处理，增加了计算成本、数据采集复杂度和实时应用难度。

Method: 提出SnapPose3D框架：训练阶段以视觉上下文和2D姿态特征为条件，确定性去噪3D姿态；推理阶段通过从标准高斯分布随机采样生成多个姿态假设，并聚合这些假设得到最终准确姿态。采用单帧输入而非时序序列。

Result: 在多个3D人体姿态估计公开基准上达到SOTA结果，证明该方法能有效生成并聚合准确假设。

Conclusion: 基于扩散模型的单帧输入多假设生成与聚合策略能有效解决深度模糊性和关节不确定性问题，在降低计算和数据复杂度的同时取得SOTA性能，适合在线实时应用。

Original Abstract: Depth ambiguity and joint uncertainty are the two main obstacles in obtaining accurate human pose predictions by 2D-to-3D lifting methods proposed in the literature. In particular, these issues are caused by 2D joint locations that can be mapped to multiple 3D positions, inducing multiple possible final poses. Following these considerations, we propose leveraging diffusion-based models generation capability to predict multiple hypotheses and aggregate them in a final accurate pose. Therefore, we introduce SnapPose3D, a pose-lifting framework trained deterministically to denoise 3D poses conditioned on both visual context and 2D pose features. SnapPose3D adopts a probabilistic approach during inference, generating multiple hypotheses through random sampling from a unit Gaussian distribution. Unlike most previous methods that address pose ambiguity by processing temporal sequences, SnapPose3D uses single frames as input, avoiding tracking and limiting computational cost, data acquisition complexity, and the need for online, real-time applications. We extensively evaluate SnapPose3D on well-known benchmarks for the 3D human pose estimation task showing its ability to generate and aggregate accurate hypotheses that lead to state-of-the-art results.

中文摘要翻译: 深度模糊性和关节不确定性是现有文献中2D-to-3D提升方法获得准确人体姿态预测的两个主要障碍。具体而言，这些问题源于2D关节位置可映射到多个3D位置，从而产生多种可能的最终姿态。基于这些考虑，我们提出利用基于扩散模型的生成能力来预测多个假设并将它们聚合为最终的准确姿态。因此，我们引入了SnapPose3D，一个以视觉上下文和2D姿态特征为条件进行确定性去噪3D姿态的姿态提升框架。SnapPose3D在推理时采用概率方法，通过从标准高斯分布中随机采样生成多个假设。与大多数通过处理时序序列来解决姿态模糊性的先前方法不同，SnapPose3D使用单帧作为输入，避免了跟踪并限制了计算成本、数据采集复杂性以及对在线实时应用的需求。我们在3D人体姿态估计任务的知名基准上对SnapPose3D进行了广泛评估，展示了其生成和聚合准确假设的能力，并取得了最先进的结果。

### [47] [SynSur: An end-to-end generative pipeline for synthetic industrial surface defect generation and detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26633)
*Paul Julius Kühn,Mika Pommeranz,Arjan Kuijper,Saptarshi Neil Sinha*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套结合视觉语言模型提示、LoRA微调扩散模型、掩码引导修补和自动标注过滤的端到端合成缺陷生成与标注管线，通过在滚珠丝杠驱动点蚀缺陷数据集和手机屏幕缺陷数据集上的实验证明，合成缺陷在补充真实稀缺数据时能保持甚至小幅提升检测性能，但无法完全替代真实数据。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 工业缺陷检测中标注数据稀缺是主要瓶颈——缺陷样本稀少、标注成本高、难以构建平衡训练集，因此需要一种能够自动生成高质量合成缺陷并附带标注的方法来增强真实数据集。

Method: 提出端到端管线：(1) 使用视觉语言模型（VLM）生成提示；(2) 结合LoRA适配的扩散模型进行微调；(3) 采用掩码引导的修补（mask-guided inpainting）生成缺陷；(4) 利用DreamSim和CLIPScore进行样本过滤；(5) 自动推导标签，实现合成缺陷的自动标注。

Result: 在滚珠丝杠点蚀缺陷数据集（BSData）和手机屏幕缺陷数据集（MSD）上的实验表明：(1) 仅使用合成数据训练无法替代真实数据；(2) 合成数据与真实数据结合时，可以保持检测性能并在部分训练设置中取得小幅提升；(3) 跨域迁移实验验证了管线结构可迁移至其他工业检测领域，但需领域特定适配和标注质量控制。

Conclusion: 基于扩散模型的工业缺陷合成管线的最大价值在于增强稀缺的真实数据集，而非替代真实数据。同时，跨域迁移需要领域特定的适配和严格的标注质量控制。

Original Abstract: The bottleneck in learning-based industrial defect detection is often limited not by model capacity, but by the scarcity of labeled defect data: defects are rare, annotations are expensive, and collecting balanced training sets is slow. We present an end-to-end pipeline for synthetic defect generation and annotation, combining Vision-Language-Model-based prompts, LoRA-adapted diffusion, mask-guided inpainting, and sample filtering with automatic label derivation, and demonstrates the potential of real data with realistic synthetic samples to overcome data scarcity. The evaluation is conducted on, a challenging dataset of pitting defects on ball screw drives, and then on a subset of the Mobile phone screen surface defect segmentation dataset (MSD) dataset to test cross-domain transfer. Beyond downstream detector performance, we analyze key stages of the pipeline, including prompt construction, LoRA selection, and sample filtering with DreamSim and CLIPScore, to understand which synthetic samples are both realistic and useful. Experiments with YOLOv26, YOLOX, and LW-DETR show that synthetic-only training does not replace real data. When combined with real data, synthetic defects can preserve performance and yield modest gains in selected BSData training regimes. The MSD transfer study shows that the overall pipeline structure carries over to a second industrial inspection domain, while also highlighting the importance of domain-specific adaptation and annotation-quality control. Overall, the paper provides an end-to-end assessment of diffusion-based industrial defect synthesis and shows that its strongest value lies in strengthening scarce real datasets rather than substituting for them.

中文摘要翻译: 基于学习的工业缺陷检测的瓶颈往往不在于模型容量，而在于标注缺陷数据的稀缺性：缺陷罕见、标注昂贵、构建平衡训练集耗时。本文提出了一套端到端的合成缺陷生成与标注管线，结合了基于视觉语言模型的提示、LoRA适配的扩散模型、掩码引导的修补、样本过滤以及自动标签推导，展示了利用真实数据与逼真合成样本来克服数据稀缺的潜力。我们在具有挑战性的滚珠丝杠驱动点蚀缺陷数据集（BSData）以及手机屏幕表面缺陷分割数据集（MSD）的子集上进行评估，以测试跨领域迁移能力。除了下游检测器的性能分析外，我们还对管线的关键阶段进行了分析，包括提示构建、LoRA选择和基于DreamSim与CLIPScore的样本过滤，以理解哪些合成样本既逼真实用。基于YOLOv26、YOLOX和LW-DETR的实验表明，仅用合成数据训练无法替代真实数据。当与真实数据结合时，合成缺陷可以保持检测性能，并在选定的BSData训练方案中取得小幅提升。MSD迁移研究表明，整体管线结构可迁移至第二个工业检测领域，同时也突显了领域特定适配和标注质量控制的重要性。总体而言，本文对基于扩散的工业缺陷合成进行了端到端的评估，并表明其最大价值在于增强稀缺的真实数据集，而非替代它们。

### [48] [Hearing the Room Through the Shape of the Drum: Modal-Guided Sound Recovery from Multi-Point Surface Vibrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26678)
*Shai Bagon,Matan Kichler,Mark Sheinin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于散斑振动测量的多点成像系统，结合物理引导的振动形成模型，从振动响应较差或高谐振的固体物体表面多点多轴振动信号中恢复场景声音，显著优于传统单点散斑测振法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 以往光学振动传感方法主要聚焦于振动响应良好的特定物体（如扬声器膜、芯片袋等），而对于振动响应差或高谐振的固体物体（如厚实表面），声音恢复效果不佳。本文旨在解决这类更具挑战性的物体的声音恢复问题。

Method: 1) 使用基于散斑的振动测量成像系统，同时捕获物体表面多个点的振动信号。2) 提出物理引导的振动形成模型，通过物体振动模态将场景声源与多点多轴振动信号关联起来。3) 利用该模型反转振动物体的共振传递函数，融合多路振动信号以估计原始声源。

Result: 在多种日常物体上评估表明，该方法在挑战性场景下显著优于传统单点散斑测振法以及其他基于信号处理的多信号融合方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了通过多点振动测量和物理模型引导的融合策略，可以有效从振动响应差的固体物体中恢复声音，拓展了视觉麦克风技术的适用范围。

Original Abstract: Optical vibration sensing enables recovering the scene sound directly from the surface vibration of nearby objects, turning everyday objects into ``visual microphones''. However, most prior methods had focused on capturing the vibrations of specific objects with highly favorable vibration responses. These include objects where the surface vibrations are generated by the object itself (e.g., speaker membrane or guitar body) or objects consisting of a thin membrane which is highly reactive to sound (e.g., a chip bag or the leaf of a plant). In this paper, we tackle sound recovery for a more challenging class of solid objects whose vibration responses are poor or highly resonant. We simultaneously capture vibrations for multiple surface points on the object using a speckle-based vibrometry imaging system. Then, we derive a novel physics-guided vibration formation model that relates the scene sound source to the captured multi-point multi-axis vibrations via the object's vibrational modes. The model is then used to reverse the resonant transfer function of the vibrating object, fusing multiple vibration signals to estimate the original sound source in the scene. We evaluate our approach by recovering sound from a variety of everyday objects, demonstrating that it significantly outperforms traditional single-point speckle vibrometry in challenging scenarios and other signal-processing-based methods for multi-signal fusing.

中文摘要翻译: 光学振动传感能够通过恢复附近物体表面的振动来捕获场景声音，将日常物体变成"视觉麦克风"。然而，先前大多数方法专注于捕获具有高振动响应的特定物体，包括由物体自身产生表面振动的物体（如扬声器膜或吉他琴身）或由对声音高反应性的薄膜构成的物体（如薯片袋或植物叶片）。在本文中，我们针对更具挑战性的固体物体类别进行声音恢复，这些物体的振动响应较差或高度谐振。我们使用基于散斑的振动测量成像系统同时捕获物体表面多个点的振动。然后，我们推导出一种新颖的物理引导的振动形成模型，该模型通过物体的振动模态将场景声源与捕获的多点多轴振动关联起来。利用该模型反转振动物体的共振传递函数，融合多个振动信号以估计场景中的原始声源。我们在多种日常物体上评估了所提方法，结果表明在挑战性场景下，该方法显著优于传统的单点散斑测振法以及其他基于信号处理的多信号融合方法。

### [49] [GLM-5V-Turbo: Toward a Native Foundation Model for Multimodal Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26752)
*GLM-V Team,:,Wenyi Hong,Xiaotao Gu,Ziyang Pan,Zhen Yang,Yuting Wang,Yue Wang,Yuanchang Yue,Yu Wang,Yanling Wang,Yan Wang,Xijun Liu,Wenmeng Yu,Weihan Wang,Wei Li,Shuaiqi Duan,Sheng Yang,Ruiliang Lv,Mingdao Liu,Lihang Pan,Ke Ning,Junhui Ji,Jinjiang Wang,Jing Chen,Jiazheng Xu,Jiale Zhu,Jiale Cheng,Ji Qi,Guobing Gan,Guo Wang,Cong Yao,Zijun Dou,Zihao Zhou,Zihan Wang,Zhiqi Ge,Zhijie Li,Zhenyu Hou,Zhao Xue,Zehui Wang,Zehai He,Yusen Liu,Yukuo Cen,Yuchen Li,Yuan Wang,Yijian Lu,Yanzi Wang,Yadong Xue,Xinyu Zhang,Xinyu Liu,Wenkai Li,Tianyu Tong,Tianshu Zhang,Shengdong Yan,Qinkai Zheng,Mingde Xu,Licheng Bao,Jiaxing Xu,Jiaxin Fan,Jiawen Qian,Jiali Chen,Jiahui Lin,Haozhi Zheng,Haoran Wang,Haochen Li,Fan Yang,Dan Zhang,Chuangxin Zhao,Chengcheng Wu,Boyan Shi,Bowei Jia,Baoxu Wang,Peng Zhang,Debing Liu,Bin Xu,Juanzi Li,Minlie Huang,Yuxiao Dong,Jie Tang*

TL;DR: GLM-5V-Turbo 是一个面向多模态智能体的原生基础模型，将多模态感知作为推理、规划、工具使用和执行的核心理念，而非语言模型的辅助接口。该模型在模型设计、多模态训练、强化学习、工具链扩展和智能体框架集成方面进行了改进，在多模态编码、视觉工具使用和框架级智能体任务上表现出色，同时保持了纯文本编码能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 随着基础模型在真实环境中部署，智能体能力不仅依赖于语言推理，还需要感知、解释和处理异构上下文（如图像、视频、网页、文档、GUI）的能力。现有方法通常将多模态感知作为语言模型的辅助接口，而非核心组成部分，这限制了智能体在多模态环境中的表现。

Method: GLM-5V-Turbo 将多模态感知作为推理、规划、工具使用和执行的核心理念进行集成。主要改进包括：模型设计优化、多模态训练、强化学习、工具链扩展以及与智能体框架的集成。

Result: 该模型在多模态编码、视觉工具使用和基于框架的智能体任务上表现强劲，同时保持了有竞争力的纯文本编码能力。

Conclusion: 开发过程为构建多模态智能体提供了实用见解，强调了多模态感知、层次化优化和可靠的端到端验证的核心作用。

Original Abstract: We present GLM-5V-Turbo, a step toward native foundation models for multimodal agents. As foundation models are increasingly deployed in real environments, agentic capability depends not only on language reasoning, but also on the ability to perceive, interpret, and act over heterogeneous contexts such as images, videos, webpages, documents, GUIs. GLM-5V-Turbo is built around this objective: multimodal perception is integrated as a core component of reasoning, planning, tool use, and execution, rather than as an auxiliary interface to a language model. This report summarizes the main improvements behind GLM-5V-Turbo across model design, multimodal training, reinforcement learning, toolchain expansion, and integration with agent frameworks. These developments lead to strong performance in multimodal coding, visual tool use, and framework-based agentic tasks, while preserving competitive text-only coding capability. More importantly, our development process offers practical insights for building multimodal agents, highlighting the central role of multimodal perception, hierarchical optimization, and reliable end-to-end verification.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了 GLM-5V-Turbo，这是向多模态智能体原生基础模型迈出的一步。随着基础模型越来越多地部署在真实环境中，智能体能力不仅依赖于语言推理，还需要感知、解释并作用于异构上下文（如图像、视频、网页、文档、图形用户界面）的能力。GLM-5V-Turbo 正是围绕这一目标构建的：多模态感知被集成作为推理、规划、工具使用和执行的核心组成部分，而非语言模型的辅助接口。本报告总结了 GLM-5V-Turbo 在模型设计、多模态训练、强化学习、工具链扩展以及与智能体框架集成方面的主要改进。这些改进使得模型在多模态编码、视觉工具使用和基于框架的智能体任务上表现出色，同时保持了有竞争力的纯文本编码能力。更重要的是，我们的开发过程为构建多模态智能体提供了实用见解，突出了多模态感知、层次化优化和可靠的端到端验证的核心作用。

</details>


### [50] [TAP into the Patch Tokens: Leveraging Vision Foundation Model Features for AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26772)
*Ahmed Abdullah,Nikolas Ebert,Oliver Wasenmüller*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了多种现代视觉基础模型（VFM）在AI生成图像检测中的表现，发现最优模型相比原始CLIP准确率提升超12%，并提出一种基于可调注意力池化（TAP）的分类头设计，进一步提升了检测性能，在多个基准上达到新SOTA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 尽管CLIP-ViT已被广泛用于AI生成图像检测，但自CLIP发布以来涌现了大量架构更优、训练范式不同的视觉基础模型（VFM），它们在AI生成图像检测和图像取证领域的潜力尚未被充分探索。

Method: 1) 构建了一个涵盖多种VFM家族（不同预训练目标、输入分辨率、模型规模）的综合基准；2) 系统评估这些模型在完整AI生成图像和AI修补图像检测上的开箱即用性能；3) 提出一种基于可调注意力池化（TAP）的分类头，通过聚合输出token形成精细的全局表示，以充分利用现代VFM的特征。

Result: 最优VFM在准确率上比原始CLIP提升超过12%，超越了已有方法；将TAP与最新VFM结合后，在多个AI生成图像和AI修补图像检测基准上取得显著性能提升，并在两个具有挑战性的野外检测基准上达到了新SOTA。

Conclusion: 现代视觉基础模型在AI生成图像检测任务上显著优于原始CLIP，结合所提可调注意力池化分类头可进一步大幅提升性能，为该领域提供了新的技术路径和基准参考。

Original Abstract: Recent methods demonstrate that large-scale pretrained models, such as CLIP vision transformers, effectively detect AI-generated images (AIGIs) from unseen generative models when used as feature extractors. Many state-of-the-art methods for AI-generated image detection build upon the original CLIP-ViT to enhance this generalization. Since CLIP's release, numerous vision foundation models (VFMs) have emerged, incorporating architectural improvements and different training paradigms. Despite these advances, their potential for AIGI detection and AI image forensics remains largely unexplored. In this work, we present a comprehensive benchmark across multiple VFM families, covering diverse pretraining objectives, input resolutions, and model scales. We systematically evaluate their out-of-the-box performance for detecting fully-generated AI-images and AI-inpainted images, and discover that the best model outperforms the original CLIP by more than 12% in accuracy, beating established approaches in the process. To fully leverage the features of a modern VFM, we propose a simple redesign of the classifier head by utilizing tunable attention pooling (TAP), which aggregates output tokens into a refined global representation. Integrating TAP with the latest VFMs yields substantial performance gains across several AIGI detection benchmarks, establishing a new state-of-the-art on two challenging benchmarks for in-the-wild detection of AI-generated and -inpainted images.

中文摘要翻译: 近期研究表明，大规模预训练模型（如CLIP视觉变换器）在作为特征提取器时，能够有效检测来自未知生成模型的AI生成图像。许多先进的AI生成图像检测方法都基于原始CLIP-ViT进行改进以增强其泛化能力。自CLIP发布以来，大量视觉基础模型（VFM）相继涌现，融入了架构改进和不同的训练范式。尽管取得了这些进展，它们在AI生成图像检测和AI图像取证方面的潜力仍未得到充分探索。在本工作中，我们提出了一个涵盖多个VFM家族的综合基准，覆盖了不同的预训练目标、输入分辨率和模型规模。我们系统评估了它们在检测完全AI生成图像和AI修补图像时的开箱即用性能，发现最优模型在准确率上比原始CLIP提升了超过12%，并且超越了已有方法。为了充分利用现代VFM的特征，我们提出了一种简单的分类头重新设计，利用可调注意力池化（TAP）将输出token聚合为精细的全局表示。将TAP与最新VFM相结合，在多个AI生成图像检测基准上取得了显著的性能提升，并在两个具有挑战性的野外检测基准上——针对AI生成图像和AI修补图像——建立了新的最先进水平。

### [51] [MemOVCD: Training-Free Open-Vocabulary Change Detection via Cross-Temporal Memory Reasoning and Global-Local Adaptive Rectification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26774)
*Zuzheng Kuang,Honghao Chang,Boqiang Liang,Haoqian Wang,Lijun He,Fan Li,Haixia Bi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MemOVCD，一种无需训练、基于跨时间记忆推理和全局-局部自适应修正的开放词汇变化检测框架，通过将双时相变化检测重构为两帧跟踪问题，有效提升语义变化检测的准确性和空间一致性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法独立处理每个时间戳或仅在最终比较阶段交互，导致时间耦合不充分，难以区分真正的语义变化与非语义外观差异；同时，基于分块推理的方式削弱了全局语义连续性，产生碎片化变化区域。

Method: (1) 将双时相变化检测重构为两帧跟踪问题，引入加权双向传播聚合两个时间方向的语义证据；(2) 构建直方图对齐的过渡帧，平滑跨大时间间隙的外观突变以稳定记忆传播；(3) 采用全局-局部自适应修正策略，自适应融合局部和全局视图预测，提升空间一致性同时保留细粒度细节。

Result: 在五个基准数据集上的实验表明，MemOVCD在两个变化检测任务上均取得了优越性能，验证了其在多种开放词汇设置下的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 提出了一种训练自由的开放词汇变化检测框架，通过跨时间记忆推理和全局-局部自适应修正，有效解决了时间耦合不足和空间碎片化问题，在不同数据集上展现出良好的性能与泛化性。

Original Abstract: Open-vocabulary change detection aims to identify semantic changes in bi-temporal remote sensing images without predefined categories. Recent methods combine foundation models such as SAM, DINO and CLIP, but typically process each timestamp independently or interact only at the final comparison stage. Such paradigms suffer from insufficient temporal coupling during semantic reasoning, which limits their ability to distinguish genuine semantic changes from non-semantic appearance discrepancies. In addition, patch-dominant inference on high-resolution images often weakens global semantic continuity and produces fragmented change regions. To address these issues, we propose MemOVCD, a training-free open-vocabulary change detection framework based on cross-temporal memory reasoning and global-local adaptive rectification. Specifically, we reformulate bi-temporal change detection as a two-frame tracking problem and introduce weighted bidirectional propagation to aggregate semantic evidence from both temporal directions. To stabilize memory propagation across large temporal gaps, we construct histogram-aligned transition frames to smooth abrupt appearance changes. Moreover, a global-local adaptive rectification strategy adaptively fuses local and global-view predictions, improving spatial consistency while preserving fine-grained details. Experiments on five benchmarks demonstrate that MemOVCD achieves favorable performance on two change detection tasks, validating its effectiveness and generalization under diverse open-vocabulary settings.

中文摘要翻译: 开放词汇变化检测旨在无需预定义类别的情况下，识别双时相遥感图像中的语义变化。近期方法结合了SAM、DINO和CLIP等基础模型，但通常独立处理每个时间戳或仅在最终比较阶段进行交互。这种范式在语义推理过程中存在时间耦合不足的问题，限制了其区分真正语义变化与非语义外观差异的能力。此外，在高分辨率图像上进行分块主导的推理往往会削弱全局语义连续性，产生碎片化的变化区域。为解决这些问题，我们提出了MemOVCD，一种无需训练的开放词汇变化检测框架，基于跨时间记忆推理和全局-局部自适应修正。具体而言，我们将双时相变化检测重构为一个两帧跟踪问题，并引入加权双向传播，从两个时间方向聚合语义证据。为稳定跨大时间间隙的记忆传播，我们构建了直方图对齐的过渡帧，以平滑突变的外观变化。此外，一种全局-局部自适应修正策略自适应地融合局部和全局视图的预测，在保留细粒度细节的同时提升空间一致性。在五个基准数据集上的实验表明，MemOVCD在两个变化检测任务上均取得了优越性能，验证了其在多种开放词汇设置下的有效性和泛化能力。

### [52] [Virtual-reality based patient-specific simulation of spine surgical procedures: A fast, highly automated and high-fidelity system for surgical education and planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26781)
*Raj Kumar Ranabhat,Tayler D Ross,Tony Jiao,Jeremie Larouche,Joel Finkelstein,Michael Hardisty*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于AI计算机视觉的方法，从CT和MRI数据自动生成患者特异性3D解剖模型，并构建了针对椎管狭窄的脊柱减压手术VR模拟平台，显著提高了模型构建效率（每例约2.5分钟）和分割精度（骨结构DSC=0.95），为术前规划、术后评估和手术模拟提供了高效、低成本的解决方案。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统外科培训因临床压力增大导致手术室暴露机会有限，现有VR培训多基于标准化场景而非个性化临床病例，缺乏针对具体患者的模拟能力。

Method: 采用基于AI的计算机视觉方法，对CT和MRI进行多模态融合（配准）并分割相关解剖结构，自动生成患者特异性3D解剖模型，并构建虚拟手术室中的脊柱减压手术（包括椎板切除术、椎间盘切除术和椎间孔切开术）VR仿真环境。

Result: 每例模型构建约2.5分钟（N=15）；椎骨分割DSC为0.95（±0.03），软组织结构DSC为0.895（±0.02）；配准精度平均TRE为1.73（±0.42）mm；半结构化访谈表明空间理解能力提升、操作信心增强及教育价值认可。

Conclusion: 该平台显著降低了患者特异性建模的时间和成本，促进了术前规划、术后评估和综合手术模拟，具有重要的临床培训和手术准备应用价值。

Original Abstract: Surgical training involves didactic teaching, mentor-led learning, surgical skills laboratories, and direct exposure to surgery; however, increasing clinical pressures have limited operating room (OR) exposure. This work leverages virtual reality (VR) to provide a safe and immersive training environment. Existing VR training is often based on standardized scenarios not tailored to individual clinical cases. This study addresses this limitation using artificial intelligence (AI) based computer vision methods to generate patient-specific simulations from computed tomography (CT) and magnetic resonance imaging (MRI). This study focuses on patient-specific spinal decompression simulation for spinal stenosis in a virtual operating room. The objectives were (1) automatic creation of 3D anatomical models and (2) VR simulation of spinal decompression procedures including laminectomy, disc resection, and foraminotomy. Model construction required multimodal fusion (registration) of CT and MRI and segmentation of relevant structures. Segmentation was evaluated using the Dice Similarity Coefficient (DSC), and registration accuracy using Target Registration Error (TRE). Qualitative feedback was obtained from surgeons and trainees. High-fidelity patient-specific 3D models were generated efficiently (approximately 2.5 minutes per case, N = 15). Segmentation accuracy was high, with a DSC of 0.95 (+/- 0.03) for vertebral bone and 0.895 (+/- 0.02) for soft tissue structures. Registration accuracy showed a mean TRE of 1.73 (+/- 0.42) mm. Semi-structured interviews indicated improved spatial understanding, increased procedural confidence, and strong perceived educational value. This platform significantly reduced the time and costs of patient-specific modelling, thereby facilitating pre-operative planning, post-procedural assessments, and comprehensive surgical simulation.

中文摘要翻译: 外科培训包括课堂教学、导师指导学习、手术技能实验室以及直接接触手术；然而，日益增加的临床压力限制了手术室（OR）的暴露机会。本研究利用虚拟现实（VR）提供安全且沉浸式的培训环境。现有VR培训通常基于标准化场景，而非针对个体临床病例量身定制。本研究通过基于人工智能（AI）的计算机视觉方法，从计算机断层扫描（CT）和磁共振成像（MRI）生成患者特异性模拟，解决了这一局限性。本研究聚焦于虚拟手术室中针对椎管狭窄的患者特异性脊柱减压仿真。目标包括：（1）自动创建3D解剖模型；（2）脊柱减压手术（包括椎板切除术、椎间盘切除术和椎间孔切开术）的VR仿真。模型构建需要CT与MRI的多模态融合（配准）以及相关结构的分割。分割性能采用Dice相似系数（DSC）评估，配准精度采用目标配准误差（TRE）评估。从外科医生和受训者处获得定性反馈。高效生成了高保真的患者特异性3D模型（每例约2.5分钟，N=15）。分割精度较高，椎骨DSC为0.95（±0.03），软组织结构DSC为0.895（±0.02）。配准精度显示平均TRE为1.73（±0.42）mm。半结构化访谈表明空间理解能力提升、操作信心增强且感知教育价值显著。该平台显著减少了患者特异性建模的时间和成本，从而促进了术前规划、术后评估以及全面手术模拟的实现。

### [53] [MesonGS++: Post-training Compression of 3D Gaussian Splatting with Hyperparameter Searching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26799)
*Shuzhao Xie,Junchen Ge,Weixiang Zhang,Jiahang Liu,Chen Tang,Yunpeng Bai,Shijia Ge,Jingyan Jiang,Yuzhi Huang,Fengnian Yang,Cong Zhang,Xiaoyi Fan,Zhi Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MesonGS++ 是一种面向 3D 高斯泼溅（3DGS）的、尺寸感知的训练后编解码器，通过联合优化剪枝率与位宽分配，在目标存储预算下实现超过 34 倍压缩比，同时保持渲染质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有 3DGS 压缩方法依赖大量耦合的超参数（如剪枝、变换、量化、熵编码），难以精确控制最终压缩尺寸，且无法充分利用率-失真权衡。

Method: 编解码端：联合基于重要性的剪枝、八叉树几何编码、属性变换、高阶球谐选择向量量化、分组混合精度量化与熵编码。配置端：将保留比率和位宽分配作为主导率-失真旋钮，通过离散采样和 0-1 整数线性规划在目标存储预算下联合优化。提出线性尺寸估计器和 CUDA 并行量化算子加速超参数搜索。

Result: 实现超过 34 倍压缩同时保持渲染质量，优于现有训练后方法；在 Stump 场景下，20 倍压缩时 PSNR 甚至超越原始 3DGS；能精确满足目标尺寸预算。

Conclusion: MesonGS++ 是一种无需训练的高效 3DGS 压缩方案，可在可控存储预算下大幅降低存储开销，并保持甚至提升渲染保真度。

Original Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) achieves high-quality novel view synthesis with real-time rendering, but its storage cost remains prohibitive for practical deployment. Existing post-training compression methods still rely on many coupled hyperparameters across pruning, transformation, quantization, and entropy coding, making it difficult to control the final compressed size and fully exploit the rate-distortion trade-off. We propose MesonGS++, a size-aware post-training codec for 3D Gaussian compression. On the codec side, MesonGS++ combines joint importance-based pruning, octree geometry coding, attribute transformation, selective vector quantization for higher-degree spherical harmonics, and group-wise mixed-precision quantization with entropy coding. On the configuration side, it treats the reserve ratio and bit-width allocation as the dominant rate-distortion knobs and jointly optimizes them under a target storage budget via discrete sampling and 0--1 integer linear programming. We further propose a linear size estimator and a CUDA parallel quantization operator to accelerate the hyperparameter searching process. Extensive experiments show that MesonGS++ achieves over 34$\times$ compression while preserving rendering fidelity, outperforming state-of-the-art post-training methods and accurately meeting target size budgets. Remarkably, without any training, MesonGS++ can even surpass the PSNR of vanilla 3DGS at a 20$\times$ compression rate on the Stump scene. Our code is available at https://github.com/mmlab-sigs/mesongs_plus

中文摘要翻译: 3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）通过实时渲染实现了高质量的新视角合成，但其存储成本对于实际部署而言仍然过高。现有的训练后压缩方法仍依赖大量耦合的超参数（涉及剪枝、变换、量化与熵编码），导致难以控制最终压缩后的大小并充分利用率-失真权衡。我们提出MesonGS++，一种面向3D高斯压缩的尺寸感知训练后编解码器。在编解码端，MesonGS++结合了基于联合重要性的剪枝、八叉树几何编码、属性变换、高阶球谐的选择性向量量化，以及分组混合精度量化与熵编码。在配置端，它将保留比率和位宽分配作为主导率-失真调节旋钮，并通过离散采样和0-1整数线性规划在目标存储预算下联合优化它们。我们进一步提出了线性尺寸估计器和CUDA并行量化算子，以加速超参数搜索过程。大量实验表明，MesonGS++在保持渲染保真度的同时实现了超过34倍的压缩，优于现有的训练后方法，并能精确满足目标尺寸预算。值得注意的是，无需任何训练，MesonGS++在Stump场景下20倍压缩率时，其PSNR甚至超过了原始3DGS。我们的代码已在 https://github.com/mmlab-sigs/mesongs_plus 公开。

</details>


### [54] [Bridge: Basis-Driven Causal Inference Marries VFMs for Domain Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26820)
*Mingbo Hong,Feng Liu,Caroline Gevaert,George Vosselman,Hao Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种名为Bridge的基元驱动域泛化框架，通过因果推断中的前门调整学习低秩基，消除混杂因素（如光照、共现、风格）导致的虚假相关，提升目标检测在跨域场景下的泛化能力，并能无缝集成多种视觉基础模型。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 检测器在源域和目标域之间存在分布差异时性能严重下降，尤其在单源域数据有限的情况下，模型容易依赖源域中的混杂因素（如光照、共现、风格），产生虚假相关，阻碍泛化能力。

Method: 提出Bridge框架，通过因果推断中的前门调整策略，学习低秩基来阻断混杂因素的影响，缓解虚假相关；同时过滤冗余和任务无关的成分以优化特征表示。该框架可无缝集成判别式（如DINOv2/3、SAM）和生成式（如Stable Diffusion）视觉基础模型。

Result: 在多个域泛化目标检测数据集（跨相机、恶劣天气、真实到艺术风格、多样化天气数据集以及新增的无人机航拍基准Diverse Weather DroneVehicle）上的实验表明，该方法显著优于先前的最先进方法。

Conclusion: Bridge通过因果推断有效消除了域泛化中的虚假相关，提升了检测器的跨域泛化能力，且具有良好的兼容性，可适配多种主流视觉基础模型。

Original Abstract: Detectors often suffer from degraded performance, primarily due to the distributional gap between the source and target domains. This issue is especially evident in single-source domains with limited data, as models tend to rely on confounders (e.g., illumination, co-occurrence, and style) from the source domain, leading to spurious correlations that hinder generalization. To this end, this paper proposes a novel Basis-driven framework for domain generalization, namely \textbf{\textit{Bridge}}, that incorporates causal inference into object detection. By learning the low-rank bases for front-door adjustment, \textbf{\textit{Bridge}} blocks confounders' effects to mitigate spurious correlations, while simultaneously refining representations by filtering redundant and task-irrelevant components. \textbf{\textit{Bridge}} can be seamlessly integrated with both discriminative (e.g., DINOv2/3, SAM) and generative (e.g., Stable Diffusion) Vision Foundation Models (VFMs). Extensive experiments across multiple domain generalization object detection datasets, i.e., Cross-Camera, Adverse Weather, Real-to-Artistic, Diverse Weather Datasets, and Diverse Weather DroneVehicle (our newly augmented real-world UAV-based benchmark), underscore the superiority of our proposed method over previous state-of-the-art approaches. The project page is available at: https://mingbohong.github.io/Bridge/.

中文摘要翻译: 检测器常常因源域与目标域之间的分布差异而导致性能下降。这一问题在单源域数据有限时尤为突出，因为模型容易依赖源域中的混杂因素（例如光照、共现和风格），从而产生阻碍泛化的虚假相关。为此，本文提出了一种新颖的基于基驱动的域泛化框架，即\textbf{\textit{Bridge}}，它将因果推断引入目标检测任务。通过学习低秩基进行前门调整，\textbf{\textit{Bridge}}能够阻断混杂因素的影响以缓解虚假相关，同时通过过滤冗余和任务无关的成分来优化特征表示。\textbf{\textit{Bridge}}可以无缝集成判别式（如DINOv2/3、SAM）和生成式（如Stable Diffusion）视觉基础模型。在多个域泛化目标检测数据集上的大量实验，包括跨相机、恶劣天气、真实到艺术风格、多样化天气数据集以及我们新增的基于真实世界无人机航拍基准Diverse Weather DroneVehicle，均表明我们的方法显著优于先前的最先进方法。项目页面地址：https://mingbohong.github.io/Bridge/。

</details>


### [55] [Breaking the Rigid Prior: Towards Articulated 3D Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26868)
*Jinye Gan,Bozhong Zheng,Xiaohao Xu,Junye Ren,Zixuan Zhang,Na Ni,Yingna Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对铰接/滑动关节物体在姿态变化下的3D异常检测问题，提出了首个大规模基准ArtiAD（15,229个点云，39类物体，6种结构异常类型），并设计了姿态感知隐式场方法SPA-SDF，在已见和未见关节配置上分别达到0.884和0.874的AUROC，显著优于所有基于刚性先验的基线方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有3D异常检测方法基于"正常几何是姿态不变且可通过配准对齐标准化"的刚性先验，该先验不适用于铰链或滑动关节的铰接物体——有效姿态变化会引发结构化的几何变形，无法归一化到单一规范模板，导致姿态引起的变形被误判为异常，而真实结构缺陷被掩盖。目前尚无基准解决此问题。

Method: 提出形状-姿态感知的有符号距离场（SPA-SDF），用连续姿态条件隐式场替代刚性先验。该场分解为与关节无关的结构先验和傅里叶编码的关节嵌入两部分。推理时通过最小化重建能量恢复关节状态，将异常识别为点云相对于学习流形的逐点偏离。

Result: SPA-SDF在ArtiAD基准上，已见关节配置的物体级AUROC为0.884，未见配置为0.874，大幅超越所有基于刚性先验的基线方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了铰接物体的3D异常检测需要显式建模姿态与几何的耦合关系，所提出的ArtiAD基准和SPA-SDF方法为这一重要但被忽视的问题提供了有效的评估框架和基线方案。

Original Abstract: Existing 3D anomaly detection methods are built on a rigid prior: normal geometry is pose-invariant and can be canonicalized through registration or alignment. This prior does not hold for articulated objects with hinge or sliding joints, where valid pose changes induce structured geometric variations that cannot be collapsed to a single canonical template, causing pose-induced deformations to be misidentified as anomalies while true structural defects are obscured. No existing benchmark addresses this challenge. We introduce ArtiAD, the first large-scale benchmark for articulated 3D anomaly detection, comprising 15,229 point clouds across 39 object categories with dense joint-angle variations and six structural anomaly types. Each sample is annotated with its joint configuration and part-level motion labels, enabling explicit disentanglement of pose-induced geometry from structural defects. ArtiAD also provides a seen/unseen articulation split to evaluate both interpolation and extrapolation to novel joint configurations. We propose Shape-Pose-Aware Signed Distance Field (SPA-SDF), a baseline that replaces the rigid prior with a continuous pose-conditioned implicit field, factorized into an articulation-independent structural prior and a Fourier-encoded joint embedding. At inference, the articulation state is recovered by minimizing reconstruction energy, and anomalies are identified as point-wise deviations from the learned manifold. SPA-SDF achieves 0.884 object-level AUROC on seen configurations and 0.874 on unseen configurations, substantially outperforming all rigid-based baselines. Our code and benchmark will be publicly released to facilitate future research.

中文摘要翻译: 现有的3D异常检测方法建立在一种刚性先验之上：正常几何体是姿态不变的，可以通过配准或对齐进行标准化。这一先验对于具有铰链或滑动关节的铰接物体并不成立——有效的姿态变化会导致结构化的几何变形，这些变形无法归约到单一的规范模板，从而导致姿态引发的变形被误判为异常，而真正的结构缺陷却被掩盖。现有基准均未解决这一挑战。我们提出了ArtiAD，首个面向铰接物体3D异常检测的大规模基准，包含39个物体类别、15,229个点云，覆盖密集的关节角度变化和六种结构异常类型。每个样本都标注了关节配置和部件级运动标签，从而能够显式地将姿态引起的几何变化与结构缺陷分离开来。ArtiAD还提供了已见/未见关节配置的划分，以评估对新颖关节配置的内插和外推能力。我们提出了形状-姿态感知有符号距离场（SPA-SDF），该基线方法用连续姿态条件隐式场替代刚性先验，将其分解为与关节无关的结构先验和傅里叶编码的关节嵌入。在推理时，通过最小化重建能量恢复关节状态，并将异常识别为点云相对于所学流形的逐点偏离。SPA-SDF在已见配置上取得了0.884的物体级AUROC，在未见配置上取得了0.874，显著优于所有基于刚性先验的基线方法。我们的代码和基准将公开发布，以促进未来研究。

</details>


### [56] [Uncertainty-Aware Pedestrian Attribute Recognition via Evidential Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26873)
*Zhuofan Lou,Shihang Zhang,Fangle Zhu,Shengjie Ye,Pingyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了UAPAR，一种基于证据深度学习（EDL）的不确定性感知行人属性识别框架，首次将EDL引入该领域，通过区域感知证据推理模块和不确定性引导的双阶段课程学习策略，在多个数据集上取得竞争性表现，并能有效识别不可靠预测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统的行人属性识别方法为确定性方法，无法评估低质量样本上的预测可靠性，在复杂真实场景中鲁棒性不足。因此需要一种能够量化预测不确定性、识别不可靠预测的不确定性感知框架。

Method: 将证据深度学习（EDL）集成到CLIP架构中。核心包括：1）区域感知证据推理模块，利用交叉注意力和空间先验掩码捕获细粒度局部特征；2）证据头用于估计属性层面的认知不确定性；3）不确定性引导的双阶段课程学习策略，减轻训练中严重标签噪声的不利影响。

Result: 在PA100K、PETA、RAPv1和RAPv2四个数据集上取得竞争性或更优性能；定性结果表明该框架生成的不确定性估计能够有效预测具有挑战性或错误的样本。

Conclusion: UAPAR是首个基于EDL的不确定性感知行人属性识别框架，能有效识别不可靠预测，增强系统在复杂真实场景中的鲁棒性，不确定性估计与样本困难程度具有良好对应关系。

Original Abstract: We propose UAPAR, an Uncertainty-Aware Pedestrian Attribute Recognition framework. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first EDL-based uncertainty-aware framework for pedestrian attribute recognition (PAR). Unlike conventional deterministic methods, which fail to assess prediction reliability on low-quality samples, UAPAR effectively identifies unreliable predictions and thus enhances system robustness in complex real-world scenarios. To achieve this, UAPAR incorporates Evidential Deep Learning (EDL) into a CLIP-based architecture. Specifically, a Region-Aware Evidence Reasoning module employs cross-attention and spatial prior masks to capture fine-grained local features, which are further processed by an evidence head to estimate attribute-wise epistemic uncertainty. To further enhance training robustness, we develop an uncertainty-guided dual-stage curriculum learning strategy to alleviate the adverse effects of severe label noise during training. Extensive experiments on the PA100K, PETA, RAPv1, and RAPv2 datasets demonstrate that UAPAR achieves competitive or superior performance. Furthermore, qualitative results confirm that the proposed framework generates uncertainty estimates that are predictive of challenging or erroneous samples.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了UAPAR，一种不确定性感知的行人属性识别框架。据我们所知，这是首个基于证据深度学习（EDL）的不确定性感知行人属性识别（PAR）框架。与无法评估低质量样本预测可靠性的传统确定性方法不同，UAPAR能够有效识别不可靠预测，从而增强系统在复杂真实场景中的鲁棒性。为实现这一目标，UAPAR将证据深度学习集成到基于CLIP的架构中。具体而言，区域感知证据推理模块采用交叉注意力和空间先验掩码来捕获细粒度局部特征，这些特征进一步由证据头处理以估计属性层面的认知不确定性。为进一步增强训练鲁棒性，我们开发了一种不确定性引导的双阶段课程学习策略，以减轻训练过程中严重标签噪声带来的不利影响。在PA100K、PETA、RAPv1和RAPv2数据集上的大量实验表明，UAPAR取得了具有竞争力或更优的性能。此外，定性结果证实，所提出的框架生成的不确定性估计能够有效预测具有挑战性或错误的样本。

### [57] [AnimateAnyMesh++: A Flexible 4D Foundation Model for High-Fidelity Text-Driven Mesh Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26917)
*Zijie Wu,Chaohui Yu,Fan Wang,Xiang Bai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AnimateAnyMesh++ 是一个前馈式框架，通过扩充数据集（DyMesh-XL 从6万增至30万）、改进VAE架构（DyMeshVAE-Flex，引入幂律拓扑注意力与顶点法线增强特征）和支持可变长度序列的整流流生成器，实现了对任意3D网格的文本驱动动画生成，在质量和效率上超越先前方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 4D内容生成虽受关注，但高质量动画3D模型的创建仍面临挑战，主要原因在于时空分布建模复杂以及4D训练数据稀缺。

Method: 1) 数据集扩充：从Objaverse-XL挖掘动态内容，将DyMesh-XL数据集的身份数从6万扩展到30万；2) 架构升级：设计DyMeshVAE-Flex，引入幂律拓扑感知注意力（power-law topology-aware attention）和顶点法线增强特征（vertex-normal enhanced features），改善轨迹重建和局部几何保持，减少轨迹粘连伪影；3) 支持可变长度序列：对DyMeshVAE-Flex和整流流生成器进行架构改进，支持变长序列训练与生成，实现更长的动画同时保持重建保真度。

Result: 大量实验表明，AnimateAnyMesh++能在数秒内生成语义准确且时间连贯的网格动画，在质量和效率上均超越先前方法；数据集扩充、VAE升级和变长整流流在基准测试和野外网格上均取得一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: AnimateAnyMesh++通过数据增强、架构改进和变长序列支持，有效提升了文本驱动3D网格动画的质量与效率，将开源代码、模型和扩展后的DyMesh-XL数据集以促进4D内容创作研究。

Original Abstract: Recent advances in 4D content generation have attracted increasing attention, yet creating high-quality animated 3D models remains challenging due to the complexity of modeling spatio-temporal distributions and the scarcity of 4D training data. We present AnimateAnyMesh++, a feed-forward framework for text-driven animation of arbitrary 3D meshes with substantial upgrades in data, architecture, and generative capability. First, we expand the DyMesh-XL dataset by mining dynamic content from Objaverse-XL, increasing the number of unique identities from 60K to 300K and substantially broadening category and motion diversity. Second, we redesign DyMeshVAE-Flex with power-law topology-aware attention and vertex-normal enhanced features, which significantly improves trajectory reconstruction, local geometry preservation, and mitigates trajectory-sticking artifacts. Third, we introduce architectural changes to both DyMeshVAE-Flex and the rectified-flow (RF) generator to support variable-length sequence training and generation, enabling longer animations while preserving reconstruction fidelity. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AnimateAnyMesh++ generates semantically accurate and temporally coherent mesh animations within seconds, surpassing prior approaches in quality and efficiency. The enlarged DyMesh-XL, the upgraded DyMeshVAE-Flex, and variable-length RF together deliver consistent gains across benchmarks and in-the-wild meshes. We will release code, models, and the expanded DyMesh-XL upon acceptance of this manuscript to facilitate research in 4D content creation.

中文摘要翻译: 近期4D内容生成的进展引起了越来越多的关注，但由于时空分布建模的复杂性以及4D训练数据的稀缺，创建高质量动画3D模型仍然具有挑战性。我们提出AnimateAnyMesh++，一个用于文本驱动任意3D网格动画的前馈式框架，在数据、架构和生成能力方面进行了重大升级。首先，我们通过从Objaverse-XL中挖掘动态内容来扩展DyMesh-XL数据集，将唯一身份数量从6万增加到30万，大幅拓宽了类别和运动多样性。其次，我们重新设计了DyMeshVAE-Flex，引入幂律拓扑感知注意力机制和顶点法线增强特征，显著改善了轨迹重建和局部几何保持，并减轻了轨迹粘连伪影。第三，我们对DyMeshVAE-Flex和整流流生成器进行了架构改进，以支持可变长度序列训练和生成，从而在保持重建保真度的同时实现更长的动画。大量实验表明，AnimateAnyMesh++能在数秒内生成语义准确且时间连贯的网格动画，在质量和效率上均超越先前方法。扩展后的DyMesh-XL、升级后的DyMeshVAE-Flex和可变长度整流流共同在基准测试和野外网格上带来一致的性能提升。我们将在论文被接收后开源代码、模型和扩展后的DyMesh-XL数据集，以促进4D内容创作研究。

### [58] [Color-Encoded Illumination for High-Speed Volumetric Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26920)
*David Novikov,Eilon Vaknin,Narek Tumanyan,Mark Sheinin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种仅使用未改装低速相机，通过时序彩色编码照明和动态3D高斯泼溅（Dynamic Gaussian Splatting）来捕捉和重建高速动态场景三维体积表示的方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统相机受限于30-60 FPS的带宽，难以捕捉高速3D动态场景；现有高速成像方法需要改造相机光学系统或增加机械部件，且局限于单一视角，无法用于多视角3D高速场景重建。

Method: 使用快速时序彩色编码序列照明场景，将高速时间信息编码到多视角图像的强度和颜色变化中；然后基于动态3D高斯泼溅（Dynamic Gaussian Splatting）的方法从图像中解码时间信息，构建高速场景的体积表示。

Result: 在模拟场景和真实多相机成像系统实验上，实现了首种（first-of-a-kind）高速体积场景重建。

Conclusion: 无需改装相机硬件或光学系统，仅通过照明编码和多视角成像结合动态高斯泼溅，即可实现高速动态场景的3D体积重建。

Original Abstract: The task of capturing and rendering 3D dynamic scenes from 2D images has become increasingly popular in recent years. However, most conventional cameras are bandwidth-limited to 30-60 FPS, restricting these methods to static or slowly evolving scenes. While overcoming bandwidth limitations is difficult for general scenes, recent years have seen a flurry of computational imaging methods that yield high-speed videos using conventional cameras for specific applications (e.g., motion capture and particle image velocimetry). However, most of these methods require modifications to a camera's optics or the addition of mechanically moving components, limiting them to a single-view high-speed capture. Consequently, these methods cannot be readily used to capture a 3D representation of rapid scene motion. In this paper, we propose a novel method to capture and reconstruct a volumetric representation of a high-speed scene using only unaugmented low-speed cameras. Instead of modifying the hardware or optics of each individual camera, we encode high-speed scene dynamics by illuminating the scene with a rapid, sequential color-coded sequence. This results in simultaneous multi-view capture of the scene, where high-speed temporal information is encoded in the spatial intensity and color variations of the captured images. To construct a high-speed volumetric representation of the dynamic scene, we develop a novel dynamic Gaussian Splatting-based approach that decodes the temporal information from the images. We evaluate our approach on simulated scenes and real-world experiments using a multi-camera imaging setup, showing first-of-a-kind high-speed volumetric scene reconstructions.

中文摘要翻译: 近年来，从二维图像捕捉和渲染三维动态场景的任务变得越来越流行。然而，大多数传统相机受限于30-60 FPS的带宽，限制了这些方法仅能处理静态或缓慢演变的场景。虽然克服带宽限制对于一般场景十分困难，但近年来涌现了大量计算成像方法，利用传统相机为特定应用（如运动捕捉和粒子图像测速）生成高速视频。然而，大多数此类方法需要改造相机的光学系统或添加机械运动部件，使其局限于单视角高速捕捉。因此，这些方法无法直接用于捕捉快速场景运动的三维表示。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖方法，仅使用未改装的低速相机即可捕捉和重建高速场景的体积表示。我们不修改单个相机的硬件或光学系统，而是通过快速、顺序的彩色编码序列照明场景来编码高速场景动态。这实现了场景的同时多视角捕捉，其中高速时间信息被编码在捕获图像的空間强度和颜色变化中。为了构建动态场景的高速体积表示，我们开发了一种基于动态高斯泼溅（Dynamic Gaussian Splatting）的新方法，从图像中解码时间信息。我们在模拟场景和真实多相机成像系统实验上评估了我们的方法，展示了首种（first-of-a-kind）高速体积场景重建。

### [59] [World2VLM: Distilling World Model Imagination into VLMs for Dynamic Spatial Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26934)
*Wanyue Zhang,Wenxiang Wu,Wang Xu,Jiaxin Luo,Helu Zhi,Yibin Huang,Shuo Ren,Zitao Liu,Jiajun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出World2VLM框架，通过将生成式世界模型的空间想象能力蒸馏到视觉-语言模型中，使VLM无需推理时生成即可内化动态空间推理能力，在多个基准上取得一致提升。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有VLM在动态空间推理上表现不足：直接扩展空间监督缺乏对运动条件状态转移的显式建模，而推理时耦合世界模型的计算开销过大。需要一种既能高效训练又能显式建模运动变换的方法。

Method: 提出World2VLM训练框架：1）利用视图一致的世界模型，根据初始观测和参数化相机轨迹合成几何对齐的未来视图；2）从中提取正向（动作→结果）和逆向（结果→动作）空间推理的结构化监督信号；3）采用两阶段微调策略在紧凑数据集上对VLM进行后训练。

Result: 在SAT-Real、SAT-Synthesized、VSI-Bench和MindCube等多个空间推理基准上，World2VLM相较基模型取得一致改进，并优于推理时耦合世界模型的方法，同时消除了昂贵的推理时生成开销。

Conclusion: 世界模型不仅可以作为推理时的工具，还可以作为训练时的有效教师，使VLM以可扩展且高效的方式内化空间想象能力。

Original Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown strong performance on static visual understanding, yet they still struggle with dynamic spatial reasoning that requires imagining how scenes evolve under egocentric motion. Recent efforts address this limitation either by scaling spatial supervision with synthetic data or by coupling VLMs with world models at inference time. However, the former often lacks explicit modeling of motion-conditioned state transitions, while the latter incurs substantial computational overhead. In this work, we propose World2VLM, a training framework that distills spatial imagination from a generative world model into a vision-language model. Given an initial observation and a parameterized camera trajectory, we use a view-consistent world model to synthesize geometrically aligned future views and derive structured supervision for both forward (action-to-outcome) and inverse (outcome-to-action) spatial reasoning. We post-train the VLM with a two-stage recipe on a compact dataset generated by this pipeline and evaluate it on multiple spatial reasoning benchmarks. World2VLM delivers consistent improvements over the base model across diverse benchmarks, including SAT-Real, SAT-Synthesized, VSI-Bench, and MindCube. It also outperforms the test-time world-model-coupled methods while eliminating the need for expensive inference-time generation. Our results suggest that world models can serve not only as inference-time tools, but also as effective training-time teachers, enabling VLMs to internalize spatial imagination in a scalable and efficient manner.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言模型（VLM）在静态视觉理解上表现出色，但在需要想象场景如何随自我中心运动演变的动态空间推理方面仍然存在困难。近期的工作要么通过合成数据扩展空间监督，要么在推理时将VLM与世界模型耦合来应对这一局限。然而，前者缺乏对运动条件状态转移的显式建模，后者则引入了大量计算开销。本文提出World2VLM，一个将空间想象力从生成式世界模型蒸馏到视觉-语言模型中的训练框架。给定初始观测和参数化相机轨迹，我们使用视图一致的世界模型合成几何对齐的未来视图，并为正向（动作到结果）和逆向（结果到动作）空间推理导出结构化监督信号。我们采用两阶段微调策略，在该流水线生成的紧凑数据集上对VLM进行后训练，并在多个空间推理基准上进行了评估。World2VLM在SAT-Real、SAT-Synthesized、VSI-Bench和MindCube等多个基准上相较于基模型均取得了一致改进，同时优于推理时与世界模型耦合的方法，且无需昂贵的推理时生成。我们的结果表明，世界模型不仅可以作为推理时的工具，还可以作为训练时有效的教师，使VLM以可扩展且高效的方式内化空间想象能力。

</details>


### [60] [ProcFunc: Function-Oriented Abstractions for Procedural 3D Generation in Python](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26943)
*Alexander Raistrick,Karhan Kayan,Jack Nugent,David Yan,Lingjie Mei,Meenal Parakh,Hongyu Wen,Dylan Li,Yiming Zuo,Erich Liang,Jia Deng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ProcFunc是一个基于Blender的Python库，用于程序化3D生成，通过组合式语义组件创建大规模多样化训练数据，并支持VLM编辑和生成程序化代码。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有程序化3D生成方法在创建大规模多样化训练数据时存在编码错误率高、组合灵活性不足等问题，亟需一种易于使用、支持语义组合且能与VLM协同工作的程序化生成工具。

Method: 提出ProcFunc库，提供一系列易用的Python函数，用于简化程序化生成代码的创建、组合、分析和执行；通过语义组件的组合式编排实现多样化数据生成；利用VLM编辑程序化材质和几何代码，并生成新代码以减少编码错误。

Original Abstract: We introduce ProcFunc, a library for Blender-based procedural 3D generation in Python. We demonstrate the detail, runtime efficiency, and diversity of this room generator, as well as its use for 3D synthetic data generation. Please visit https://github.com/princeton-vl/procfunc for source code.

中文摘要翻译: 我们介绍了ProcFunc，一个基于Blender的Python程序化3D生成库。ProcFunc提供了一系列易用的Python函数，简化了程序化生成代码的创建、组合、分析和执行。通过语义组件的组合式编排，ProcFunc能够轻松创建大规模多样化的训练数据。视觉语言模型（VLM）可以利用ProcFunc编辑程序化材质和几何代码，并以显著更少的编码错误创建新的程序化代码。最后，作为一个示例用例，我们使用ProcFunc开发了一个新的室内房间程序化生成器，其中包含一系列新型组合式程序化材质。我们展示了该房间生成器的细节丰富度、运行效率和生成多样性，以及其在3D合成数据生成中的应用。源代码请访问https://github.com/princeton-vl/procfunc。

### [61] [Three-Step Nav: A Hierarchical Global-Local Planner for Zero-Shot Vision-and-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26946)
*Wanrong Zheng,Yunhao Ge,Laurent Itti*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Three-Step Nav方法，通过“向前看”、“现在看”、“向后看”三步观察协议，在不需梯度更新或微调的情况下，显著提升了基于MLLM的零样本视觉语言导航（VLN）性能，在R2R-CE和RxR-CE数据集上达到最先进水平。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的零样本视觉语言导航（VLN）智能体存在偏离路线、过早停止、整体成功率低等问题，亟需一种无需梯度更新或任务微调即可有效纠正这些缺陷的方法。

Method: 提出Three-Step Nav三步观察协议：(1) “向前看”（look forward）——提取全局地标并勾勒粗略路径规划；(2) “现在看”（look now）——将当前视觉观测与下一子目标对齐，提供细粒度引导；(3) “向后看”（look backward）——审计整个轨迹，在停止前纠正累积漂移。该方法无需梯度更新或任务微调，可直接嵌入现有VLN管线。

Result: 在R2R-CE和RxR-CE数据集上达到了零样本设置下的最先进性能。

Conclusion: Three-Step Nav通过简单有效的三步观察协议，显著提升了MLLM在零样本VLN任务中的鲁棒性和成功率，且无需额外训练开销。

Original Abstract: Breakthrough progress in vision-based navigation through unknown environments has been achieved by using multimodal large language models (MLLMs). These models can plan a sequence of motions by evaluating the current view at each time step against the task and goal given to the agent. However, current zero-shot Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) agents powered by MLLMs still tend to drift off course, halt prematurely, and achieve low overall success rates. We propose Three-Step Nav to counteract these failures with a three-view protocol: First, "look forward" to extract global landmarks and sketch a coarse plan. Then, "look now" to align the current visual observation with the next sub-goal for fine-grained guidance. Finally, "look backward" audits the entire trajectory to correct accumulated drift before stopping. Requiring no gradient updates or task-specific fine-tuning, our planner drops into existing VLN pipelines with minimal overhead. Three-Step Nav achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance on the R2R-CE and RxR-CE dataset. Our code is available at https://github.com/ZoeyZheng0/3-step-Nav.

中文摘要翻译: 通过使用多模态大语言模型（MLLM），在未知环境下的视觉导航方面取得了突破性进展。这些模型可以通过在每一步评估当前视图与给定智能体的任务和目标，来规划一系列运动。然而，当前由MLLM驱动的零样本视觉语言导航（VLN）智能体仍然倾向于偏离路线、过早停止以及实现较低的整体成功率。我们提出Three-Step Nav，通过三步观察协议来应对这些失败：首先，“向前看”以提取全局地标并勾勒粗略计划。然后，“现在看”以将当前视觉观测与下一子目标对齐，提供细粒度引导。最后，“向后看”审计整个轨迹，以在停止前纠正累积漂移。我们的规划器无需梯度更新或任务微调，即可以最小的开销嵌入现有的VLN管线。Three-Step Nav在R2R-CE和RxR-CE数据集上达到了零样本设置下的最先进性能。我们的代码可在https://github.com/ZoeyZheng0/3-step-Nav获取。

</details>

### [62] [A Multimodal and Explainable Machine Learning Approach to Diagnosing Multi-Class Ejection Fraction from Electrocardiograms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25942)
*Catherine Ning,Yu Ma,Cindy Beini Wang,Sean McMahon,Joseph Radojevic,Steven Zweibel,Dimitris Bertsimas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多模态机器学习框架，结合12导联ECG时序特征与结构化EHR变量，将LVEF分为四个临床等级（正常、轻度、中度、重度降低）。在36,784对ECG-超声心动图数据上训练XGBoost模型，多模态模型在重度降低类别上AUROC达0.95，优于仅ECG或仅EHR基线模型，支持在资源有限场景下作为超声心动图的筛查辅助工具。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 左心室射血分数（LVEF）评估依赖超声心动图，在初级医疗和资源受限环境中可及性有限，亟需一种更便捷、低成本的筛查方法。

Method: 构建多模态机器学习框架，将12导联ECG时序特征（经工程化提取）与结构化EHR变量相结合，使用XGBoost模型将LVEF分类为四个临床常用等级（>50%、40-50%、30-40%、<30%），并利用SHAP归因分析识别最具影响力的特征。

Result: 在来自Hartford HealthCare的36,784对ECG-超声心动图数据（30,952名门诊患者）上训练，并在19,966个ECG（后续时间段）上进行时序泛化评估。多模态模型在One-vs-Rest AUROC上达到：重度0.95、中度0.92、轻度0.82、正常0.91，优于仅ECG和仅EHR基线，且在时序验证中保持性能。

Conclusion: 基于ECG的多模态LVEF分层可作为实用的筛查和分诊辅助工具，在资源有限情况下优先安排确认性影像学检查。

Original Abstract: Left ventricular ejection fraction (LVEF) assessment depends on echocardiography, limiting access in primary care and resource-constrained settings. We developed a multimodal machine-learning framework that combines engineered 12-lead ECG timeseries features with structured EHR variables to classify LVEF into four clinically used strata: normal (>50%), mildly reduced (40-50%), moderately reduced (30-40%), and severely reduced (<30%). To support model explainability, we identified the most influential ECG and EHR features via SHAP attributions. Using retrospective data from Hartford HealthCare, we trained XGBoost models on 36,784 ECG-echocardiogram pairs from 30,952 outpatients and evaluated temporal generalizability on 19,966 ECGs from a subsequent period. The multimodal model achieved one-vs-rest AUROCs of 0.95 (severe), 0.92 (moderate), 0.82 (mild), and 0.91 (normal), outperforming ECG-only and EHR-only baselines, and maintained performance under temporal validation. This work supports ECG-based, multimodal LVEF stratification as a practical screening and triage aid to prioritize confirmatory imaging where resources are limited.

中文摘要翻译: 左心室射血分数（LVEF）评估依赖于超声心动图，这在初级医疗和资源受限环境中限制了其可及性。我们开发了一种多模态机器学习框架，将经过工程化处理的12导联ECG时序特征与结构化EHR变量相结合，将LVEF分为四个临床常用分层：正常（>50%）、轻度降低（40-50%）、中度降低（30-40%）和重度降低（<30%）。为支持模型可解释性，我们通过SHAP归因分析识别了最具影响力的ECG和EHR特征。利用来自Hartford HealthCare的回顾性数据，我们在30,952名门诊患者的36,784对ECG-超声心动图数据上训练了XGBoost模型，并在后续时间段的19,966个ECG上评估了时序泛化能力。多模态模型在One-vs-Rest AUROC上分别达到0.95（重度）、0.92（中度）、0.82（轻度）和0.91（正常），优于仅ECG和仅EHR的基线模型，并在时序验证中保持性能。本研究支持将基于ECG的多模态LVEF分层作为一种实用的筛查和分诊辅助手段，在资源有限的情况下优先安排确认性影像学检查。
